// Regex Patterns for Email Subject Matching
const PATTERNS = {
  ZEPTO_PO: /P\d{7}/,
  INSTAMART_UNDERSCORE: /_([A-Z0-9]+PO\d+)/,
  INSTAMART_STANDARD: /\b([A-Z0-9]+PO\d+)\b/,
  INSTAMART_STORE_NEW: /^([A-Za-z0-9\s]+)-/,
  INSTAMART_STORE_GRN: /\|\|\s*([A-Za-z0-9\s]+)_/,
  BIGBASKET_ID: /PO No\s+([A-Z0-9]+)/i, // <-- REPLACE with this line
  BIGBASKET_BODY: /PO No\(s\)?\s*[:\-]?\s*([A-Z0-9]+)/i,
  BIGBASKET_STORE: /Big Basket\s+(.+?)\s+PO Details/i, // <-- ADD THIS NEW PATTERN
  RBL_PO: /\b\d{10}\b/,
  BLINKIT_PO: /-(\d{10,})\s*[:\s]/,
  GENERIC_PO: /PO\s?[:#]?\s?(\w+)/,
  CAT_GRN: /GRN|RETURN/i,
  CAT_REV: /REVISED|AMENDMENT|AMENDED|RESCHEDULED/i,
  CAT_CANC: /CANCELLED/i,
  CAT_APP: /SCHEDULED/i,
  CAT_AMAZON_PICKUP: /FBA PICKUP APPOINTMENT CONFIRMED/i,
  STARMARK_LOCATION: /Stock For Location\s*:\s*(.+)/i,
  STARMARK_PO_NUM: /Po No\s*:\s*([^\n\r]+)/i,
  STARMARK_PO_DATE: /Date\s*:\s*([^\n\r]+)/i,
  STARMARK_PO_EXPIRY: /Valid Till\s*:\s*([^\n\r]+)/i,
  STARMARK_ITEM_ROW: /^\d+\s+CODE\s+[\d\w]+\s+(.*?)\s+(\d+)\s+RS\.\s+([\d.]+)/,
  STARMARK_EMBEDDED_SKU: /(\b\d{7}\b|\bTB\w+\b)/i
};

// ==========================================
// 2. WEB APP HANDLERS
// ==========================================

function doGet(e) {
  const action = e.parameter.action;
  
  try {
    switch (action) {
      case 'getPurchaseOrders': 
        const poNumber = e.parameter.poNumber;
        return getPurchaseOrders(poNumber);
      case 'getInventory': return getInventory();
      case 'getChannelConfigs': return getChannelConfigs();
      case 'getSystemConfig': return getSystemConfig();
      case 'getUsers' : return getUsers(); // Fetch users list; added by Avinav
      case 'getUploadMetadata' : return getUploadMetadata();  //added by Avinav
      case 'getPackingData' :  return getPackingData(e.parameter.referenceCode);
      case 'getQuotations' : return getQuotations();

      default: return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Invalid action'});
    }
  } catch (err) {
    return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: err.toString()});
  }
}


function doPost(e) {
  try {
    if (!e || !e.postData || !e.postData.contents) {
      return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'No post data received'});
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(e.postData.contents);
    
    // Nimbus webhook detection
    if (data.awb_number && data.status && data.event_time) 
    {
    return handleNimbusWebhook(data);
    }

    const action = data.action;
    
    debugLog(action || "UNKNOWN_ACTION", data);

    let result;

    if (action === 'ping') result = { status: 'success', message: 'pong' };
    else if (action === 'saveUser') result = saveUser(data); 
    else if (action === 'deleteUser') result = deleteUser(data.userId); 
    else if (action === 'logFileUpload') result = logFileUpload(data);
    else if (action === 'createItem') result = createInventoryItem(data);
    else if (action === 'updatePrice') result = updateInventoryPrice(data);
    else if (action === 'saveChannelConfig') result = saveChannelConfig(data);
    else if (action === 'saveSystemConfig') result = saveSystemConfig(data);
    else if (action === 'pushToEasyEcom') result = pushToEasyEcom(data);
    else if (action === 'createZohoInvoice') result = handleCreateZohoInvoice(data.eeReferenceCode);
    else if (action === 'pushToShippingPartner') result = handlePushToShippingAggregator(data.eeReferenceCode);
    else if (action === 'updatePOStatus') result = updatePOStatus(data.poNumber, data.status);
    else if (action === 'syncZohoContacts') result = handleSyncZohoContacts();
    else if (action === 'syncInventory') result = handleSyncInventory();
    else if (action === 'manual_sync_inventory_allocation') result = manual_sync_inventory_allocation();
    else if (action === 'cancelLineItem') result = handleCancelLineItem(data.poNumber, data.articleCode);
    else if (action === 'updateFBAShipmentId') result = handleUpdateFBAShipmentId(data.poNumber, data.fbaShipmentId);
    else if (action === 'fetchEasyEcomShipments' || action == 'syncEasyEcomShipments') result = handleSyncEasyEcomShipments();
    else if (action === 'processFlipkartConsignment') result = processFlipkartConsignment(data);
    else if (action === 'processFlipkartEInvoice' || action === 'FLIPKART_E_INVOICE') result = processFlipkartEInvoice(data);
    else if (action === 'SEND_AND_ACCEPT_ESTIMATE') result = SEND_AND_ACCEPT_ESTIMATE(data);
    else if (action === 'FETCH_LAST_14_DAYS_QUOTATIONS') result = FETCH_LAST_14_DAYS_QUOTATIONS();
    else if (action === 'syncSinglePO') result = { status: 'success', message: 'PO ' + data.poNumber + ' sync triggered.' };
    else if (action === 'getSalesOrders') result = getSalesOrders(data.referenceCode);
    else if (action === 'FETCH_BOX_DETAILS') result = getBoxSummaryByEEReference(data.eeReferenceCode);
    else if (action === 'sendAppointmentEmail') result = { status: 'success', message: 'Appointment email sent' };
    else if (action === 'updateZeptoOrderStatus') result = { status: 'success', message: 'Zepto order status updated.' };
    else if (action === 'updateZeptoAppointmentDetails') result = { status: 'success', message: 'Zepto appointment details updated.' };
    else if (action === 'processBlinkitAppointmentPasses') result = processBlinkitAppointmentPasses();
    else if (action === 'updateZeptoASN') result = updateZeptoASN(data);
    else if (action === 'updateRTOStatus') result = updateRTOStatus(data);
    else if (action === 'sendBBOrderConfirmationEmail') 
    {
      const poNumbers = (data.poNumbers || []).map(p => String(p).trim()).filter(p => p);
      if (poNumbers.length === 0) {return responseJSON({Status: "error",message: "No PO numbers received."});}
      const result = sendBBOrderConfirmationEmail(poNumbers);
      return responseJSON(result);
    }
    else if (action === 'sendZeptoAppointmentRequestEmail' ||action === 'sendInstamartAppointmentRequestEmail' ||action === 'sendBBAppointmentRequestEmail') 
    {
      const saleOrderList = data.orders?.map(o => String(o.id).trim()) || [];
      const channelMap = {
        sendZeptoAppointmentRequestEmail: "Zepto",
        sendInstamartAppointmentRequestEmail: "Instamart",
        sendBBAppointmentRequestEmail: "BB"
        };
      result = processChannelAppointments(channelMap[action], saleOrderList);
    }
    else if (action === 'addOrderNote') result = addOrderNote(data);
    else if (action === 'updateInstamartAppointmentDetails') result = updateInstamartAppointmentDetails(data);
    else if (action === 'syncZohoContactToEasyEcom') {
      const ok = syncZohoContactToEasyEcom(data.contactId);
      result = ok === true ? {status: 'success'} : {status: 'error', message: 'Sync failed'};
    }
    else {
      return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Invalid action: ' + action});
    }

    // Ensure we always wrap the result in responseJSON if the function didn't already
    if (result && result.getContentText) return result; // It's already a TextOutput
    return responseJSON(result || {status: 'success', message: 'Action processed'});

  } catch (error) {
    return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: "doPost Error: " + error.toString()});
  }
}

function updateRTOStatus(data) {
  const { eeReferenceCode, rtoStatus } = data;
  if (!eeReferenceCode || !rtoStatus) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing required fields' };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0];

  const eeRefIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
  const rtoStatusIdx = headers.indexOf("RTO Status");

  if (eeRefIdx === -1 || rtoStatusIdx === -1) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Required columns not found in PO_Database' };
  }

  let updated = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][eeRefIdx]).trim() === String(eeReferenceCode).trim()) {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, rtoStatusIdx + 1).setValue(rtoStatus);
      updated = true;
    }
  }

  if (updated) {
    return { status: 'success', message: 'RTO Status updated successfully' };
  } else {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Order not found' };
  }
}


/**
 * Specialized logic for Flipkart Consignment PDF text processing.
 */
function processFlipkartConsignment(data) {
  const { poNumber, fileText, userEmail } = data;
  
  if (!poNumber || !fileText) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'PO Number or PDF text content missing' };
  }

  try {
    // 1. Extract details using Regex based on standard Flipkart portal PDF format
    const extractedPoMatch = fileText.match(/PO Number:\s*([A-Z0-9]+)/i);
    const extractedConsignmentMatch = fileText.match(/Consignment Number:\s*([A-Z0-9]+)/i);
    const extractedDateMatch = fileText.match(/Delivery Date:\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})\s*(\d{2}:\d{2}:\d{2})/i);

    const extractedPo = extractedPoMatch ? extractedPoMatch[1].trim() : null;
    const consignmentId = extractedConsignmentMatch ? extractedConsignmentMatch[1].trim() : null;
    const deliveryDate = extractedDateMatch ? extractedDateMatch[1] : null;
    const deliveryTime = extractedDateMatch ? extractedDateMatch[2] : null;

    // 2. Strict Validation
    if (!extractedPo) {
        return { status: 'error', message: 'Could not find PO Number in PDF content.' };
    }
    // Clean PO numbers of trailing version suffixes (like -1, _1) for matching
    const cleanPoForMatch = function(po) {
        return String(po).replace(/[-_]\d+$/, '').trim().toUpperCase();
    };
    if (cleanPoForMatch(extractedPo) !== cleanPoForMatch(poNumber)) {
        return { status: 'error', message: `PO Mismatch! PDF belongs to ${extractedPo}, but you are uploading for ${poNumber}.` };
    }
    if (!consignmentId) {
        return { status: 'error', message: 'Consignment Number not found in PDF.' };
    }

    // 3. Update PO_Database
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dbData[0];
    
    const poColIndex = headers.indexOf('PO Number');
    const statusColIndex = headers.indexOf('Status');
    const apptDateColIndex = headers.indexOf('Appointment Date');
    const apptTimeColIndex = headers.indexOf('Appointment Time');
    const apptIdColIndex = headers.indexOf('Appointment ID');

    let updated = false;
    for (let i = 1; i < dbData.length; i++) {
      if (String(dbData[i][poColIndex]) === poNumber) {
        // Update fields
        dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, apptIdColIndex + 1).setValue(consignmentId);
        if (deliveryDate) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, apptDateColIndex + 1).setValue(deliveryDate);
        if (deliveryTime) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, apptTimeColIndex + 1).setValue(deliveryTime);
        
        // Also update status to 'Appointment Pending' if it was earlier stage
        const currentStatus = String(dbData[i][statusColIndex]);
        if (currentStatus === 'New' || currentStatus === 'Confirmed') {
            dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, statusColIndex + 1).setValue('Appointment to be taken');
        }
        updated = true;
      }
    }

    if (!updated) {
        return { status: 'error', message: `PO ${poNumber} not found in database.` };
    }

    return { 
      status: 'success', 
      message: `Consignment ${consignmentId} successfully linked to PO ${poNumber}.`,
      details: { consignmentId, deliveryDate, deliveryTime }
    };

  } catch (e) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Processing Error: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Processes Flipkart E-Invoice data to create a Zoho Invoice without IRP push.
 */
function processFlipkartEInvoice(data) {
  const { pos, invoiceDate, invoiceNumber, irn, items, userEmail } = data;
  
  if (!pos || !invoiceNumber || !items || items.length === 0) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing required fields (pos, invoiceNumber, items)' };
  }

  try {
    const token = getZohoAccessToken();
    const orgId = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');
    if (!token || !orgId) throw new Error("Zoho credentials (token/orgId) not configured.");

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dbData[0];
    
    const poColIdx = headers.indexOf('PO Number');
    const contactColIdx = headers.indexOf('Zoho Contact ID');
    const invoiceNumColIdx = headers.indexOf('Invoice Number');
    const invoiceDateColIdx = headers.indexOf('Invoice Date');
    const statusColIdx = headers.indexOf('Status');
    const invoiceIdColIdx = headers.indexOf('Invoice Id');
    const irnColIdx = headers.indexOf('IRN'); // We'll try to find an IRN column

    // 1. Find Zoho Contact ID
    let zohoContactId = null;
    let foundPoRows = [];
    const poList = (Array.isArray(pos) ? pos : [pos]).map(p => String(p).trim());

    for (let i = 1; i < dbData.length; i++) {
       const rowPo = String(dbData[i][poColIdx]).trim();
       if (poList.includes(rowPo)) {
         if (!zohoContactId) zohoContactId = dbData[i][contactColIdx];
         foundPoRows.push(i + 1);
       }
    }
    
    if (!zohoContactId) {
      throw new Error("Could not find Zoho Contact ID for the provided PO(s). Ensure they exist in PO_Database.");
    }

    // 2. Map items to Zoho Item IDs
    const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
    const lineItems = items.map(item => {
      const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, 'flipkart', item.sku);
      if (!zohoItemId) throw new Error(`Zoho Item ID not found for Flipkart SKU: ${item.sku}. Please update Master_SKU_Mapping.`);
      
      return {
        "item_id": zohoItemId,
        "rate": parseFloat(item.amount).toFixed(2),
        "quantity": item.qty,
        "tax_id": "1975394000000027292" // Standard Integrated Tax (IGST 12%)
      };
    });

    // 3. Construct Zoho Invoice Payload
    const createPayload = {
      "customer_id": zohoContactId,
      "invoice_number": invoiceNumber,
      "date": invoiceDate,
      "reference_number": poList.join(', '),
      "line_items": lineItems,
      "notes": `IRN: ${irn}`, // Recording IRN in notes
      "payment_terms": 0,
      "payment_terms_label": "Due on Receipt"
    };

    const createUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices?organization_id=${orgId}&ignore_auto_number_generation=true`;
    const createOptions = {
      'method': 'post',
      'headers': { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` },
      'contentType': 'application/json',
      'payload': JSON.stringify(createPayload),
      'muteHttpExceptions': true
    };
    
    const createResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(createUrl, createOptions);
    const createResult = JSON.parse(createResponse.getContentText());
    
    if (createResponse.getResponseCode() !== 201) {
      throw new Error(`Zoho API Error: ${createResponse.getContentText()}`);
    }

    const newInvoiceId = createResult.invoice.invoice_id;

    // 4. Mark as Sent
    const sentUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices/${newInvoiceId}/status/sent?organization_id=${orgId}`;
    UrlFetchApp.fetch(sentUrl, {
      'method': 'post',
      'headers': { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` },
      'muteHttpExceptions': true
    });

    // 5. Update PO_Database
    foundPoRows.forEach(rowIndex => {
      dbSheet.getRange(rowIndex, invoiceNumColIdx + 1).setValue(invoiceNumber);
      dbSheet.getRange(rowIndex, invoiceDateColIdx + 1).setValue(invoiceDate);
      dbSheet.getRange(rowIndex, statusColIdx + 1).setValue('Invoiced');
      dbSheet.getRange(rowIndex, invoiceIdColIdx + 1).setValue(newInvoiceId);
      if (irnColIdx !== -1) {
        dbSheet.getRange(rowIndex, irnColIdx + 1).setValue(irn);
      }
    });

    return { status: 'success', message: `Flipkart E-Invoice ${invoiceNumber} created and linked.`, invoiceId: newInvoiceId };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log("processFlipkartEInvoice Error: " + e.toString());
    return { status: 'error', message: e.toString() };
  }
}

function getPackingData(referenceCode) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_MASTER_DATA);
  if (!sheet) return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: `Sheet "${SHEET_MASTER_DATA}" not found.`});
  
  const rawData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (rawData.length <= 1) return responseJSON({status: 'success', data: []});
  
  const headers = rawData[0];
  const refCodeIdx = headers.indexOf("Reference Code");

  const data = [];
  for (let i = 1; i < rawData.length; i++) {
    const row = rawData[i];
    if (row.every(cell => cell === "")) continue;
    
    if (referenceCode && refCodeIdx !== -1 && String(row[refCodeIdx]).trim() !== String(referenceCode).trim()) {
        continue;
    }

    const obj = {};
    for (let j = 0; j < headers.length; j++) { obj[headers[j]] = row[j]; }
    data.push(obj);
  }
  
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', data: data});
}

function handleCancelLineItem(poNumber, articleCode) {
    try {
        const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
        const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
        if (!sheet) throw new Error("PO_Database sheet not found");

        const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const headers = data[0].map(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase());
        
        const poNumIdx = headers.indexOf("po number");
        const artCodeIdx = headers.indexOf("item code");
        const statusIdx = headers.indexOf("status");

        if (poNumIdx === -1 || artCodeIdx === -1 || statusIdx === -1) throw new Error("Database schema missing required columns.");

        let found = false;
        for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
            const row = data[i];
            if (String(row[poNumIdx]).trim() === String(poNumber).trim() && String(row[artCodeIdx]).trim() === String(articleCode).trim()) {
                sheet.getRange(i + 1, statusIdx + 1).setValue("Cancelled");
                found = true;
                break; // Assuming unique PO-SKU combo per row
            }
        }

        if (!found) return responseJSON({ status: 'error', message: 'Line item not found.' });

        SpreadsheetApp.flush();
        return responseJSON({ status: 'success', message: `Item ${articleCode} in PO ${poNumber} cancelled.` });
    } catch (e) {
        return responseJSON({ status: 'error', message: e.toString() });
    }
}

/**
 * Updates the FBA Shipment IDs column in the PO Database
 */
function handleUpdateFBAShipmentId(poNumber, fbaShipmentId) {
    try {
        const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
        const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
        if (!sheet) throw new Error("PO_Database sheet not found");

        const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const headers = data[0].map(h => String(h).trim());
        
        let poNumIdx = headers.indexOf("PO Number");        
        const fbaColIdx = headers.indexOf("FBA Shipment IDs");
        const carrierColIdx = headers.indexOf("Carrier");

        if (poNumIdx === -1 || fbaColIdx === -1) {
            throw new Error(`Required columns missing (PO Number or FBA Shipment IDs). Columns found: ${headers.join(', ')}`);
        }

        let updateCount = 0;
        const targetPo = String(poNumber).trim();

        // poNumber might be a comma separated list from the UI (grouped order)
        const poList = targetPo.split(',').map(p => p.trim());

        for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
            const rowPo = String(data[i][poNumIdx]).trim();
            if (poList.includes(rowPo)) {
                sheet.getRange(i + 1, fbaColIdx + 1).setValue(fbaShipmentId);
                sheet.getRange(i + 1, carrierColIdx + 1).setValue("ATS");
                updateCount++;
            }
        }

        SpreadsheetApp.flush();
        return responseJSON({ status: 'success', message: `Updated FBA Shipment ID for ${updateCount} row(s).` });
    } catch (e) {
        return responseJSON({ status: 'error', message: e.toString() });
    }
}

    try {
        if (typeof updateMasterSkuInventory === 'function') {
            syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation();

        } else {
            return responseJSON({ status: 'error', message: 'updateMasterSkuInventory function not found in GAS.' });
        }
    } catch (e) {
        return responseJSON({ status: 'error', message: e.toString() });
    }
}

function handleSyncEasyEcomShipments() {
    try {
  
            fetchEasyEcomShipments();
            return responseJSON({ status: 'success', message: 'EasyEcom sync completed.' });

    } catch (e) {
        return responseJSON({ status: 'error', message: e.toString() });
    }
}

  try {
    if (typeof syncZohoContacts === 'function') {
      syncZohoContacts();
      return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'Zoho contacts sync initiated.'});
    } else {
      return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'syncZohoContacts function not implemented in GAS.'});
    }
  } catch (e) {
    return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: e.toString()});
  }
}

/**
 * Universal Logger for Debugging
 */
function debugLog(action, data) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(LOG_DEBUG_SHEET);
    if (!sheet) {
      sheet = ss.insertSheet(LOG_DEBUG_SHEET);
      sheet.appendRow(["Timestamp", "Action", "Raw Payload"]);
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3).setFontWeight("Bold").setBackground("#f3f3f3");
      sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
    }
    sheet.appendRow([new Date(), action, JSON.stringify(data)]);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error("Logging failed: " + err.toString());
  }
}



function responseJSON(data) {
  return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(data)).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
}

// ==========================================
// 3. FRONTEND DATA API
// ==========================================


function getPurchaseOrders(poNumberFilter) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  if (!sheet) return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: `Sheet "${SHEET_PO_DB}" not found.`});
  
  const rawData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (rawData.length <= 1) return responseJSON({status: 'success', data: []});
  
  const headers = rawData[0];
  let poNumIdx = headers.indexOf("PO Number");
  if (poNumIdx === -1) poNumIdx = headers.indexOf("PO_Number");

  const data = [];
  for (let i = 1; i < rawData.length; i++) {
    const row = rawData[i];
    if (row.every(cell => cell === "")) continue;
    
    // If filter is provided, skip non-matching rows
    if (poNumberFilter && poNumIdx !== -1 && String(row[poNumIdx]).trim() !== String(poNumberFilter).trim()) {
        continue;
    }

    const obj = {};
    for (let j = 0; j < headers.length; j++) { obj[headers[j]] = row[j]; }
    data.push(obj);
  }
  
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', data: data});
}


function getSalesOrders(referenceCodeFilter) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  if (!sheet) return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: `Sheet "${SHEET_PO_DB}" not found.`});

  if (rawData.length <= 1) return responseJSON({status: 'success', data: []});
  
  const headers = rawData[0];
  const refCodeIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");

  const data = [];
  for (let i = 1; i < rawData.length; i++) {
    const row = rawData[i];
    if (row.every(cell => cell === "")) continue;
    
    // If filter is provided, skip non-matching rows
    if (referenceCodeFilter && refCodeIdx !== -1 && String(row[refCodeIdx]).trim() !== String(referenceCodeFilter).trim()) {
        continue;
    }

    const obj = {};
    for (let j = 0; j < headers.length; j++) { obj[headers[j]] = row[j]; }
    data.push(obj);
  }
  
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', data: data});
}

/**
 * Appends a note to the "Order Notes" column in PO_Database.
 * Delimiter: "##"
 */
function addOrderNote(data) {
  const { poNumber, note, userName } = data;
  if (!poNumber || !note) return { status: 'error', message: 'PO Number or Note missing' };

  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
    const dataRange = sheet.getDataRange();
    const values = dataRange.getValues();
    const headers = values[0];

    const poCol = headers.indexOf('PO Number');
    const notesCol = headers.indexOf('Order Notes');

    if (poCol === -1) return { status: 'error', message: 'PO Number column not found' };
    if (notesCol === -1) return { status: 'error', message: 'Order Notes column not found' };

    let rowIndex = -1;
    for (let i = 1; i < values.length; i++) {
      if (String(values[i][poCol]).trim() === String(poNumber).trim()) {
        rowIndex = i + 1;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (rowIndex === -1) return { status: 'error', message: 'PO not found: ' + poNumber };

    const currentNotes = String(values[rowIndex - 1][notesCol] || "").trim();
    const timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+5:30", "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm");
    const newNoteEntry = `[${timestamp}] ${userName || 'System'}: ${note}`;
    
    const updatedNotes = currentNotes ? currentNotes + " ## " + newNoteEntry : newNoteEntry;

    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, notesCol + 1).setValue(updatedNotes);

    return { 
      status: 'success', 
      message: 'Note added successfully',
      updatedNotes: updatedNotes
    };
  } catch (err) {
    return { status: 'error', message: err.toString() };
  }
}

function getUploadMetadata() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_UPLOAD_LOGS);
  const rows = getDataAsJSON(sheet);
  
  // Return unique last entry for each function ID
  const map = {};
  rows.forEach(r => {
    map[r['ID']] = {
      id: r['ID'],
      functionName: r['FunctionName'],
      lastUploadedBy: r['LastUploadedBy'],
      lastUploadedAt: r['LastUploadedAt'],
      status: r['Status']
    };
  });
  
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', data: Object.values(map)});
}



function updatePOStatus(poNumber, status) {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
    if (!sheet) throw new Error("PO_Database sheet not found");

    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0].map(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase());

    const poNumIndex = headers.indexOf("po number");
    const statusIndex = headers.indexOf("status");

    if (poNumIndex === -1 || statusIndex === -1) {
      throw new Error("Required columns missing: PO Number or Status");
    }

    let updateCount = 0;

    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][poNumIndex]).trim() === String(poNumber).trim()) {

        const currentStatus = String(data[i][statusIndex]).trim().toLowerCase();

        // ⛔ Do not update if already Cancelled
        if (currentStatus === 'cancelled') {
          continue;
        }

        sheet.getRange(i + 1, statusIndex + 1).setValue(status);
        updateCount++;
      }
    }

    if (updateCount === 0) {
      return responseJSON({
        status: 'error',
        message: `PO ${poNumber} not found or already cancelled.`
      });
    }

    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    return responseJSON({
      status: 'success',
      message: `Successfully marked PO ${poNumber} as ${status}.`
    });

  } catch (err) {
    return responseJSON({ status: 'error', message: err.toString() });
  }
}



function ProcessAmazonB2BShipment(base64Data, fileName) {
  try {
    if (!base64Data || !fileName) {
      throw new Error("File data or file name is missing.");
    }
    
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);

    const decoded = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decoded, MimeType.CSV, fileName);
 
    // --- The rest of the function continues as before ---
    
    const file = folder.createFile(blob);
    file.setName(`${fileName}`);
    const fileUrl = file.getUrl();
    
    const newLog = [
      new Date(),
      "Amazon_FBA",
      "Manual Upload",
      fileName,
      fileName,
      fileUrl,
      "New PO",
      ""
    ];

    logSheet.getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, newLog.length).setValues([newLog]);
    
    const successMessage = `Successfully processed and logged Shipping Plan for Amazon".`;
    Logger.log(successMessage);
    extractDatabaseDetails();
    return { status: "success", message: successMessage, fileUrl: fileUrl };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR during manual upload processing: ${e.message}`);
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}

/**
 * **CORRECTED & ROBUST:** Logs the upload and triggers the specific backend
 * processing function requested by the user. This version has consistent error
 * handling and response logic for all function IDs.
 */
function logFileUpload(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_UPLOAD_LOGS);
  const now = new Date().toLocaleString();
  const functionNameMap = { 
    'b2b-packing-list': 'B2B Packing List Data',
    'flipkart-minutes-po': 'FlipkartMinutes PO Upload',
    'amazon-b2b-shipment': 'Amazon B2B Shipment Plan' // Add the new name
  };
  
  let processingResult;
  let status;

  try {
    // Use a switch statement for cleaner, more scalable logic.
    switch (data.functionId) {
      
      case 'b2b-packing-list':
        if (typeof UpdatePackingListData !== "function") {
          throw new Error("Function 'UpdatePackingListData' is not defined in the backend.");
        }
        UpdatePackingListData(data.fileData, data.fileName);
        status = 'Success';
        processingResult = "Packing list data processed successfully.";
        break;

      case 'flipkart-minutes-po':
        if (typeof ProcessFlipkartMinutesPO !== "function") {
          throw new Error("Function 'ProcessFlipkartMinutesPO' is not defined in the backend.");
        }
        const flipkartResult = ProcessFlipkartMinutesPO(data.fileData, data.fileName);
        if (flipkartResult && flipkartResult.status === 'success') {
          status = 'Success';
          processingResult = flipkartResult.message;
        } else {
          throw new Error(flipkartResult ? flipkartResult.message : "Flipkart function returned an invalid response.");
        }
        break;

      // =========================================================================
      // THE FIX IS IN THIS BLOCK
      // =========================================================================
      case 'amazon-b2b-shipment':
        if (typeof ProcessAmazonB2BShipment !== "function") {
          throw new Error("Function 'ProcessAmazonB2BShipment' is not defined in the backend.");
        }
        // Correctly pass the file data and name from the 'data' object.
        const amazonResult = ProcessAmazonB2BShipment(data.fileData, data.fileName);
        
        // Check the response from the function to determine the outcome.
        if (amazonResult && amazonResult.status === 'success') {
          status = 'Success';
          processingResult = amazonResult.message;
        } else {
          // If the function returns an error, throw it to be caught below.
          throw new Error(amazonResult ? amazonResult.message : "Amazon function returned an invalid response.");
        }
        break;
      
      default:
        status = 'Pending';
        processingResult = "No specific backend function found for this ID. Logged only.";
        break;
    }

    // --- Log the final success status to the sheet ---
    sheet.appendRow([
      data.functionId, 
      functionNameMap[data.functionId] || data.functionId, 
      data.userName, 
      now, 
      status, 
      data.fileName || 'N/A',
      processingResult // Add the result message to the log
    ]);
    
    // --- Return the final success response to the front-end ---
    return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: processingResult});

  } catch (e) {
    // --- This single catch block now handles ALL errors from any function ---
    status = 'Error';
    processingResult = e.toString();
    Logger.log(`Error processing ${data.functionId}: ${processingResult}`);
    
    // Log the error to the sheet.
    sheet.appendRow([
      data.functionId, 
      functionNameMap[data.functionId] || data.functionId, 
      data.userName, 
      now, 
      status, 
      data.fileName || 'N/A', 
      processingResult // Log the specific error message
    ]);
    
    // Return a structured error response to the front-end.
    return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: processingResult});
  }
}


/**
 * **REWRITTEN & EFFICIENT:** This function processes an uploaded packing list. It now:
 * 1. Fetches a list of "processable" orders from the PO_Database based on their status.
 * 2. Only appends rows from the uploaded file that match these processable orders.
 * 3. Cleans the 'Reference Code' and calculates the 'Value' for the valid rows.
 */
function UpdatePackingListData(base64Data, fileName) {

  //fetchEasyEcomShipments();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  // =========================================================================
  // Step 1: Get the list of "Processable" Reference Codes from the PO_Database
  // =========================================================================
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const processableRefCodes = new Set();

  if (dbSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const dbHeaders = dbData.shift();
    
    // Find the indexes of the columns we need to check
    const statusIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("EE_order_status");
    const invoiceDateIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("EE_invoice_date");
    const boxDataIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("Box Data");
    const refIdIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("EE_reference_code");

    if ([statusIndex, invoiceDateIndex, boxDataIndex, refIdIndex].includes(-1)) {
      throw new Error("One or more required columns (EE_order_status, EE_invoice_date, Box Data, EE_reference_code) not found in PO_Database.");
    }

    dbData.forEach(row => {
      const status = String(row[statusIndex]).trim();
      const invoiceDate = String(row[invoiceDateIndex]).trim();
      const boxData = String(row[boxDataIndex]).trim();
      
      // Check if the row meets all three conditions
      if (status === 'Confirmed' && invoiceDate !== '' && boxData === '') {
        const refCode = String(row[refIdIndex]).trim();
        if (refCode) {
          processableRefCodes.add(refCode);
        }
      }
    });
  }
  
  if (processableRefCodes.size === 0) {
    throw new Error("No processable orders found in the PO_Database. (Status must be 'Confirmed' with blank Invoice Date and Box Data).");
  }
  Logger.log(`Found ${processableRefCodes.size} processable POs to check against.`);

  // =========================================================================
  // Step 2: Decode and Parse the Uploaded File
  // =========================================================================
  const decoded = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
  const csvString = Utilities.newBlob(decoded, 'text/csv', fileName).getDataAsString();
  const csvData = Utilities.parseCsv(csvString);
  
  if (csvData.length < 2) throw new Error("The uploaded file is empty or missing data.");

  const rawHeaders = csvData[0];
  const headers = rawHeaders.map(h => String(h).trim().replace(/^\uFEFF/, ''));
  const rows = csvData.slice(1);

  // Define headers and find column indexes in the uploaded file
  const targetHeaders = [
    "Reference Code", "SKU", "Product Name", "EAN", "Item Quantity", "Box ID",
    "Box Weight", "Box Width", "Box Height", "Box Length", "Item Price(Excluding Tax)", "Value"
  ];
  const colMap = {};
  targetHeaders.slice(0, -1).forEach(h => { // All headers except the calculated 'Value'
    const index = headers.indexOf(h);
    if (index === -1) throw new Error(`Required column "${h}" not found in uploaded file.`);
    colMap[h] = index;
  });

  // =========================================================================
// Step 3: Validate Box Dimensions and Filter Data
// =========================================================================

// Track orders that have invalid box data
const invalidOrders = new Set();

// First pass: detect invalid orders
rows.forEach(row => {

  const refCode = (row[colMap["Reference Code"]] || "").replace(/`/g, '').trim();

  const weight = row[colMap["Box Weight"]];
  const width = row[colMap["Box Width"]];
  const height = row[colMap["Box Height"]];
  const length = row[colMap["Box Length"]];

  // If any dimension missing → mark order invalid
  if (!weight || !width || !height || !length) {
    invalidOrders.add(refCode);
  }
});

const rowsToAppend = [];

// Second pass: process only valid rows
rows.forEach(row => {

  const refCode = (row[colMap["Reference Code"]] || "").replace(/`/g, '').trim();

  // Skip if not processable OR marked invalid
  if (!refCode || !processableRefCodes.has(refCode) || invalidOrders.has(refCode)) return;

  const quantity = parseFloat(row[colMap["Item Quantity"]]) || 0;
  const priceExclTax = parseFloat(row[colMap["Item Price(Excluding Tax)"]]) || 0;
  const calculatedValue = quantity * priceExclTax * 1.05;

  rowsToAppend.push([
    refCode,
    row[colMap["SKU"]],
    row[colMap["Product Name"]],
    row[colMap["EAN"]],
    quantity,
    row[colMap["Box ID"]],
    row[colMap["Box Weight"]],
    row[colMap["Box Width"]],
    row[colMap["Box Height"]],
    row[colMap["Box Length"]],
    priceExclTax,
    calculatedValue.toFixed(2)
  ]);

});

if (invalidOrders.size > 0) {
  Logger.log(`Skipped ${invalidOrders.size} orders due to missing box dimensions.`);
}

  // =========================================================================
  // Step 4: Save the Filtered Data to the Master Sheet
  // =========================================================================
  if (rowsToAppend.length > 0) {
    let targetSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_MASTER_DATA);
    if (!targetSheet) {
      targetSheet = ss.insertSheet(SHEET_MASTER_DATA);
      targetSheet.appendRow(targetHeaders);
    }
    
    targetSheet.getRange(targetSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rowsToAppend.length, targetHeaders.length)
      .setValues(rowsToAppend);
    
    console.log(`Successfully processed and appended ${rowsToAppend.length} valid rows.`);
  } else {
    console.log("No matching rows found in the uploaded file for the processable POs.");
  }

  updatePoDatabaseWithBoxDataStatus();
  
  return rowsToAppend.length;
}

/**
 * **UPDATED & MORE POWERFUL:** This function now calculates the count of unique
 * 'Box ID's for each 'Reference Code' in the 'Master_Packing_Data' sheet. It then
 * updates the 'Box Data' column in the 'PO_Database' with this count.
 *
 * @return {number} The number of rows that were updated.
 */
function updatePoDatabaseWithBoxDataStatus() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const packingSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_MASTER_DATA);

  if (!packingSheet || packingSheet.getLastRow() < 2 || !dbSheet || dbSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
    Logger.log("One or both sheets are missing or empty. Aborting status update.");
    return 0;
  }

  // =========================================================================
  // THE NEW LOGIC STARTS HERE
  // =========================================================================

  // --- Step 1: Create a Map of PO Number -> Count of Unique Box IDs ---
  const packingData = packingSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const packingHeaders = packingData.shift();
  const packingRefCodeIndex = packingHeaders.indexOf("Reference Code");
  const packingBoxIdIndex = packingHeaders.indexOf("Box ID");

  if (packingRefCodeIndex === -1 || packingBoxIdIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error: 'Reference Code' or 'Box ID' column not found in 'Master_Packing_Data'.");
    return 0;
  }
  
  // Use .reduce() to efficiently build the count map.
  const poToBoxCountMap = packingData.reduce((acc, row) => {
    const refCode = String(row[packingRefCodeIndex]).trim();
    const boxId = String(row[packingBoxIdIndex]).trim();

    if (refCode && boxId) {
      // If we haven't seen this PO before, initialize it with a new Set.
      if (!acc[refCode]) {
        acc[refCode] = new Set();
      }
      // Add the Box ID to the Set. Sets automatically handle uniqueness.
      acc[refCode].add(boxId);
    }
    return acc;
  }, {});

  // Convert the Set sizes to simple counts.
  for (const refCode in poToBoxCountMap) {
    poToBoxCountMap[refCode] = poToBoxCountMap[refCode].size;
  }
  Logger.log(`Created a map with unique box counts for ${Object.keys(poToBoxCountMap).length} POs.`);

  // --- Step 2: Read the PO Database and prepare updates in memory ---
  const dbRange = dbSheet.getDataRange();
  const dbData = dbRange.getValues();
  const dbHeaders = dbData.shift();

  const dbPoNumIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("EE Order Ref ID");
  const dbBoxDataIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("Box Data");

  if (dbPoNumIndex === -1 || dbBoxDataIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error: 'PO Number' or 'Box Data' column not found in 'PO_Database'.");
    return 0;
  }
  
  let updatesMade = 0;
  // Create a 2D array to hold the new values for the 'Box Data' column.
  const newBoxDataColumn = dbData.map(row => {
    const poNum = String(row[dbPoNumIndex]).trim();
    
    // Check if our new map has a box count for this PO Number.
    if (poToBoxCountMap.hasOwnProperty(poNum)) {
      const boxCount = poToBoxCountMap[poNum];
      const currentBoxCount = row[dbBoxDataIndex];

      // Only update if the new count is different from the current one.
      if (boxCount !== currentBoxCount) {
        updatesMade++;
        return [boxCount]; // Return the count of unique boxes.
      }
    }
    // If no match or if the count is the same, keep the existing value.
    return [row[dbBoxDataIndex]]; 
  });

  // --- Step 3: Perform a single, efficient batch update ---
  if (updatesMade > 0) {
    dbSheet.getRange(2, dbBoxDataIndex + 1, newBoxDataColumn.length, 1).setValues(newBoxDataColumn);
    Logger.log(`Successfully updated box counts for ${updatesMade} rows.`);
  } else {
    Logger.log('No new box counts to update.');
  }
  
  return updatesMade;
}

function createInventoryItem(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  if (!sheet) return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Inventory sheet not found'});
  
  sheet.appendRow([
    data.channel, data.articleCode, data.sku, data.spIncTax || 0, data.stock || 0, data.ean || '', data.itemName || '', data.mrp || 0
  ]);
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'Item created'});
}

function updateInventoryPrice(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  
  // Find indexes
  const headers = rows[0].map(h => String(h).toLowerCase().trim());
  const colChannel = headers.indexOf('channel');
  let colArticle = headers.indexOf('channel item code');
  if (colArticle === -1) colArticle = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('item code') || h.includes('article'));
  let colPrice = headers.indexOf('selling price');
  if (colPrice === -1) colPrice = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('selling') || h.includes('sp'));

  if (colChannel === -1 || colArticle === -1 || colPrice === -1) {
    return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Required columns not found'});
  }
  
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    const rowChannel = String(rows[i][colChannel]).trim();
    const rowArticle = String(rows[i][colArticle]).trim();
    if (rowChannel.toLowerCase() === data.channel.toLowerCase() && rowArticle === String(data.articleCode)) {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, colPrice + 1).setValue(data.newPrice);
      return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'Price updated'});
    }
  }
  return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Item not found'});
}

function saveChannelConfig(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp
    .openById(SPREADSHEET_ID)
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);

  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0].map(h => String(h).toLowerCase().trim());

  const nameIdx = headers.indexOf('channel name');
  if (nameIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error('Channel Name column not found');
  }

  let rowIndex = -1;

  // Find existing row
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (
      String(rows[i][nameIdx]).toLowerCase() ===
      String(data.channelName).toLowerCase()
    ) {
      rowIndex = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  const getCol = (name) => {
    const idx = headers.indexOf(name.toLowerCase());
    return idx === -1 ? -1 : idx + 1;
  };

  const mapping = {
    status: getCol('status'),
    sourceEmail: getCol('source email'),
    searchKeyword: getCol('search keyword'),
    minOrderThreshold: getCol('min order threshold'),
    pocName: getCol('poc name'),
    pocEmail: getCol('poc email'),
    pocPhone: getCol('poc phone'),
    appointmentTo: getCol('appointment to'),
    appointmentCc: getCol('appointment cc')
  };

  if (rowIndex > 0) {
    // Update
    Object.keys(mapping).forEach(key => {
      if (mapping[key] > 0 && key in data) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, mapping[key]).setValue(data[key]);
      }
    });
    return responseJSON({ status: 'success', message: 'Channel updated' });
  } else {
    // Create
    const newRow = new Array(headers.length).fill('');
    newRow[nameIdx] = data.channelName;

    Object.keys(mapping).forEach(key => {
      if (mapping[key] > 0 && key in data) {
        newRow[mapping[key] - 1] = data[key];
      }
    });

    sheet.appendRow(newRow);
    return responseJSON({ status: 'success', message: 'Channel created' });
  }
}

function saveSystemConfig(data) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  if (data.easyecom_token) props.setProperty('EASY_ECOM_TOKEN', data.easyecom_token);
  if (data.easyecom_email) props.setProperty('EASY_ECOM_EMAIL', data.easyecom_email);
  if (data.nimbus_notification_email) props.setProperty('NIMBUS_NOTIFICATION_EMAIL', data.nimbus_notification_email);
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'Config saved'});
}

function getSystemConfig() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  return responseJSON({
    status: 'success',
    data: {
      easyecom_url: EASYECOM_ORDERS_URL,
      easyecom_email: props.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_EMAIL') || '',
      easyecom_token: props.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_TOKEN') ? '********' : '', // Masked
      nimbus_notification_email : props.getProperty('NIMBUS_NOTIFICATION_EMAIL') || '', // Masked
    }
  });
}


// --- USER MANAGEMENT FUNCTIONS ---

function saveUser(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_USERS);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0];
  const idIdx = headers.indexOf('ID');
  
  let found = false;
  // Check if user exists to update
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][idIdx]) === String(data.id)) {
      const range = sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, headers.length);
      const newRow = headers.map(h => {
        if (h === 'ID') return data.id;
        if (h === 'Name') return data.name;
        if (h === 'Email') return data.email;
        if (h === 'Contact') return data.contactNumber;
        if (h === 'Role') return data.role;
        if (h === 'Avatar') return data.avatarInitials;
        return '';
      });
      range.setValues([newRow]);
      found = true;
      break;
    }
  }
  
  if (!found) {
    sheet.appendRow([data.id, data.name, data.email, data.contactNumber, data.role, data.avatarInitials]);
  }
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'User saved'});
}

function deleteUser(userId) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_USERS);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const idIdx = rows[0].indexOf('ID');
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][idIdx]) === String(userId)) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
      break;
    }
  }
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'User deleted'});
}

// ==========================================
// 4. AUTOMATION: EMAIL PROCESSING (Gmail)
// ==========================================

function processPurchaseOrders() {

  updateZohoItemIDs();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
  const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

  // -------------------------------
  // Gmail Label Setup
  // -------------------------------
  const LABEL_NAME = 'ProcessedPO';
  let processedLabel = GmailApp.getUserLabelByName(LABEL_NAME);
  if (!processedLabel) {
    processedLabel = GmailApp.createLabel(LABEL_NAME);
  }

  const lastRow = configSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  const configData = configSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 4).getValues();

  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const BUFFER_SECONDS = 5 * 60;
  let startTime = parseInt(scriptProperties.getProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME') || '0');

  if (startTime === 0) {
    const d = new Date();
    d.setDate(d.getDate() - 1);
    startTime = Math.floor(d.getTime() / 1000);
  }

  startTime = startTime - BUFFER_SECONDS;

  const currentRunTime = Math.floor(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
  const newLogs = [];


  const processedMessageIds = new Set();

  // =============================================
  // PROCESS CHANNELS
  // =============================================

  configData.forEach(row => {

    const [channelName, status, rawEmails, subjectKeyword] = row;

    if (!channelName || !rawEmails || String(status).toLowerCase() !== 'active') return;

    const channelKey = channelName.toLowerCase();

    const emailList = rawEmails.split(',').map(e => e.trim()).filter(Boolean);

    if (emailList.length === 0) return;

    const fromClause = `from:(${emailList.join(' OR ')})`;

    // ✅ INCLUDE AMAZON EMAILS ALSO
    let query = `${fromClause} -from:me after:${startTime} -label:${LABEL_NAME}`;
    if (subjectKeyword) query += ` subject:("${subjectKeyword}")`;

    try {

      const threads = GmailApp.search(query);
      if (threads.length === 0) return;

      const allMessages = GmailApp.getMessagesForThreads(threads);

      allMessages.forEach(messages => {

        messages.forEach(message => {

          const messageId = message.getId();
          if (processedMessageIds.has(messageId)) return;

          if (Math.floor(message.getDate().getTime() / 1000) <= startTime) return;

          const sender = message.getFrom().toLowerCase();
          const subject = message.getSubject();
          const emailBody = message.getPlainBody();
          const attachments = message.getAttachments();

          Logger.log(`Processing Email → ${subject}`);

          // ======================================================
          // 🔥 AMAZON PICKUP HANDLING
          // ======================================================

          if (isAmazonPickupEmail(sender, subject)) {

            const shipmentId = extractShipmentId(subject);
            const pickupSlotRaw = extractPickupSlot(emailBody);
            const pickupSlot = formatPickupSlot(pickupSlotRaw);

            if (shipmentId && pickupSlot) {
              updateAmazonPickup(shipmentId, pickupSlot);
            } else {
              Logger.log("Amazon extraction failed");
            }

            message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
            return;
          }
          

          // ======================================================
          // 🔍 METADATA
          // ======================================================

          const metadata = analyzeEmailMetadata(
            channelKey,
            subject,
            subject.toUpperCase(),
            emailBody
          );

          // ======================================================
          // 🔥 REVISION HANDLING
          // ======================================================

          const isRevised = isRevisedEmail(subject, emailBody);

          if (isRevised && metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") {

            const poNumber = metadata.poNumber;
            const finalChannel = channelName || channelKey;

            Logger.log(`Revision detected → ${poNumber}`);

            // -----------------------
            // Appointment (BODY)
            // -----------------------
            const appointmentDate = extractAppointmentFromBody(emailBody);

            let expiryDate = "";

            // -----------------------
            // Expiry (ATTACHMENT)
            // -----------------------

            if (attachments.length > 0) {

              const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
              const channelThresholds = loadChannelThresholds(ss);

              for (let att of attachments) {

                try {

                  const fileName = att.getName().toLowerCase();
                  const blob = att.copyBlob();

                  let rawData = null;

                  if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
                    rawData = Utilities.parseCsv(blob.getDataAsString());
                  }
                  else if (fileName.endsWith(".xls") || fileName.endsWith(".xlsx")) {
                    rawData = getExcelDataViaBlobFromAttachment(blob);
                  }
                  else if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {

                    const tempFile = DriveApp.createFile(blob);
                    rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(tempFile.getId());
                    tempFile.setTrashed(true);
                  }

                  if (!rawData) continue;

                  const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
                    rawData,
                    finalChannel,
                    poNumber,
                    metadata.storeCode,
                    skuMapping,
                    {},
                    channelThresholds,
                    new Date()
                  );

                  if (extracted && extracted.length > 0) {
                    expiryDate = extracted[0][6];
                    break;
                  }

                } catch (e) {
                  Logger.log("Attachment parse error: " + e.message);
                }
              }
            }

            if (!expiryDate) {
              Logger.log(`No expiry extracted for ${poNumber}`);
            }

            // -----------------------
            // UPDATE DB
            // -----------------------

            const changes = updateExistingPO(poNumber, {
              appointmentDate,
              expiryDate
            });

            // -----------------------
            // UPDATE REPO STATUS
            // -----------------------

            try {

              const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
              const repoData = repoSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
              const headers = repoData[0];

              const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

              const IDX = {
                PO: col("PO Number"),
                STATUS: col("Status")
              };

              for (let i = 1; i < repoData.length; i++) {

                const repoPo = String(repoData[i][IDX.PO]).trim();

                if (repoPo === poNumber) {

                  if (changes.length > 0) {
                    repoSheet.getRange(i + 1, IDX.STATUS + 1)
                      .setValue(`Updated → ${changes.join(" | ")}`);
                  } else {
                    repoSheet.getRange(i + 1, IDX.STATUS + 1)
                      .setValue("Checked (No Change)");
                  }
                }
              }

            } catch (e) {
              Logger.log("Repo update error: " + e.message);
            }

            message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
            return;
          }

          // ======================================================
          // 🟢 NORMAL PO FLOW (UNCHANGED)
          // ======================================================

          let successfullyProcessed = false;

          if (attachments.length > 0) {

            attachments.forEach(att => {

              try {

                const blob = att.copyBlob();
                const file = folder.createFile(blob);
                file.setName(`[${channelName}] ${att.getName()}`);

                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(),
                  channelName,
                  sender,
                  subject,
                  att.getName(),
                  file.getUrl(),
                  metadata.category,
                  metadata.poNumber,
                  metadata.storeCode,
                  ""
                ]);

                successfullyProcessed = true;

              } catch (e) {

                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(),
                  channelName,
                  sender,
                  subject,
                  att.getName(),
                  "SAVE FAILED",
                  "Error",
                  metadata.poNumber,
                  metadata.storeCode,
                  e.message
                ]);
              }
            });

          } else {

            if (metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") {

              newLogs.push([
                message.getDate(),
                channelName,
                sender,
                subject,
                "No Attachment",
                "",
                metadata.category,
                metadata.poNumber,
                metadata.storeCode,
                ""
              ]);

              successfullyProcessed = true;
            }
          }

          if (successfullyProcessed) {
            message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
          }

        });
      });

    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log(`Error processing ${channelName}: ${e.message}`);
    }

  });

  // =============================================
  // FINAL WRITE
  // =============================================

  if (newLogs.length > 0) {

    logSheet
      .getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, newLogs.length, newLogs[0].length)
      .setValues(newLogs);
  }

  const SAFE_OFFSET = 60;
  const newRunTime = currentRunTime - SAFE_OFFSET;

  scriptProperties.setProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME', newRunTime.toString());
}

/**
 * **UPDATED & ROBUST:** This function now prevents duplicate processing by using
 * Gmail labels ('ProcessedPO') and in-memory Message ID tracking.
 */
function processPurchaseOrdersold() {
  updateZohoItemIDs();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
  const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

  // --- NEW: Setup the Gmail Label ---
  const LABEL_NAME = 'ProcessedPO';
  let processedLabel = GmailApp.getUserLabelByName(LABEL_NAME);
  if (!processedLabel) {
    Logger.log(`Creating missing Gmail label: ${LABEL_NAME}`);
    processedLabel = GmailApp.createLabel(LABEL_NAME);
  }

  // 1. Get Config & Timer Logic
  const lastRow = configSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;
  const configData = configSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 4).getValues();
  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const BUFFER_SECONDS = 5 * 60; // 5 mins
  let startTime = parseInt(scriptProperties.getProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME') || '0');

  if (startTime === 0) {
    const threeDaysAgo = new Date();
    threeDaysAgo.setDate(threeDaysAgo.getDate() - 1);
    startTime = Math.floor(threeDaysAgo.getTime() / 1000);
  }

    // 🔥 APPLY BUFFER
  startTime = startTime - BUFFER_SECONDS;

  if (startTime === 0) {
    const threeDaysAgo = new Date();
    threeDaysAgo.setDate(threeDaysAgo.getDate() - 1);
    startTime = Math.floor(threeDaysAgo.getTime() / 1000);
    
  }

  const currentRunTime = Math.floor(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
  const newLogs = [];
  
  
  // --- NEW: Track processed IDs during this run to prevent instant duplicates ---
  const processedMessageIds = new Set();

  // 2. Process Channels
  configData.forEach(row => {
    const [channelName, status, rawEmails, subjectKeyword] = row;
    if (!channelName || !rawEmails || String(status).toLowerCase() !== 'active') return;

    const channelKey = channelName.toLowerCase();
    const emailList = rawEmails.split(',').map(e => e.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    if (emailList.length === 0) return;
     
    const fromClause = `from:(${emailList.join(' OR ')})`;
    
    // --- THE CHANGE IS HERE: Exclude emails that already have the label ---
    let query = `${fromClause} -from:me after:${startTime} -label:${LABEL_NAME}`;
    if (subjectKeyword) query += ` subject:("${subjectKeyword}")`;

    try {
      const threads = GmailApp.search(query);
      if (threads.length === 0) return;

      const allThreadMessages = GmailApp.getMessagesForThreads(threads);
      allThreadMessages.forEach(messages => {
        messages.forEach(message => {
          // --- THE SECOND CHANGE IS HERE: Check the in-memory Set ---
          const messageId = message.getId();
          if (processedMessageIds.has(messageId)) return; // Skip if already seen this run
          
          if (Math.floor(message.getDate().getTime() / 1000) <= startTime) return;
          const sender = message.getFrom().toLowerCase();
          if (!emailList.some(e => sender.includes(e.toLowerCase()))) return;

          const attachments = message.getAttachments();
          const subject = message.getSubject();
          const emailBody = message.getPlainBody();
          const metadata = analyzeEmailMetadata(channelKey, subject, subject.toUpperCase(), emailBody);

          // ======================================================
// 🔥 AMAZON FBA PICKUP HANDLING
// ======================================================

if (isAmazonPickupEmail(sender, subject)) {

  const shipmentId = extractShipmentId(subject);
  const pickupSlot = extractPickupSlot(emailBody);

  Logger.log(`Amazon Pickup Email Detected → ${shipmentId}`);

  if (shipmentId && pickupSlot) {

    updateAmazonPickup(shipmentId, pickupSlot);

  } else {

    Logger.log(`Amazon Pickup Extraction Failed → Subject: ${subject}`);
  }

  // Mark processed
  message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
  processedMessageIds.add(message.getId());

  return; // 🚀 STOP further processing
}

          // ======================================================
// 🔥 FINAL: REVISED / AMENDMENT PO HANDLING
// ======================================================

const isRevised = isRevisedEmail(subject, emailBody);

if (isRevised && metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") 
{

  const poNumber = metadata.poNumber;
  const channelName = channelNameGlobal || channelName || channelKey;

  Logger.log(`Revised PO detected: ${poNumber}`);

  // --------------------------------------
  // 1. Appointment Date → EMAIL BODY
  // --------------------------------------

  const appointmentDate = extractAppointmentFromBody(emailBody);

  let expiryDate = "";

  // --------------------------------------
  // 2. Expiry Date → ATTACHMENT (CHANNEL PARSER)
  // --------------------------------------

  if (attachments.length > 0) {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
    const channelThresholds = loadChannelThresholds(ss);

    for (let att of attachments) {

      try {

        const fileName = att.getName().toLowerCase();
        const blob = att.copyBlob();

        let rawData = null;

        if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
          rawData = Utilities.parseCsv(blob.getDataAsString());
        }
        else if (fileName.endsWith(".xls") || fileName.endsWith(".xlsx")) {
          rawData = getExcelDataViaBlobFromAttachment(blob);
        }
        else if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {

          const tempFile = DriveApp.createFile(blob);
          rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(tempFile.getId());
          tempFile.setTrashed(true);
        }

        if (!rawData) continue;

        // 🚀 USE YOUR EXISTING CHANNEL PARSER
        const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
          rawData,
          channelName,
          poNumber,
          metadata.storeCode,
          skuMapping,
          {}, // pdfMap not needed
          channelThresholds,
          new Date()
        );

        if (extracted && extracted.length > 0) {

          // Expiry Date = Column index 6
          expiryDate = extracted[0][6];

          Logger.log(`Expiry extracted: ${expiryDate}`);
          break;
        }

      } catch (e) {
        Logger.log("Attachment parsing error: " + e.message);
      }
    }
    }

  // --------------------------------------
  // 3. UPDATE DB (ONLY IF PO EXISTS)
  // --------------------------------------

  const changes = updateExistingPO(poNumber, {
  appointmentDate,
  expiryDate
});

// --------------------------------------
// 🔥 UPDATE PO REPOSITORY STATUS
// --------------------------------------

  if (changes.length > 0) {

  const changeText = changes.join(" | ");

  Logger.log(`PO Updated (${poNumber}) → ${changeText}`);

  // ✅ Update Repo Sheet Status
  try {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);

    const repoData = repoSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const repoHeaders = repoData[0];

    const col = name => repoHeaders.indexOf(name);

    const IDX = {
      PO: col("PO Number"),
      STATUS: col("Status")
    };

    for (let i = 1; i < repoData.length; i++) {

      const repoPo = String(repoData[i][IDX.PO]).trim();

      if (repoPo === poNumber) {

        repoSheet
          .getRange(i + 1, IDX.STATUS + 1)
          .setValue(`Updated → ${changeText}`);
      }
    }

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log("Repo update error: " + e.message);
  }

} else {

  Logger.log(`No changes for PO: ${poNumber}`);

  // Optional: mark as checked
  try {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);

    const repoData = repoSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const repoHeaders = repoData[0];

    const col = name => repoHeaders.indexOf(name);

    const IDX = {
      PO: col("PO Number"),
      STATUS: col("Status")
    };

    for (let i = 1; i < repoData.length; i++) {

      const repoPo = String(repoData[i][IDX.PO]).trim();

      if (repoPo === poNumber) {

        repoSheet
          .getRange(i + 1, IDX.STATUS + 1)
          .setValue("Checked (No Change)");
      }
    }

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log("Repo update error: " + e.message);
  }
}

  if (updates.length > 0) {
    Logger.log(`PO Updated (${poNumber}) → ${updates.join(", ")}`);
  } else {
    Logger.log(`No changes for PO: ${poNumber}`);
  }

  

  // --------------------------------------
  // 4. MARK EMAIL PROCESSED
  // --------------------------------------

  message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
  processedMessageIds.add(message.getId());

  return; // 🚀 STOP normal flow
}
          
          let successfullyProcessed = false; // Flag to track if we should label it

          if (attachments.length > 0) {
            // --- CASE 1: Attachments EXIST ---
            attachments.forEach(att => {
              const fileName = att.getName();
              try {
                const blob = att.copyBlob();
                if (fileName.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls')) {
                  blob.setContentType(MimeType.MICROSOFT_EXCEL_LEGACY);
                }

                const file = folder.createFile(blob);
                file.setName(`[${channelName}] ${fileName}`);

                let finalPO = metadata.poNumber === "Not Found" ? extractPOFromText(channelKey, fileName.toUpperCase()) : metadata.poNumber;
                let finalCategory = metadata.category === "New PO" ? determineCategory(fileName.toUpperCase()) : metadata.category;

                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, fileName,
                  file.getUrl(), finalCategory, finalPO, metadata.storeCode, ""
                ]);
                
                successfullyProcessed = true; // Mark as success

              } catch (e) {
                Logger.log(`ERROR: Failed to save attachment "${fileName}". Error: ${e.message}`);
                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, fileName,
                  "SAVE FAILED", "Error", metadata.poNumber, metadata.storeCode, e.message
                ]);
              }
            });
          } else {
            // --- CASE 2: NO Attachments ---
            if (metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") {
              newLogs.push([
                message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, "No Attachment",
                "", metadata.category, metadata.poNumber, metadata.storeCode, ""
              ]);
              successfullyProcessed = true; // Mark as success
            }
          }
          
          // --- FINAL STEP: Apply Label and remember the ID ---
          if (successfullyProcessed) {
            try {
              // Apply the label to the specific message's thread
              message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            } catch(e) {
              Logger.log(`Warning: Failed to apply label to message ${messageId}.`);
            }
            // Add the ID to our set to prevent duplicate processing in the same run
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
          }
          
        });
      });
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(`Error processing ${channelName}: ${e.message}`);
    }
  });

  // 3. Batch Write Logs & Update Timer
  if (newLogs.length > 0) {
    newLogs.sort((a, b) => new Date(a[0]) - new Date(b[0]));
    logSheet.getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, newLogs.length, newLogs[0].length).setValues(newLogs);
    console.log(`Successfully processed ${newLogs.length} new log entries.`);
  }
  
  const SAFE_OFFSET = 60; // 1 min safety
  const newRunTime = currentRunTime - SAFE_OFFSET;
  scriptProperties.setProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME', newRunTime.toString());
}

// =================================================================================
// FRONT-END FILE UPLOAD PROCESSOR
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **NEW MAIN FUNCTION FOR UPLOADS:** Called from a front-end UI. It receives a file,
 * analyzes it to determine the channel, uploads it to Drive, and logs the details
 * to the 'PO_Repository' sheet, mirroring the email processing logic.
 *
 * @param {string} base64Data - The base64 encoded string of the file.
 * @param {string} fileName - The original name of the uploaded file.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a message.
 */
/**
 * **UPDATED:** Called from a front-end UI. It now includes specific logic
 * to extract the PO number directly from filenames formatted as 'purchase_order_{PO_ID}'.
 *
 * @param {string} base64Data - The base64 encoded string of the file.
 * @param {string} fileName - The original name of the uploaded file.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a message.
 */
function ProcessFlipkartMinutesPO(base64Data, fileName) {
  try {
    if (!base64Data || !fileName) {
      throw new Error("File data or file name is missing.");
    }
    
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);

    const decoded = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decoded, MimeType.MICROSOFT_EXCEL_LEGACY, fileName);
    // =========================================================================
    // THE CHANGE IS HERE: Extract the PO Number from the filename first.
    // =========================================================================
    let poNum = "";
    
    // Use a regex to match the pattern 'purchase_order_{PO_ID}'
    const poMatch = fileName.match(/purchase_order_([A-Z0-9]+)/i);
    if (poMatch && poMatch[1]) 
    {
      poNum = poMatch[1];
      Logger.log(`Extracted PO Number "${poNum}" directly from the filename.`);
    }
        
    // --- The rest of the function continues as before ---
    
    const file = folder.createFile(blob);
    file.setName(`${fileName}`);
    const fileUrl = file.getUrl();
    
    const newLog = [
      new Date(),
      "FlipkartMinutes",
      "Manual Upload",
      fileName,
      fileName,
      fileUrl,
      "New PO",
      poNum
    ];

    logSheet.getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, newLog.length).setValues([newLog]);
    
    const successMessage = `Successfully processed and logged PO "${poNum}" for Flipkartminutes".`;
    Logger.log(successMessage);
    extractDatabaseDetails();
    return { status: "success", message: successMessage, fileUrl: fileUrl, poNumber: poNum };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR during manual upload processing: ${e.message}`);
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}


  /**
 * **CORRECTED & ROBUST:** Analyzes email metadata with a proper if/else if structure
 * to ensure only one channel's logic runs per email.
 */
function analyzeEmailMetadata(channelKey, subjectOriginal, subjectUpper, emailBody) {
  // These calls get the category and PO number using your other existing functions.
  let category = determineCategory(subjectUpper); 
  let poNumber = extractPOFromText(channelKey, subjectUpper); 
  let storeCode = ""; // Default to blank

  // Safety check for the email body, which is required by some parsers.
  const body = emailBody || "";

  // Use a proper if/else if chain to ensure only one block executes.
  if (channelKey.includes("instamart") && category === "New PO") {
    const match = subjectOriginal.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_STORE_NEW);
    if (match) storeCode = match[1].trim();
  } 
  // --- FIX: Changed 'if' to 'else if' ---
  else if (channelKey.includes("bb") || channelKey.includes("bigbasket")) {
    const storeMatch = subjectOriginal.match(PATTERNS.BIGBASKET_STORE);
    if (storeMatch && storeMatch[1]) {
      storeCode = storeMatch[1].trim();
      Logger.log("SUCCESS: Extracted BigBasket store code: '" + storeCode + "'");
    } else {
      Logger.log("Warning: Could not extract BigBasket store code from subject: " + subjectOriginal);
    }
  }
  else if (channelKey.includes("blinkit") && subjectUpper.includes("PO_BCPL")) {
    category = "New PO";
    const extractionRegex = /^\*?\s*Bill To:\*?\s*BCPL - (.*)/im;
    const storeMatch = body.match(extractionRegex);
    if (storeMatch && storeMatch[1]) {
      let rawStoreCode = storeMatch[1].trim();
      Logger.log("Found raw store code: '" + rawStoreCode + "'");

      // =========================================================================
      // THE FINAL FIX IS HERE: A simple, non-regex, step-by-step method.
      // =========================================================================
      
      let lowerCaseCode = rawStoreCode.toLowerCase();
      let basePart = "";
      let warehousePart = "";

      // 1. Identify which warehouse suffix the string has.
      if (lowerCaseCode.endsWith(' feeder warehouse')) {
        // Get the part of the string BEFORE " feeder warehouse"
        basePart = rawStoreCode.substring(0, rawStoreCode.length - 17);
        warehousePart = 'Feeder Warehouse';
      } else if (lowerCaseCode.endsWith(' warehouse')) {
        // Get the part of the string BEFORE " warehouse"
        basePart = rawStoreCode.substring(0, rawStoreCode.length - 10);
        warehousePart = 'Warehouse';
      }

      // 2. If we found a warehouse part, clean up the base and re-join them.
      if (basePart && warehousePart) {
        // This is the key step: Remove any trailing space or hyphen from the base part.
        // The regex `/\s*-?\s*$/` matches optional spaces, an optional hyphen, and optional spaces at the end of the string.
        let cleanedBase = basePart.replace(/\s*-?\s*$/, '');
        
        // Reconstruct the string with the standardized separator.
        storeCode = `${cleanedBase} - ${warehousePart}`;
      } else {
        // If the string doesn't end with a known warehouse type, use it as-is.
        storeCode = rawStoreCode;
      }
      
      Logger.log("SUCCESS: Final formatted Blinkit store code: '" + storeCode + "'");
      
    }
    else {
      Logger.log("Warning: Could not find Blinkit 'Bill To:' details in email body.");
    }
  }
   
  return { category, poNumber, storeCode };
}



function determineCategory(text) {

  // 🔥 1. AMAZON FIRST (highest priority)
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_AMAZON_PICKUP.test(text)) {
    return "Amazon Pickup";
  }

  // Existing logic
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_GRN.test(text)) return "GRN";
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_REV.test(text)) return "Revision";
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_CANC.test(text)) return "Cancellation";
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_APP.test(text)) return "Appointment Confirmation";

  return "New PO";
}

function extractPOFromText(channelKey, text) {
  if (!text) return "Not Found";
  let match;
  if (channelKey.includes("zepto")) match = text.match(PATTERNS.ZEPTO_PO);
  else if (channelKey.includes("instamart")) {
    match = text.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_UNDERSCORE) || text.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_STANDARD);
    if (match && text.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_UNDERSCORE)) return match[1]; 
  }
  else if (channelKey.includes("bb")) {
  match = text.match(PATTERNS.BIGBASKET_ID); // Use the new, correct regex
  if (match) return match[1]; // Return ONLY the captured part (e.g., "IRM30207487")
  }
  else if (channelKey.includes("rbl") || channelKey.includes("reliance")) match = text.match(PATTERNS.RBL_PO);
  else if (channelKey.includes("blinkit")) {
    match = text.match(PATTERNS.BLINKIT_PO);
    if (match) return match[1];
  }
  
  if (!match) match = text.match(PATTERNS.GENERIC_PO);
  return match ? match[0] : "Not Found";
}

// ==========================================
// 5. AUTOMATION: DATA EXTRACTION (Repo -> DB)
// ==========================================


/**
 * **CORRECTED:** Extracts details from the PO Repository, parses attachments,
 * and logs the results to the PO Database. It now correctly handles .pdf data
 * files for channels like Starmark.
 */
function extractDatabaseDetailsold() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  // Load Mapping Data
  const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
  const channelThresholds = loadChannelThresholds(ss);

  const lastRow = repoSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;
