  const repoRange = repoSheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 13);
  const repoData = repoRange.getValues();
  
  const headers = repoData.shift(); 
  const dataRows = repoData; 

  const channelIndex = headers.indexOf("Channel Name");
  const fileNameIndex = headers.indexOf("File Name");
  const fileUrlIndex = headers.indexOf("Drive Link"); // Assuming you changed header to "Drive Link"
  const categoryIndex = headers.indexOf("Category");
  const poNumIndex = headers.indexOf("PO Number");
  const statusIndex = headers.indexOf("Status"); 
  const appointmentIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment ID");
  const appointmentDateIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment Date");
  const appointmentTimeIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment Time");

  // --- Build the pdfMap ---
  const pdfMap = {};
  dataRows.forEach(row => {
    const channelName = String(row[channelIndex]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const fileName = String(row[fileNameIndex]).toLowerCase();
    const category = String(row[categoryIndex]);
    const status = String(row[statusIndex]);
    const poNumber = String(row[poNumIndex]).trim();
    const fileUrl = row[fileUrlIndex];

    if (!poNumber || !fileUrl) return;

    switch (channelName) {
      case 'bb':
      case 'flipkartminutes':
        if (category === "New PO" && status === "" && (fileName.endsWith(".xls") || fileName.endsWith(".xlsx"))) {
          pdfMap[poNumber] = fileUrl;
        }
        break;
      default:
        // For standard channels and Starmark, the PDF is the reference file
        if (category === "New PO" && fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {
          pdfMap[poNumber] = fileUrl;
        }
        break;
    }
  });

  let databaseRows = [];
  const rowsToUpdate = {}; 
  const rowsToSkip = [];

  // --- Data Processing Loop ---
  dataRows.forEach((row, index) => {
    const rowIndexInSheet = index + 2; 
    const currentStatus = row[statusIndex];
    const fileUrl = row[fileUrlIndex];
    const category = row[categoryIndex];
    const fileName = String(row[fileNameIndex]).toLowerCase();
    const channelName = String(row[channelIndex]).trim();

    if (currentStatus === "" && fileUrl && category === "New PO") {
      
      // =========================================================================
      // THE FIX IS HERE: Added 'pdf' to the allowed extensions.
      // =========================================================================
      const isDataFile = fileName.match(/\.(xls|xlsx|csv|pdf)$/);
      
      if (isDataFile) {
        const fileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(fileUrl);
        if (fileId) {
          try {
            let rawData;
            
            // =========================================================================
            // NEW LOGIC: Handle PDF data extraction for specific channels (Starmark)
            // =========================================================================
            if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {
              //Logger.log(fileId);
               // Only try to parse data from a PDF if it's for a channel we know how to parse (like Starmark)
               if (channelName.toLowerCase().includes('starmark')) {
                   // Extract text from the PDF using Google Docs OCR (requires Drive API)
                   rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(fileId);
                   //Logger.log(rawData);
               } else {
                   // If it's a PDF but NOT Starmark (e.g. Zepto), we don't parse it for data.
                   // It's just a reference file.
                   rawData = null;
                   rowsToSkip.push(rowIndexInSheet); // We don't process it, so skip it.
               }
            } else if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
               rawData = getCsvData(fileId);
            } else {
               rawData = getExcelDataViaBlob(fileId);
            }

            // Only attempt parsing if we actually extracted rawData
            if (rawData) {
              const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(rawData, channelName, row[poNumIndex], row[headers.indexOf("Store Code")], skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds, row[0]);
              
              if (extracted && extracted.length > 0) {
                databaseRows = databaseRows.concat(extracted);
                rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Extracted";
              } else {
                rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Extracted (No Items)";
              }
            }
          } catch (e) {
            rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Error: " + e.message;
            Logger.log(`Error parsing file ${fileName}: ${e.message}`);
          }
        }
      } else {
        rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Skipped (Not Data)";
      }
    }
  });


  // --- Appointment Data Logic (No Changes Here) ---
  dataRows.forEach((row, index) => {
    const category = row[categoryIndex];
    const currentStatus = row[statusIndex];
    const rowIndexInSheet = index + 2; 

    if ((currentStatus || "").trim() === "" && (category || "").trim().toLowerCase() === "appointment pass") {
      const appointmentId = row[appointmentIdIndex] || "Not Found";
      const appointmentDate = row[appointmentDateIndex] || "Not Found";
      const appointmentTime = row[appointmentTimeIndex] || "Not Found";
      const poNumber = String(row[poNumIndex]).trim();
      const fileUrl = row[fileUrlIndex];

      const dbRowIndexes = findRowIndexesByPoNumber(dbSheet, poNumber); // Assumes helper exists
      if (dbRowIndexes.length > 0) {
        const dbHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, dbSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
        const appointmentIdColumnIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("Appointment ID");

        const appointmentValues = [appointmentId, appointmentDate, appointmentTime, fileUrl];

        dbRowIndexes.forEach(dbRowIndex => {
          dbSheet.getRange(dbRowIndex, appointmentIdColumnIndex + 1, 1, 4).setValues([appointmentValues]);
          rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Extracted"; 
        });
      } else {
        // If PO not found, mark it so we know it failed
         rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Skipped (PO Not Found in DB)"; 
      }
    }
  });



  // --- Perform Batch Updates ---
  if (databaseRows.length > 0) {
    dbSheet.getRange(dbSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, databaseRows.length, databaseRows[0].length).setValues(databaseRows);
  }
  
  for (const rowIndex in rowsToUpdate) {
    const row = parseInt(rowIndex, 10); 
    if (statusIndex === -1) return;
    if (row > 0 && statusIndex + 1 > 0) {
      repoSheet.getRange(row, statusIndex + 1).setValue(rowsToUpdate[rowIndex]);
    }
  }

  // Handle skips
  rowsToSkip.forEach(r => repoSheet.getRange(r, statusIndex + 1).setValue("Skipped (Not Data)"));

  syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();
}

function extractDatabaseDetailsold2() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
  const channelThresholds = loadChannelThresholds(ss);

  const repoLastRow = repoSheet.getLastRow();
  if (repoLastRow < 2) return;

  const repoData = repoSheet.getRange(1,1,repoLastRow,repoSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
  const repoHeaders = repoData.shift();

  const col = name => repoHeaders.indexOf(name);

  const IDX = {
    CHANNEL: col("Channel Name"),
    FILE_NAME: col("File Name"),
    FILE_URL: col("Drive Link"),
    CATEGORY: col("Category"),
    PO_NUMBER: col("PO Number"),
    STATUS: col("Status"),
    STORE_CODE: col("Store Code"),
    APPOINTMENT_ID: col("Appointment ID"),
    APPOINTMENT_DATE: col("Appointment Date"),
    APPOINTMENT_TIME: col("Appointment Time")
  };

  const dataRows = repoData;

  // ------------------------------------------------
  // BUILD EXISTING PO SET (prevents duplicates)
  // ------------------------------------------------

  const dbHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1,1,1,dbSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const dbPoIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("PO Number");

  const existingPoSet = new Set();

  if (dbSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const poValues = dbSheet
      .getRange(2, dbPoIndex + 1, dbSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1)
      .getValues()
      .flat();

    poValues.forEach(p => {
      if (p) existingPoSet.add(String(p).trim());
    });
  }

  // ------------------------------------------------
  // BUILD PDF MAP
  // ------------------------------------------------

  const pdfMap = {};

  dataRows.forEach(row => {

    const channel = String(row[IDX.CHANNEL]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const fileName = String(row[IDX.FILE_NAME]).toLowerCase();
    const category = String(row[IDX.CATEGORY]);
    const po = String(row[IDX.PO_NUMBER]).trim();
    const url = row[IDX.FILE_URL];
    const status = String(row[IDX.STATUS]);

    if (!po || !url) return;

    switch(channel){

      case 'bb':
      case 'flipkartminutes':
        if(category === "New PO" && status === "" && fileName.match(/\.(xls|xlsx)$/)){
          pdfMap[po] = url;
        }
        break;

      default:
        if(category === "New PO" && fileName.endsWith(".pdf")){
          pdfMap[po] = url;
        }

    }

  });

  // ------------------------------------------------
  // PROCESS FILES
  // ------------------------------------------------

  let databaseRows = [];
  let statusUpdates = {};

  dataRows.forEach((row,i)=>{

    const sheetRow = i + 2;

    const status = String(row[IDX.STATUS]).trim();
    const category = String(row[IDX.CATEGORY]).trim();
    const fileUrl = row[IDX.FILE_URL];
    const fileName = String(row[IDX.FILE_NAME]).toLowerCase();
    const channel = String(row[IDX.CHANNEL]).trim();
    const poNumber = String(row[IDX.PO_NUMBER]).trim();

    if(status !== "" || (!fileUrl)) return;

    // -----------------------------------------
    // DUPLICATE PO PROTECTION
    // -----------------------------------------

    if(existingPoSet.has(poNumber)){
      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Skipped (PO Already Exists)";
      return;
    }

    if(!fileName.match(/\.(xls|xlsx|csv|pdf)$/)){
      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Skipped (Not Data)";
      return;
    }

    try{

      const fileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(fileUrl);
      if(!fileId) return;

      let rawData = null;

      if(fileName.endsWith(".pdf")){

        if(channel.toLowerCase().includes('starmark')){
          rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(fileId);
        }

      }
      else if(fileName.endsWith(".csv")){
        rawData = getCsvData(fileId);
      }
      else{
        rawData = getExcelDataViaBlob(fileId);
      }

      if(!rawData) return;

      const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
        rawData,
        channel,
        poNumber,
        row[IDX.STORE_CODE],
        skuMapping,
        pdfMap,
        channelThresholds,
        row[0]
      );

      if(extracted && extracted.length){

        databaseRows.push(...extracted);

        existingPoSet.add(poNumber); // Prevent duplicates within same run

        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Extracted";

      }else{

        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Extracted (No Items)";

      }

    }
    catch(e){

      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Error: " + e.message;
      Logger.log(e);

    }

  });

  // ------------------------------------------------
  // BATCH WRITE NEW DATABASE ROWS
  // ------------------------------------------------

  if(databaseRows.length){

    const startRow = dbSheet.getLastRow() + 1;

    dbSheet
      .getRange(startRow,1,databaseRows.length,databaseRows[0].length)
      .setValues(databaseRows);

  }

  // ------------------------------------------------
  // BATCH STATUS UPDATE
  // ------------------------------------------------

  Object.keys(statusUpdates).forEach(r=>{
    repoSheet.getRange(Number(r), IDX.STATUS + 1).setValue(statusUpdates[r]);
  });

  // ------------------------------------------------
  // APPOINTMENT UPDATE (unchanged logic)
  // ------------------------------------------------

  dataRows.forEach((row,i)=>{

    const sheetRow = i + 2;

    const category = String(row[IDX.CATEGORY]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const status = String(row[IDX.STATUS]).trim();

    if(status !== "" || category !== "appointment pass") return;

    const po = String(row[IDX.PO_NUMBER]).trim();
    const fileUrl = row[IDX.FILE_URL];

    const appointmentValues = [
      row[IDX.APPOINTMENT_ID] || "Not Found",
      row[IDX.APPOINTMENT_DATE] || "Not Found",
      row[IDX.APPOINTMENT_TIME] || "Not Found",
      fileUrl
    ];

    const dbRowIndexes = findRowIndexesByPoNumber(dbSheet,po);

    if(dbRowIndexes.length){

      const dbHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1,1,1,dbSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
      const colIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("Appointment ID");

      dbRowIndexes.forEach(r=>{
        dbSheet.getRange(r,colIndex+1,1,4).setValues([appointmentValues]);
      });

      repoSheet.getRange(sheetRow,IDX.STATUS+1).setValue("Extracted");

    }

  });

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation();
  updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();

}

function extractDatabaseDetails() 
{

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
  const channelThresholds = loadChannelThresholds(ss);

  const repoLastRow = repoSheet.getLastRow();
  if (repoLastRow < 2) return;

  const repoData = repoSheet.getRange(1,1,repoLastRow,repoSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
  const repoHeaders = repoData.shift();

  const col = name => repoHeaders.indexOf(name);

  const IDX = {
    CHANNEL: col("Channel Name"),
    FILE_NAME: col("File Name"),
    FILE_URL: col("Drive Link"),
    CATEGORY: col("Category"),
    PO_NUMBER: col("PO Number"),
    STATUS: col("Status"),
    STORE_CODE: col("Store Code"),
    APPOINTMENT_DATE: col("Appointment Date")
  };

  // ---------------------------------------------
  // EXISTING PO SET (for new PO duplicate prevention)
  // ---------------------------------------------

  const dbHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1,1,1,dbSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const dbPoIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("PO Number");

  const existingPoSet = new Set();

  if (dbSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    const poValues = dbSheet
      .getRange(2, dbPoIndex + 1, dbSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1)
      .getValues()
      .flat();

    poValues.forEach(p => {
      if (p) existingPoSet.add(String(p).trim());
    });
  }

  let databaseRows = [];
  let statusUpdates = {};

  // =============================================
  // MAIN LOOP
  // =============================================

  repoData.forEach((row, i) => {

    const sheetRow = i + 2;

    const status = String(row[IDX.STATUS]).trim();
    const category = String(row[IDX.CATEGORY]).trim();
    const fileUrl = row[IDX.FILE_URL];
    const fileName = String(row[IDX.FILE_NAME]).toLowerCase();
    const channel = String(row[IDX.CHANNEL]).trim();
    const poNumber = String(row[IDX.PO_NUMBER]).trim();

    if (status !== "" || !fileUrl) return;

    // ======================================================
    // 🔥 REVISION LOGIC
    // ======================================================

    if (category === "Revision") {

      try {

        let expiryDate = "";

        const fileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(fileUrl);
        if (!fileId) return;

        let rawData = null;

        if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
          rawData = getCsvData(fileId);
        }
        else if (fileName.endsWith(".xls") || fileName.endsWith(".xlsx")) {
          rawData = getExcelDataViaBlob(fileId);
        }
        else if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {
          if (channel.toLowerCase().includes("starmark")) {
            rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(fileId);
          }
        }

        if (rawData) {

          const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
            rawData,
            channel,
            poNumber,
            row[IDX.STORE_CODE],
            skuMapping,
            {},
            channelThresholds,
            row[0]
          );

          if (extracted && extracted.length > 0) {
            expiryDate = extracted[0][6]; // Expiry
          }
        }

        const appointmentDate = row[IDX.APPOINTMENT_DATE];

        const changes = updateExistingPO(poNumber, {
          appointmentDate,
          expiryDate
        });

        if (changes.length > 0) {

          statusUpdates[sheetRow] = `Revision Updated → ${changes.join(" | ")}`;

        } else {

          statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Revision Checked (No Change)";
        }

      } catch (e) {

        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Revision Error: " + e.message;
        Logger.log(e);
      }

      return; // 🚀 skip new PO logic
    }

    // ======================================================
    // 🟢 NEW PO LOGIC (UNCHANGED)
    // ======================================================

    if (category !== "New PO") return;

    // Duplicate protection
    if (existingPoSet.has(poNumber)) {
      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Skipped (PO Already Exists)";
      return;
    }

    if (!fileName.match(/\.(xls|xlsx|csv|pdf)$/)) {
      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Skipped (Not Data)";
      return;
    }

    try {

      const fileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(fileUrl);
      if (!fileId) return;

      let rawData = null;

      if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {
        if (channel.toLowerCase().includes('starmark')) {
          rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(fileId);
        }
      }
      else if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
        rawData = getCsvData(fileId);
      }
      else {
        rawData = getExcelDataViaBlob(fileId);
      }

      if (!rawData) return;

      const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
        rawData,
        channel,
        poNumber,
        row[IDX.STORE_CODE],
        skuMapping,
        {},
        channelThresholds,
        row[0]
      );

      if (extracted && extracted.length) {

        databaseRows.push(...extracted);
        existingPoSet.add(poNumber);

        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Extracted";

      } else {

        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Extracted (No Items)";
      }

    } catch (e) {

      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Error: " + e.message;
      Logger.log(e);
    }

  });

  // =============================================
  // WRITE NEW DATA
  // =============================================

  if (databaseRows.length) {

    dbSheet
      .getRange(dbSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, databaseRows.length, databaseRows[0].length)
      .setValues(databaseRows);
  }

  // =============================================
  // UPDATE STATUS
  // =============================================

  Object.keys(statusUpdates).forEach(r => {
    repoSheet.getRange(Number(r), IDX.STATUS + 1)
      .setValue(statusUpdates[r]);
  });

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation();
  updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();
}

/**
 * **CORRECTED HELPER:** Extracts text from a PDF file using Google Drive OCR.
 * It correctly identifies the input as a PDF and asks Drive to convert it.
 * Requires the Drive API Advanced Service to be enabled.
 */
function _extractTextFromPdf(fileId) {
  try {
    const file = DriveApp.getFileById(fileId);
    const blob = file.getBlob();
    
    // =========================================================================
    // THE FIX IS HERE: Do NOT set the target MIME type in the resource object.
    // Let Drive infer the input type (PDF) and convert it based on the flags.
    // =========================================================================
    const resource = {
      title: "Temp_OCR_" + new Date().getTime()
      // Do NOT include mimeType: MimeType.GOOGLE_DOCS here.
    };
    
    // Insert the PDF.
    // ocr: true tells Drive to extract text from images/PDFs.
    // convert: true is usually required alongside ocr to force the creation of a Google Doc.
    const docFile = Drive.Files.insert(resource, blob, { ocr: true, ocrLanguage: 'en', convert: true });
    
    // Open the newly created Google Doc and extract the text.
    const doc = DocumentApp.openById(docFile.id);
    const text = doc.getBody().getText();
    
    // Clean up: delete the temporary Google Doc.
    Drive.Files.remove(docFile.id);
    
    return text;
    
  } catch (e) {
    throw new Error(`Failed to extract text from PDF via OCR: ${e.message}`);
  }
}

// Function to find all PO row indexes in the PO database sheet (for multiple rows with the same PO Number)
function findRowIndexesByPoNumber(dbSheet, poNumber) {
  //Logger.log(`Searching for PO Number: ${poNumber}`);

  const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const rowIndexes = []; // To store all row indexes where PO number matches

  for (let i = 0; i < dbData.length; i++) {
    // Assuming PO Number is in column D (index 3, since columns are 0-based)
    const dbPoNumber = String(dbData[i][3]).trim(); // Convert to string for comparison
    if (dbPoNumber === String(poNumber).trim()) {
      //Logger.log(`Found PO Number: ${dbPoNumber} at row ${i + 1}`);
      rowIndexes.push(i + 1); // Push the 1-based row index into the array
    }
  }

  if (rowIndexes.length === 0) {
    Logger.log(`PO Number not found: ${poNumber}`);
  }

  return rowIndexes; // Return an array of row indexes (1-based)
}

// Channel Parsers
function getExtractedDataByChannel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds, poDate) {
  const key = channelName.toLowerCase();
  if (key.includes("instamart")) return parseInstamartExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds);
  if (key.includes("zepto")) return parseZeptoExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds);
  if (key.includes("blinkit")) return parseBlinkitExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds, poDate);
  if (key.includes("bb"))  return parseBigbasketExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping,pdfMap,thresholds);
  if(key.includes("flipkartminutes")) return parseFlipkartMinutesExcel(data, channelName, mapping,pdfMap,thresholds);
  if(key.includes("amazon")) return parseAmazonExcel(data,channelName,mapping);
  if(key.includes("starmark")) return parseStarmarkPdf(data, channelName, poNum, mapping, pdfMap);
  return [];
}

function parseStarmarkPdf(data, channel, poNum, skuMapping, pdfMap) {
  const rows = [];


  // -------------------------
  // HEADER EXTRACTION
  // -------------------------
  let poDate = "";
  let poExpiry = "";
  let extractedPoNum = poNum || "";

  
  // PO Number
  const poMatch =
  data.match(/PURCHASE\s+ORDER\s+([A-Z0-9\-\/]+)/i) ||
  data.match(/PO\s*NO\.?\s*[:\-]?\s*([A-Z0-9\-\/]+)/i) ||
  data.match(/\bMI-\d{2}-POR-\d+\b/i);

  if (poMatch) {
  extractedPoNum = poMatch[1] || poMatch[0];
  } 

  const dateMatch = data.match(/Date\s+(\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})/i);
  if (dateMatch) poDate = _formatStarmarkDate(dateMatch[1]);

  const expiryMatch = data.match(/Valid Till\s+(\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})/i);
  if (expiryMatch) poExpiry = _formatStarmarkDate(expiryMatch[1]);

  const poEDD = poDate;

  // Normalize text
  const text = data.replace(/\n+/g, " ").replace(/\s+/g, " ");

  const rsRegex = /RS\./g;
  const rsMatches = [...text.matchAll(rsRegex)];

  for (let i = 0; i < rsMatches.length; i++) {
    const rsIndex = rsMatches[i].index;
    const prevRsIndex = i === 0 ? 0 : rsMatches[i - 1].index + 3;
    const nextRsIndex = i < rsMatches.length - 1
      ? rsMatches[i + 1].index
      : text.length;

    const leftWindow = text.substring(prevRsIndex, rsIndex).trim();
    const rightWindow = text.substring(rsIndex + 3, nextRsIndex).trim();

    const qtyMatch = leftWindow.match(/(\d+)\s*$/);
    const qty = qtyMatch ? Number(qtyMatch[1]) : 0;
    if (!qty) continue;

    const priceMatch = rightWindow.match(/^([\d.]+)/);
    const cost = priceMatch ? Number(priceMatch[1]) : 0;
    if (!cost) continue;

    const skuMatches = leftWindow.match(/\b(TB\d{5}|\d{7})\b/g);
    const itemCode = skuMatches ? skuMatches[skuMatches.length - 1] : "";
    if (!itemCode) continue;

    const safeChannel = String(channel).toLowerCase();
    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, safeChannel, itemCode) || "Not Found";
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, safeChannel, itemCode) || "";

    const cleanName = leftWindow
      .replace(/\b(TB\d{5}|\d{7})\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\d+\s*$/, "")
      .replace(/CODE/ig, "")
      .replace(/\b\d{13}\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\b\d+\.\d+\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\b\d+\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\s{2,}/g, " ")
      .trim();

    rows.push([
      "New",
      poDate,
      channel,
      extractedPoNum,
      "Kolkata Warehouse",
      poEDD,
      poExpiry,
      itemCode,
      masterSKU,
      cleanName,
      qty,
      0,
      cost,
      pdfMap ? pdfMap[poNum] || "" : "",
      zohoItemId
    ]);
  }

  return rows;
}

function extractStarmarkSKU(text) {
  if (!text) return "";

  // TBxxxxx
  let m = text.match(/\bTB\d{5}\b/i);
  if (m) return m[0];

  // Exactly 7-digit numeric SKU
  m = text.match(/\b\d{7}\b/);
  if (m) return m[0];

  return "";
}

/**
 * **NEW HELPER:** Specifically parses the 'DD-MM-YYYY' format from Starmark POs.
 */
function _formatStarmarkDate(dateStr) {
  if (!dateStr || typeof dateStr !== 'string') return "";
  const parts = dateStr.split('-');
  if (parts.length !== 3) return dateStr;
  
  const day = parts[0];
  const month = parts[1];
  const year = parts[2].length === 2 ? "20" + parts[2] : parts[2];

  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
}

function parseInstamartExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds) {
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;

  // ... [Header & Table Start Logic Remains the Same] ...
  // (Copy lines A and B from your previous code regarding finding headers)
  let poDate = "", poEDD = "", poExpiry = "";
  for (let r = 0; r < Math.min(data.length, 20); r++) { 
    const row = data[r]; const rowStr = row.join(" ").toLowerCase();
    if (rowStr.includes("po date")) { const val = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "PO Date"); if (val) poDate = val; }
    if (rowStr.includes("expected delivery")) { const val = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "Expected Delivery"); if (val) poEDD = val; }
    if (rowStr.includes("expiry")) { const val = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "Expiry"); if (val) poExpiry = val; }
  }
  let headerRowIndex = -1;
  for (let r = 0; r < 30; r++) { 
    const rowStr = data[r].join(" ").toLowerCase();
    if (rowStr.includes("item code") && rowStr.includes("qty")) { headerRowIndex = r; break; }
  }
  if (headerRowIndex === -1) return []; 
  // ... [End of Header Logic] ...

  // C. Iterate Items
  for (let r = headerRowIndex + 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const itemCode = row[1];
    
    if (!itemCode || itemCode.toString().trim() === "") continue;

    const rawName = row[2];
    const cleanName = cleanInstamartItemName(rawName); 
    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "instamart", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "instamart", itemCode);

    
    const qty = parseFloat(row[5]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(row[6]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[7]) || 0;

    // Accumulate Total Value
    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

    // Push to Temp
    tempItems.push({
      poDate, channel, poNum, storeCode, poEDD, poExpiry,
      itemCode, masterSKU, cleanName, qty, mrp, cost,
      pdfLink: pdfMap[poNum],zohoItemId
    });
  }

  // D. DETERMINE STATUS BASED ON THRESHOLD
  const channelKey = channel.toLowerCase();
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
  
  // Logic: If Total Value < Threshold, Flag it. Otherwise "New"
  // Note: If threshold is 0, everything is "New"
  const status = (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue*1.05 < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  // E. Map to Final Array
  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status, // Col A: Status
    formatDate(i.poDate), 
    i.channel, 
    i.poNum, 
    i.storeCode,
    formatDate(i.poEDD), 
    formatDate(i.poExpiry),
    i.itemCode, 
    i.masterSKU, 
    i.cleanName, 
    i.qty, 
    i.mrp.toFixed(2), 
    i.cost.toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink,
    i.zohoItemId
  ]);
}

/**
 * **NEW & ROBUST:** Cleans a raw, multi-line item name from an Instamart PO.
 * It finds the start of the metadata (e.g., "1.0 Piece", "Colour:") and removes
 * everything after it, then cleans up all newline characters and extra spaces.
 *
 * @param {string} rawName - The original, potentially multi-line item name.
 * @return {string} The cleaned, single-line product name.
 */
function cleanInstamartItemName(rawName) {
  // Safety check for empty or invalid input.
  if (!rawName || typeof rawName !== 'string') {
    return "";
  }

  // --- Step 1: Define the patterns that signal the end of the product name ---
  // This regex looks for the FIRST occurrence of:
  // - A number (like 1 or 1.0) followed by "piece" or "pcs"
  // - OR the word "Colour:"
  // - OR the word "Size:"
  // - OR the word "Brand:"
  // The 'i' flag makes it case-insensitive.
  const stopPattern = /(\d+(\.\d+)?\s*pieces?\b|colour:|size:|brand:)/i;

  // --- Step 2: Find the index where the metadata begins ---
  const match = stopPattern.exec(rawName);
  let cleanName = rawName;

  // If a match is found, cut the string off just before the match.
  if (match) {
    cleanName = rawName.substring(0, match.index);
  }
  
  // --- Step 3: Clean up newlines and extra spaces ---
  
  // Replace all newline characters (\n) with a single space.
  cleanName = cleanName.replace(/\n/g, '');
  
  // Replace two or more consecutive spaces with a single space.
  cleanName = cleanName.replace(/\s{2,}/g, ' ');
  
  // Trim any leading or trailing whitespace.
  cleanName = cleanName.trim();
  
  return cleanName;
}

function parseZeptoExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds) {
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;
  
  if (data.length < 2) return [];

  const headers = data[0].map(h => h.toString().trim());
  const getIdx = (name) => headers.indexOf(name);

  // Column Mappings
  const idxPoDate   = getIdx("PoDate");
  const idxStore    = getIdx("StoreName");
  const idxExpiry   = getIdx("PoExpiryDate");
  const idxItemCode = getIdx("Sku"); 
  const idxItemName = getIdx("SkuDesc");      
  const idxQty      = getIdx("Quantity");
  const idxMRP      = getIdx("MRP");
  const idxCost     = getIdx("UnitBaseCost");

  if (idxItemCode === -1 || idxQty === -1) return [];

  const timeZone = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const itemCode = row[idxItemCode];

    if (!itemCode || itemCode.toString().trim() === "") continue;

    const cleanName = row[idxItemName]; 
    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "zepto", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "zepto", itemCode);

    Logger.log(zohoItemId);

    // Dates
    const rawPoDate = row[idxPoDate];     
    const rawExpiry = row[idxExpiry];
    let finalPoDate = "", finalExpiry = "", finalEDD = "";

    if (rawPoDate) {
      const dateObj = new Date(rawPoDate);
      if (!isNaN(dateObj.getTime())) {
        finalPoDate = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
        const eddDate = new Date(dateObj); 
        eddDate.setDate(eddDate.getDate() + 10);
        finalEDD = Utilities.formatDate(eddDate, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
      } else { finalPoDate = rawPoDate; }
    }

    if (rawExpiry) {
      const dateObj = new Date(rawExpiry);
      if (!isNaN(dateObj.getTime())) {
        finalExpiry = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
      } else { finalExpiry = rawExpiry; }
    }

    const qty = parseFloat(row[idxQty]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(row[idxMRP]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[idxCost]) || 0;

    const finalStore = storeCode || row[idxStore];

    // Accumulate Value
    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

    tempItems.push({
      finalPoDate, channel, poNum, finalStore, finalEDD, finalExpiry,
      itemCode, masterSKU, cleanName, qty, mrp, cost,
      pdfLink: pdfMap[poNum],zohoItemId
    });
  }

  // CHECK THRESHOLD
  const channelKey = channel.toLowerCase();
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
  const status = (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue*1.05 < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status, // Col A: Status
    i.finalPoDate, 
    i.channel, 
    i.poNum, 
    i.finalStore,
    i.finalEDD,    
    i.finalExpiry, 
    i.itemCode, 
    i.masterSKU, 
    i.cleanName, 
    i.qty, 
    i.mrp.toFixed(2), 
    i.cost.toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink,
    i.zohoItemId
  ]);
}

function parseBlinkitExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds, repoPoDate) {
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;
  
  if (!data || data.length < 2) return [];

  // 1. Headers
  const headers = data[0].map(h => h.toString().trim());
  const getIdx = (name) => headers.indexOf(name);

  const idxItemCode = getIdx("Item Code");
  const idxItemName = getIdx("Product Description");
  const idxQty      = getIdx("Quantity");
  const idxMRP      = getIdx("MRP");
  const idxCost     = getIdx("Basic Cost Price"); 

  if (idxItemCode === -1 || idxQty === -1) {
    console.log(`Blinkit Headers not found in ${poNum}. Headers seen: ${headers.join(",")}`);
    return [];
  }

  // 2. CALCULATE DATES
  const timeZone = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
  let poDateFormatted = "";
  let poEddFormatted = "";
  let poExpiryFormatted = "";

  if (repoPoDate) {
    const d = new Date(repoPoDate);
    if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) {
      // PO Date
      poDateFormatted = Utilities.formatDate(d, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
      
      // Expiry = PO Date + 15 Days
      const expD = new Date(d);
      expD.setDate(d.getDate() + 15);
      poExpiryFormatted = Utilities.formatDate(expD, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");

      // EDD = PO Date + 13 Days
      const eddD = new Date(d);
      eddD.setDate(d.getDate() + 13);
      poEddFormatted = Utilities.formatDate(eddD, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
    }
  }

  // 3. ITERATE ROWS
  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const itemCode = row[idxItemCode];

    // STOP Condition
    const firstCell = row[0] ? row[0].toString() : "";
    if (firstCell.toLowerCase().includes("total")) break;

    if (!itemCode || String(itemCode).trim() === "") continue;

    // --- MAPPING ---
    const rawName = row[idxItemName];
    // Clean name: Blinkit names often have (Box)[SkuID] at the end.
    let cleanName = rawName ? rawName.toString() : "";
    if (cleanName.includes("[")) {
      cleanName = cleanName.split("[")[0].trim();
    }

    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "blinkit", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "blinkit", itemCode);

    
    
    // --- NUMBERS ---
    const qty = parseFloat(row[idxQty]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(row[idxMRP]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[idxCost]) || 0;

    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

    tempItems.push({
      poDate: poDateFormatted,
      channel: channel,
      poNum: poNum,
      store: storeCode,
      poEDD: poEddFormatted,
      poExpiry: poExpiryFormatted,
      itemCode: itemCode,
      masterSKU: masterSKU,
      name: cleanName,
      qty: qty,
      mrp: mrp,
      cost: cost,
      pdfLink: pdfMap[poNum],
      zohoItemId : zohoItemId
    });
  }

  // 4. CHECK THRESHOLD
  const channelKey = channel.toLowerCase();
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
  const status = (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue*1.05 < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  // 5. FORMAT OUTPUT
  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status,
    i.poDate,
    i.channel,
    i.poNum,
    i.store,
    i.poEDD,
    i.poExpiry,
    i.itemCode,
    i.masterSKU,
    i.name,
    i.qty,
    i.mrp.toFixed(2),
    i.cost.toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink,
    i.zohoItemId
  ]);
}

// =================================================================================
// BIGBASKET - EXCEL PARSER (ROBUST FOR SPARSE 2D ARRAY)
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **NEW & CORRECTED:** Parses the sparse 2D array data from a BigBasket PO Excel file.
 * This function is specifically designed to "scan" each row for keywords and find
 * the corresponding values in adjacent cells.
 *
 * @param {Array<Array>} data - The full Excel data as a 2D array from getExcelDataViaBlob.
 * @return {Array<Array>} A 2D array of the parsed and formatted line items.
 */
function parseBigbasketExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds) {
  
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;

  if (!data || data.length === 0) return [];

  // --- A. Scan for Header-Level Information ---
  let poDate = "", poExpiry = "";
  
  // First, convert the entire 2D array into a single block of text for easy searching.
  const fullText = data.map(row => row.join(',')).join('\n');

   // Use regex to find and capture the values directly from the text block.
  const poDateMatch = fullText.match(/PO Date:([^,\n]+)/i);
  if (poDateMatch && poDateMatch[1]) {
    poDate = _formatBigbasketDate(poDateMatch[1].trim());
  }

  const poExpiryMatch = fullText.match(/PO Expiry date:([^,\n]+)/i);
  if (poExpiryMatch && poExpiryMatch[1]) {
    poExpiry = _formatBigbasketDate(poExpiryMatch[1].trim());
  }
  Logger.log
  
  Logger.log(`Extracted PO Date: ${poDate}, PO Expiry: ${poExpiry}`);
  if (!poDate) {
    Logger.log("Warning: Could not find 'PO Date:' in the document.");
    // Fallback if needed, e.g., using today's date
    poDate = new Date();
  }

  // --- B. Find the Item Table Header Row ---
  let headerRowIndex = -1;
  for (let r = 0; r < data.length; r++) {
    // A more reliable way to find the header is by looking for specific, non-sparse headers.
    const row = data[r].map(h => String(h).trim());
    if (row.includes("S.No") && row.includes("SKU Code") && row.includes("Description") && row.includes("Quantity")) {
      headerRowIndex = r;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (headerRowIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error in parseBigbasketExcel: Could not find the item table header row. Aborting.");
    return []; 
  }

  // --- C. Create a Dynamic Map of Header Names to Column Indexes ---
  const headerMap = {};
  data[headerRowIndex].forEach((header, index) => {
    if (header) headerMap[String(header).trim()] = index;
  });
  
  const requiredHeaders = ['SKU Code', 'Quantity', 'Basic Cost', 'MRP', 'Description'];
  for (const h of requiredHeaders) {
    if (!(h in headerMap)) {
      Logger.log(`Error: Essential column '${h}' not found in header map.`);
      return [];
    }
  }

  // --- D. Iterate Through Item Rows and Extract Data ---
  for (let r = headerRowIndex + 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const firstCell = String(row[0]).trim();
    
    // Stop if we hit an empty row or the "Total" row.
    if (firstCell === "" || firstCell.toLowerCase().includes("total")) {
      break;
    }
    
    const itemCode = row[headerMap['SKU Code']];
    if (!itemCode) continue;

    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "bb", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "bb", itemCode);

    const qty = parseFloat(row[headerMap['Quantity']]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(row[headerMap['MRP']]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[headerMap['Basic Cost']]) || 0;

    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

           // First, find the original file ID from the map.
    const originalFileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(pdfMap[poNum] || "");
    Logger.log(originalFileId);
    
    // Now, get the PDF version URL using our new helper.
    const finalPdfUrl = _getOrCreatePdfVersion(originalFileId);
    Logger.log(finalPdfUrl);

    tempItems.push({
      itemCode: String(itemCode).replace(/E\d+/, ''), // Handle scientific notation like 4.035...E7
      masterSKU, 
      cleanName: String(row[headerMap['Description']]).trim(), 
      qty, mrp, cost, pdfLink: finalPdfUrl, zohoItemId
    });
  }


  //Logger.log(tempItems);

  // --- D. DETERMINE STATUS BASED ON THRESHOLD ---
  const channelKey = channel.toLowerCase();  
  // Get the threshold, defaulting to 0 if not found.
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
    
  const status = (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue*1.05 < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  //Logger.log(`Total PO Value: ${totalPoValue}, Threshold: ${threshold}, Status: ${status}`);

  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status,
    poDate, 
    channel, 
    poNum, 
    storeCode,
    poExpiry,
    poExpiry,
    i.itemCode, 
    i.masterSKU, 
    i.cleanName, 
    i.qty, 
    (i.mrp || 0).toFixed(2),
    (i.cost || 0).toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink || "", // Add a fallback for null pdfLink
    i.zohoItemId || ""      // 15 Zoho Item ID ✅
  ]);
}

/**
 * **NEW & ROBUST HELPER:** Specifically converts a 'DD/Mon/YYYY' date string
 * (e.g., '22/Dec/2025') into a standard 'YYYY-MM-DD' format.
 *
 * @param {string} dateStr - The date string from the BigBasket PO.
 * @return {string} The formatted 'YYYY-MM-DD' date string, or an empty string if invalid.
 */
function _formatBigbasketDate(dateStr) {
  Logger.log(dateStr);
  if (!dateStr || typeof dateStr !== 'string') return "";

  const parts = dateStr.split('/');
  if (parts.length !== 3) return dateStr; // Return original if format is wrong

  const day = parts[0];
  const monthStr = parts[1];
  const year = parts[2];
  
  const monthMap = {
    'Jan': '01', 'Feb': '02', 'Mar': '03', 'Apr': '04', 'May': '05', 'Jun': '06',
    'Jul': '07', 'Aug': '08', 'Sep': '09', 'Oct': '10', 'Nov': '11', 'Dec': '12'
  };
  
  const month = monthMap[monthStr];
  if (!month) return dateStr; // Return original if month is not found
  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
}

// You will need a robust formatDate function that can handle different formats.
function formatDate(dateString) {
    if (!dateString) return "";
    try {
        // Handles "DD/Mon/YYYY" like "22/Dec/2025" and standard formats
        const date = new Date(dateString);
        return Utilities.formatDate(date, SpreadsheetApp.getActive().getSpreadsheetTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    } catch (e) {
        return dateString; // Return original if parsing fails
    }
}
// You will also need this helper function if you don't have it already.
// It's used to robustly find values in sparse rows from the Excel conversion.
function findValueInRowAfterKey(row, key) {
  const keyIndex = row.findIndex(cell => String(cell).toLowerCase().includes(key.toLowerCase()));
  if (keyIndex !== -1) {
    // Look for the first non-empty value in the cells immediately after the key.
    for (let i = keyIndex + 1; i < row.length; i++) {
      if (row[i] && String(row[i]).trim() !== "") {
        return row[i];
      }
    }
  }
  return ""; // Return empty string if not found
}

// AMAZON - B2B SHIPMENT PLAN PARSER
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **Parses the 2D array data from an Amazon B2B Shipment Plan CSV.**
 * It extracts and transforms the data to match the 15-column format required
 * by the 'PO_Database' sheet, applying all specified business rules.
 *
 * @param {Array<Array>} data - The full CSV data as a 2D array.
 * @return {Array<Array>} A 2D array of the parsed and formatted line items.
 */
function parseAmazonExcel(data,channelName,mapping) {
  if (!data || data.length < 2) {
    Logger.log("Error in parseAmazonExcel: Input data is empty or missing headers. Aborting.");
    return [];
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Header Row and Create a Dynamic Column Map ---
  const headers = data.shift().map(h => String(h).trim()); // Get headers and remove from data
  const headerMap = {};
  headers.forEach((h, i) => { if (h) headerMap[h] = i; });

  const requiredHeaders = ['sku', 'seller-sku', 'item-name', 'qty', 'declared_cost', 'FC ID', 'Shipment ID'];
  for (const h of requiredHeaders) {
    if (!(h in headerMap)) {
      Logger.log(`Error in parseAmazonExcel: Essential column '${h}' not found. Aborting.`);
      return [];
    }
  }

  // --- 2. Prepare Calculated Date Fields (do this once) ---
  const today = new Date();
  const tenDaysFromNow = new Date();
  tenDaysFromNow.setDate(today.getDate() + 10);
  
  const timezone = SpreadsheetApp.getActive().getSpreadsheetTimeZone();
  const poDate = Utilities.formatDate(today, timezone, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const eddAndExpiryDate = Utilities.formatDate(tenDaysFromNow, timezone, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

  // --- 3. Iterate Through Item Rows and Transform Data ---
  const finalOutput = data.map(row => {

    // Extract data using the header map
    const itemCode = row[headerMap['seller-sku']];
    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(mapping, "amazon_fba", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(mapping, "amazon_fba", itemCode);


    const itemName = row[headerMap['item-name']];
    const quantity = parseFloat(row[headerMap['qty']]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[headerMap['declared_cost']]) || 0;
    const shipmentId = row[headerMap['Shipment ID']];
    const fcId = row[headerMap['FC ID']];

    // Apply your business rules to create the final row
    return [
      "New",                  // Status
      poDate,                 // PO Date (today)
      "Amazon_FBA",               // Channel Name
      shipmentId,             // PO Number (from Shipment ID)
      fcId,       // Store Code ("Amazon_" + FC ID)
      eddAndExpiryDate,       // PO EDD (today + 10 days)
      eddAndExpiryDate,       // PO Expiry Date (today + 10 days)
      itemCode,               // Item Code (from sku)
      masterSKU,              // Master SKU (from seller-sku)
      itemName,               // Item Name
      quantity,               // Qty
      "-",                     // MRP (blank as requested)
      cost,                   // Unit Cost (Tax Exclusive)
      "-",                     // PO PDF (blank as requested)
      zohoItemId                      // Zoho Item ID (leave blank to be filled later)
    ];
  }).filter(Boolean); // .filter(Boolean) removes any null rows that were skipped

  Logger.log(`Successfully parsed and transformed ${finalOutput.length} items from the Amazon shipment plan.`);
  return finalOutput;
}
