// ==========================================
function syncZohoInvoicesToDB() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  
  // --- [NEW] SAFETY CHECK: REMOVE FILTERS ---
  // This prevents the script from editing the wrong rows if a user has hidden data.
  const filter = dbSheet.getFilter();
  if (filter !== null) {
    console.log("Filter detected. Removing filter to ensure data safety.");
    filter.remove();
  }
  // ------------------------------------------

  // 1. Calculate Date (28 Days Ago)
  // Format: YYYY-MM-DD
  const today = new Date();
  const pastDate = new Date(today);
  pastDate.setDate(today.getDate() - 4); 
  const lastModifiedTime = Utilities.formatDate(pastDate, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd");

  console.log(`Fetching Zoho Invoices modified after: ${lastModifiedTime}`);

  // 2. Get Zoho Token
  const token = getZohoAccessToken();
  if (!token) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const orgId = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');

  // 3. Fetch Invoices from Zoho
  const invoiceMap = fetchZohoInvoices(token, orgId, lastModifiedTime);
  
  if (invoiceMap.size === 0) {
    console.log("No updated invoices found in Zoho.");
    return;
  }

  //Logger.log(invoiceMap);

  // 4. Update PO Database
  updateDatabaseWithInvoices(dbSheet, invoiceMap);
}


/**
 * **UPDATED & MORE POWERFUL:** Fetches all valid invoices from Zoho. It now includes
 * a conditional, secondary API call to fetch the 'E-Way Bill Number' for any
 * invoice with a total value greater than 50,000.
 *
 * @param {string} token - The Zoho API authentication token.
 * @param {string} orgId - The Zoho organization ID.
 * @param {string} dateStr - The start date in 'YYYY-MM-DD' format.
 * @return {Map<string, object>} A Map where the key is the reference_number.
 */
function fetchZohoInvoices(token, orgId, dateStr) {
  const baseUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices?organization_id=${orgId}&date_after=${dateStr}&page=`;
  
  const options = {
    method: "GET",
    headers: { "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  let page = 1;
  let hasMore = true;
  const map = new Map();

  while (hasMore) {
    try {
      const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(baseUrl + page, options);
      const code = response.getResponseCode();
      
      if (code === 200) {
        const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
        const invoices = json.invoices;

        if (invoices && invoices.length > 0) {
          invoices.forEach(inv => {
            if (inv.status === "void") return; 

            const refNum = String(inv.reference_number || "").trim();
            
            if (refNum) {
              const pdfApiUrl = `https://books.zoho.in/api/v3/invoices/${inv.invoice_id}?organization_id=${orgId}&accept=pdf`;
              let ewayBillNumber = ""; // Default to blank

              // =========================================================================
              // THE NEW LOGIC IS HERE: Conditionally fetch the E-Way Bill
              // =========================================================================
              
              // Check if the invoice total is greater than 50,000.
              if (inv.total > 50000) {
                Logger.log(`Invoice ${inv.invoice_number} has total > 50k. Fetching E-Way Bill...`);
                
                // Make a second, targeted API call for this specific invoice's details.
                const detailsUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices/${inv.invoice_id}?organization_id=${orgId}`;
                const detailsResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(detailsUrl, options);
                
                if (detailsResponse.getResponseCode() === 200) {
                  const detailsJson = JSON.parse(detailsResponse.getContentText());
                  // Safely navigate the JSON to find the eway_bill_number.
                  if (detailsJson.invoice && detailsJson.invoice.eway_bill_details) {
                    ewayBillNumber = detailsJson.invoice.eway_bill_details.eway_bill_number || "";
                    Logger.log(`Found E-Way Bill: ${ewayBillNumber}`);
                  }
                }
                
                // Be a good API citizen and pause after the extra call.
                Utilities.sleep(1100); 
              }

              // Store all the data in the map.
              map.set(refNum, {
                id: inv.invoice_id,
                status: inv.status,
                number: inv.invoice_number,
                date: inv.date,
                total: inv.total,
                portalUrl: inv.invoice_url,
                pdfUrl: pdfApiUrl,
                ewayBill: ewayBillNumber // Add the new E-Way Bill number
              });
            }
          });
          
          hasMore = (json.page_context && json.page_context.has_more_page);
          if (hasMore) page++;

        } else {
          hasMore = false;
        }
      } else {
        console.error(`Zoho API Error: ${response.getContentText()}`);
        hasMore = false;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("Invoice Fetch Error: " + e.message);
      hasMore = false;
    }
  }

  const loggableObject = Object.fromEntries(map);
  //Logger.log(JSON.stringify(loggableObject, null, 2));

  console.log(`Fetched ${map.size} valid invoices from Zoho.`);
  return map;
}

/**
 * **UPDATED:** Matches Zoho invoices to the PO Database via the Reference Number
 * and performs an efficient batch update. This version now includes the logic to
 * write the newly fetched 'E-Way Bill Number'.
 *
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - The 'PO_Database' sheet object.
 * @param {Map<string, object>} map - The invoice map from fetchZohoInvoices.
 */
function updateDatabaseWithInvoices(sheet, map) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  // 1. Define Column Indexes (Dynamic lookup is more robust)
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const COL_EE_REF = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code') + 1;
  const START_COL = headers.indexOf('Invoice Id') + 1;
  
  if (COL_EE_REF === 0 || START_COL === 0) {
      console.error("Could not find 'EE Reference Code' or 'Invoice Id' headers. Aborting update.");
      return;
  }
  
  // 2. Read existing data to match
  const refValues = sheet.getRange(2, COL_EE_REF, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues();

  // =========================================================================
  // THE CHANGES ARE HERE
  // =========================================================================
  
  // 3. Define the new number of columns to read and write (now 8, including EWB).
  const NUM_COLUMNS_TO_UPDATE = 8; 
  
  const existingInvoiceDataRange = sheet.getRange(2, START_COL, lastRow - 1, NUM_COLUMNS_TO_UPDATE);
  const existingData = existingInvoiceDataRange.getValues();
  
  const finalWriteData = existingData.map((row, i) => {
    const eeRef = String(refValues[i][0]).trim();
    const newDetails = map.get(eeRef);
    
    if (newDetails) {
      // Found an update. Return the new data, now including the ewayBill.
      return [
        newDetails.id,
        newDetails.status,
        newDetails.number,
        newDetails.date,
        newDetails.total,
        newDetails.portalUrl,
        newDetails.pdfUrl,
        newDetails.ewayBill || "" // Add the ewayBill, with a fallback to empty string
      ];
    } else {
      // No update found, KEEP THE OLD DATA for all columns.
      return row; 
    }
  });

  // Write Back the updated 8-column range.
  sheet.getRange(2, START_COL, finalWriteData.length, NUM_COLUMNS_TO_UPDATE).setValues(finalWriteData);
  console.log("Updated PO Database with Zoho Invoice details (including E-Way Bills).");
}
function update_data()
{
  processPurchaseOrders();
  extractDatabaseDetails();
}

function update_data_manual()
{
  processPurchaseOrders_oneday();
  extractDatabaseDetails();
}

function processPurchaseOrders_oneday() {
  updateZohoItemIDs();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
  const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

  // --- NEW: Setup the Gmail Label ---
  const LABEL_NAME = 'ProcessedPO';
  let processedLabel = GmailApp.getUserLabelByName(LABEL_NAME);
  if (!processedLabel) {
    Logger.log(`Creating missing Gmail label: ${LABEL_NAME}`);
    processedLabel = GmailApp.createLabel(LABEL_NAME);
  }

  // 1. Get Config & Timer Logic
  const lastRow = configSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;
  const configData = configSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 4).getValues();
  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  let startTime = parseInt(scriptProperties.getProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME') || '0');
  const oneDayAgo = new Date();
  oneDayAgo.setDate(oneDayAgo.getDate() - 1);
  startTime = Math.floor(oneDayAgo.getTime() / 1000);
  
  const currentRunTime = Math.floor(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
  const newLogs = [];
  
  // --- NEW: Track processed IDs during this run to prevent instant duplicates ---
  const processedMessageIds = new Set();

  // 2. Process Channels
  configData.forEach(row => {
    const [channelName, status, rawEmails, subjectKeyword] = row;
    if (!channelName || !rawEmails || String(status).toLowerCase() !== 'active') return;

    const channelKey = channelName.toLowerCase();
    const emailList = rawEmails.split(',').map(e => e.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    if (emailList.length === 0) return;
     
    const fromClause = `from:(${emailList.join(' OR ')})`;
    
    // --- THE CHANGE IS HERE: Exclude emails that already have the label ---
    let query = `${fromClause} -from:me after:${startTime} -label:${LABEL_NAME}`;
    if (subjectKeyword) query += ` subject:("${subjectKeyword}")`;

    try {
      const threads = GmailApp.search(query);
      if (threads.length === 0) return;

      const allThreadMessages = GmailApp.getMessagesForThreads(threads);
      allThreadMessages.forEach(messages => {
        messages.forEach(message => {
          // --- THE SECOND CHANGE IS HERE: Check the in-memory Set ---
          const messageId = message.getId();
          if (processedMessageIds.has(messageId)) return; // Skip if already seen this run
          
          if (Math.floor(message.getDate().getTime() / 1000) <= startTime) return;
          const sender = message.getFrom().toLowerCase();
          if (!emailList.some(e => sender.includes(e.toLowerCase()))) return;

          const attachments = message.getAttachments();
          const subject = message.getSubject();
          const emailBody = message.getPlainBody();
          const metadata = analyzeEmailMetadata(channelKey, subject, subject.toUpperCase(), emailBody);
          
          let successfullyProcessed = false; // Flag to track if we should label it

          if (attachments.length > 0) {
            // --- CASE 1: Attachments EXIST ---
            attachments.forEach(att => {
              const fileName = att.getName();
              try {
                const blob = att.copyBlob();
                if (fileName.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls')) {
                  blob.setContentType(MimeType.MICROSOFT_EXCEL_LEGACY);
                }

                const file = folder.createFile(blob);
                file.setName(`[${channelName}] ${fileName}`);

                let finalPO = metadata.poNumber === "Not Found" ? extractPOFromText(channelKey, fileName.toUpperCase()) : metadata.poNumber;
                let finalCategory = metadata.category === "New PO" ? determineCategory(fileName.toUpperCase()) : metadata.category;

                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, fileName,
                  file.getUrl(), finalCategory, finalPO, metadata.storeCode, ""
                ]);
                
                successfullyProcessed = true; // Mark as success

              } catch (e) {
                Logger.log(`ERROR: Failed to save attachment "${fileName}". Error: ${e.message}`);
                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, fileName,
                  "SAVE FAILED", "Error", metadata.poNumber, metadata.storeCode, e.message
                ]);
              }
            });
          } else {
            // --- CASE 2: NO Attachments ---
            if (metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") {
              newLogs.push([
                message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, "No Attachment",
                "", metadata.category, metadata.poNumber, metadata.storeCode, ""
              ]);
              successfullyProcessed = true; // Mark as success
            }
          }
          
          // --- FINAL STEP: Apply Label and remember the ID ---
          if (successfullyProcessed) {
            try {
              // Apply the label to the specific message's thread
              message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            } catch(e) {
              Logger.log(`Warning: Failed to apply label to message ${messageId}.`);
            }
            // Add the ID to our set to prevent duplicate processing in the same run
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
          }
          
        });
      });
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(`Error processing ${channelName}: ${e.message}`);
    }
  });

  // 3. Batch Write Logs & Update Timer
  if (newLogs.length > 0) {
    newLogs.sort((a, b) => new Date(a[0]) - new Date(b[0]));
    logSheet.getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, newLogs.length, newLogs[0].length).setValues(newLogs);
    console.log(`Successfully processed ${newLogs.length} new log entries.`);
  }
  scriptProperties.setProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME', currentRunTime.toString());
}

/**
 * **MAIN FUNCTION:** Fetches a contact from Zoho Books by its ID, transforms the
 * data, and creates a corresponding B2B customer in EasyEcom.
 *
 * @param {string} contactId - The Zoho Books contact_id to sync.
 * @return {boolean} True on success, false on failure.
 */

function testtt()
{
  syncZohoContactToEasyEcom("1975394000200114770");
}
function syncZohoContactToEasyEcom(contactId) {
  if (!contactId) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: No Zoho Contact ID provided.');
    return false;
  }
  
  Logger.log(`--- Starting sync for Zoho Contact ID: ${contactId} ---`);

  try {
    // --- Step 1: Fetch Full Contact Details from Zoho Books ---
    const zohoContact = _fetchZohoContactDetails(contactId);
    debugLog(zohoContact,"")
    if (!zohoContact) {
      // The helper function will have already logged the specific error.
      return false; 
    }

    // --- Step 2: Create the Customer in EasyEcom using the Zoho data ---
    const success = _createEasyEcomCustomer(zohoContact);
    
    if (success) {
      fetchEasyEcomCustomers();
      Logger.log('--- Successfully synced Zoho contact to EasyEcom. ---');
      return true;
    } else {
      Logger.log('--- Failed to create customer in EasyEcom. ---');
      return false;
    }

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`An unexpected error occurred during the sync process: ${e.message}`);
    return false;
  }
}


/**
 * **HELPER 1:** Fetches the details for a single contact from the Zoho Books API.
 * @param {string} contactId - The Zoho Books contact_id.
 * @return {object|null} The Zoho contact object, or null on failure.
 */
function _fetchZohoContactDetails(contactId) {
  const authToken = getZohoAccessToken(); // You need to implement this helper function
  const organizationId = '60032126274'; // As provided in your example
  
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/contacts/${contactId}?organization_id=${organizationId}`;
  
  const options = {
    'method': 'get',
    'headers': {
      'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${authToken}` // Use the correct auth scheme (OAuth is recommended)
    },
    'muteHttpExceptions': true
  };
  
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    Logger.log(response);
    const responseData = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    
    if (response.getResponseCode() === 200 && responseData.contact) {
      Logger.log(`Successfully fetched contact "${responseData.contact.contact_name}" from Zoho.`);
      return responseData.contact;
    } else {
      throw new Error(`(Code: ${response.getResponseCode()}) ${response.getContentText()}`);
    }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR fetching from Zoho: ${e.message}`);
    return null;
  }
}


/**
 * **UPDATED:** Creates a B2B customer in EasyEcom using data from a Zoho contact.
 * This version now includes a mapping to convert Zoho's state names (e.g., "Maharashtra")
 * into the numerical State IDs required by the EasyEcom API.
 *
 * @param {object} zohoContact - The contact object returned from the Zoho API.
 * @return {boolean} True on success, false on failure.
 */
function _createEasyEcomCustomer(zohoContact) {
  const token = getEasyEcomToken(); // Assumes this function exists
  const apiKey = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');
  if (!token || !apiKey) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: Missing EasyEcom token or API key.');
    return false;
  }
  
  // =========================================================================
  // THE CHANGE IS HERE: State Name to State ID Mapping
  // =========================================================================
  const stateNameToIdMap = {
    "Andhra Pradesh": 1, "Arunachal Pradesh": 2, "Assam": 3, "Bihar": 4,
    "Chhattisgarh": 5, "Goa": 6, "Gujarat": 7, "Haryana": 8, "Himachal Pradesh": 9,
    "Jammu & Kashmir": 10, "Jharkhand": 11, "Karnataka": 12, "Kerala": 13,
    "Madhya Pradesh": 14, "Maharashtra": 15, "Manipur": 16, "Meghalaya": 17,
    "Mizoram": 18, "Nagaland": 19, "Odisha": 20, "Punjab": 21, "Rajasthan": 22,
    "Sikkim": 23, "Tamil Nadu": 24, "Telangana": 25, "Tripura": 26,
    "Uttar Pradesh": 27, "Uttarakhand": 28, "West Bengal": 29, "Delhi": 30,
    "Puducherry": 31, "Andaman & Nicobar Islands": 32, "Chandigarh": 33,
    "Dadra & Nagar Haveli": 34, "Daman & Diu": 35, "Lakshadweep": 37,
    "Dadra & Nagar Haveli and Daman & Diu": 3848, "Ladakh": 3851
  };
  const NOT_AVAILABLE_ID = 3849; // The fallback ID for any state not found in the map.

  const url = "https://api.easyecom.io/Wholesale/CreateCustomer";
  
  // --- Data Mapping Logic ---
  const shippingAddress = zohoContact.shipping_address || {};
  const billingAddress = zohoContact.billing_address || {};

  // Safely get state names from Zoho data.
  const dispatchStateName = shippingAddress.state || '';
  const dispatchStateId = stateNameToIdMap[dispatchStateName] || NOT_AVAILABLE_ID;

  // Combine address lines safely.
  const fullBillingStreet = `${billingAddress.address || ''} ${billingAddress.street2 || ''}`.trim();
  const fullDispatchStreet = `${shippingAddress.address || ''} ${shippingAddress.street2 || ''}`.trim();

  const payload = {
    "companyName": zohoContact.contact_name,
    "taxIdentificationNumber": zohoContact.gst_no || "URP",
    "password": "test@1234",
    "email": zohoContact.email || "avinav@cubelelo.com",
    "contactNumber": String(zohoContact.phone || shippingAddress.phone || "0000000000").replace(/\D/g, '').slice(-10),    "country": "India",
    //"dispatchContactName": zohoContact.contact_name,
    //"billingContactName": zohoContact.company_name,
    "billingStateId": dispatchStateId, // Use the mapped ID
    "billingStreet": fullBillingStreet,
    "billingCity": billingAddress.city,
    "billingPostalCode": billingAddress.zip,
    "currency": "INR",
    "description": `Synced from Zoho Contact ID: ${zohoContact.contact_id}`,
    "dispatchStateId": dispatchStateId, // Use the mapped ID
    "dispatchStreet": fullDispatchStreet,
    "dispatchCity": shippingAddress.city,
    "dispatchPostalCode": shippingAddress.zip
  };
  //Logger.log(payload);
  
  const options = {
    'method': 'post',
    'headers': {
      'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
      'x-api-key': apiKey,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    'payload': JSON.stringify(payload),
    'muteHttpExceptions': true
  };
  
// =========================================================================
  // THE CHANGE IS HERE: The try/catch block now returns objects instead of booleans.
  // =========================================================================
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
    const responseText = response.getContentText();
    let responseData;
    
    // Always try to parse the JSON, as even errors contain useful messages.
    try {
      responseData = JSON.parse(responseText);
    } catch (jsonError) {
      // If parsing fails, the response was not valid JSON (e.g., an HTML error page).
      throw new Error(`API returned a non-JSON response (HTTP ${responseCode}): ${responseText.substring(0, 500)}`);
    }

    // =========================================================================
    // THE FIX IS HERE: A robust, two-level check for success.
    // =========================================================================
    
    // A true success requires BOTH a 200 HTTP code AND a 200 internal code.
    if (responseCode === 200 && responseData.code === 200) {
      Logger.log(`Successfully created customer "${payload.companyName}" in EasyEcom. API Message: ${responseData.message}`);
      return true;
    } else {
      // If either check fails, we have an error. Prioritize the message from the JSON.
      const errorMessage = responseData.message || "An unknown API error occurred.";
      throw new Error(`(HTTP ${responseCode}, API Code ${responseData.code}) - ${errorMessage}`);
    }

  } catch (e) {
    // This will now catch all thrown errors and log them clearly.
    Logger.log(`ERROR creating customer in EasyEcom: ${e.message}`);
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * **FINAL & COMPLETE:** Called from a front-end with a single EE Reference Code. It:
 * 1. Finds all matching rows in the 'PO_Database' sheet.
 * 2. Creates a draft invoice in Zoho Books.
 * 3. Immediately makes a second API call to mark the new invoice as "Sent".
 * 4. Triggers the e-invoice generation (push to IRP) during the status update.
 * 5. Returns a structured JSON object to the front-end.
 *
 * @param {string} eeReferenceCode - The 'EE Reference Code' to search for in the database.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a detailed message/data.
 */


/**
 * **FINAL & CORRECTED:** Called from a front-end. It now uses the correct,
 * three-step API process to create a Zoho Invoice:
 * 1. Creates a draft invoice.
 * 2. Pushes the invoice to the IRP for e-invoicing using the dedicated endpoint.
 * 3. Marks the invoice as "Sent".
 *
 * @param {string} eeReferenceCode - The reference code to search for.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status and a detailed message.
 */
// =================================================================================
// ZOHO BOOKS - INVOICE CREATION & SYNC-BACK WORKFLOW
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **MAIN BACKEND FUNCTION:** Called from a front-end with a single EE Reference Code. It
 * orchestrates the entire 3-step invoice creation and e-invoicing process, and then
 * triggers a sync to write the results back to the PO_Database.
 *
 * @param {string} eeReferenceCode - The 'EE Reference Code' to search for in the database.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a detailed message/data.
 */

function test_invoice()
{
  createZohoInvoiceByReferenceCode("AZ250587");
}

function createZohoInvoiceByReferenceCode(eeReferenceCode) 
{
  if (!eeReferenceCode) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No EE Reference Code was provided." };
  }

  Logger.log(`--- Starting 3-Step Zoho Invoice & E-Invoice Process for: ${eeReferenceCode} ---`);
  
  try {
    const token = getZohoAccessToken(); // Assumes this helper function exists and works
    if (!token) {
      throw new Error("Could not get Zoho Access Token. Please check credentials and setup.");
    }
    const orgId = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');
    
    // --- Step 1: Read the PO_Database and find all matching rows ---
    const dbSheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
    if (dbSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      throw new Error("The 'PO_Database' sheet is empty or has no data.");
    }
    const allData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = allData.shift();

    const refCodeIndex = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code');
    const contactIdIndex = headers.indexOf('Zoho Contact ID');
    const itemIdIndex = headers.indexOf('Zoho Item ID');
    const costIndex = headers.indexOf('Unit Cost (Tax Exclusive)');
    const shippedQtyIndex = headers.indexOf('EE_item_shipped_quantity');

    if ([refCodeIndex, contactIdIndex, itemIdIndex, costIndex, shippedQtyIndex].includes(-1)) {
      throw new Error("One or more required columns could not be found in 'PO_Database'. Please check headers.");
    }

   const matchingRows = allData.filter(row => String(row[refCodeIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode);
if (matchingRows.length === 0) throw new Error(`No rows found for EE Reference Code: ${eeReferenceCode}`);

// ---------------------------------------------------------
// Check if invoice already exists in PO_Database
// ---------------------------------------------------------
const invoiceIdIndex = headers.indexOf('Invoice Id');
if (invoiceIdIndex === -1) {
  throw new Error("'Invoice Id' column not found in PO_Database.");
}

const existingInvoice = matchingRows.find(row => String(row[invoiceIdIndex]).trim() !== "");

if (existingInvoice) {
  const existingInvoiceId = existingInvoice[invoiceIdIndex];
  Logger.log(`Invoice already exists for ${eeReferenceCode}: ${existingInvoiceId}`);
  return {
    status: "skipped",
    message: `Invoice already exists for ${eeReferenceCode}. Existing Invoice ID: ${existingInvoiceId}`
  };
}


      // Get the channel name from the first matching row
    const channelName = matchingRows[0][headers.indexOf('Channel Name')];
    
    
    // =========================================================================
    // NEW LOGIC: Determine the Invoice & Bill Number based on the channel
    // =========================================================================
    let finalInvoiceNumber = "";
    let finalBillNumber = "";

    if (String(channelName).toLowerCase() === 'amazon_fba') {
      Logger.log("Amazon_FBA channel detected. Getting FBA Shipment ID from sheet...");
      
      const fbaShipmentID = String(matchingRows[0][headers.indexOf('FBA Shipment IDs')]).trim();

      // --- THE FIX IS HERE ---
      // This is the correct way to check if the string has a value.
      if (fbaShipmentID) {
        // If fbaShipmentID is not an empty string, this block will run.
        finalInvoiceNumber = fbaShipmentID;
        finalBillNumber = fbaShipmentID;
      } else {
        // If fbaShipmentID is an empty string, null, or undefined, throw an error.
        throw new Error(`The 'FBA Shipment ID' column is empty for EE Reference Code: ${eeReferenceCode}`);
      }
     Logger.log(`Using Invoice Number: ${finalInvoiceNumber} and Bill Number: ${finalBillNumber}`);


    } else {
      // For all other channels, use the original sequential number logic.
      //finalInvoiceNumber = _getNewZohoInvoiceNumber(token, orgId);
      //if (!finalInvoiceNumber) throw new Error("Could not generate a new sequential invoice number.");
      
      //finalBillNumber = eeReferenceCode.replace(/_/g, "-").substring(0, 15);
    }

    // --- The rest of the function now uses these final numbers ---
    

    
    // --- Step 3: Process the matching rows to create Zoho line items ---
    const lineItems = matchingRows.map(row => {
      const itemId = row[itemIdIndex];
      if (!itemId) throw new Error(`Missing Zoho Item ID for a row with PO Ref: ${eeReferenceCode}.`);
      const rate = parseFloat(row[costIndex]) || 0;
      const quantity = parseInt(row[shippedQtyIndex], 10) || 0;
      if (quantity <= 0) return null;
      return { "item_id": itemId, "rate": rate.toFixed(2), "quantity": quantity, "tax_id": "1975394000000027292" };
    }).filter(Boolean);

    Logger.log(lineItems);

if (lineItems.length === 0) throw new Error("No items with a shipped quantity > 0 were found.");

// ---------------------------------------------------------
// Add Shipping Charges as a Separate Line Item
// ---------------------------------------------------------

const shippingIndex = headers.indexOf('Shipping Charge');

if (shippingIndex !== -1) {

  const shippingCharge = parseFloat(matchingRows[0][shippingIndex]) || 0;

  if (shippingCharge > 0) {

    const shippingItemId = PropertiesService
      .getScriptProperties()
      .getProperty("ZOHO_SHIPPING_ITEM_ID");

    if (!shippingItemId) {
      throw new Error("ZOHO_SHIPPING_ITEM_ID not configured in Script Properties.");
    }

    Logger.log(`Adding Shipping Charges: ${shippingCharge}`);

    lineItems.push({
      item_id: shippingItemId,
      rate: shippingCharge.toFixed(2),
      quantity: 1,
      tax_id: "1975394000000027292"
    });

  }

} else {

  Logger.log("Shipping Charge column not found in PO_Database.");

}
    // --- Step 4: Create the DRAFT invoice ---
    const customerId = matchingRows[0][contactIdIndex];
    if (!customerId) throw new Error("Zoho Contact ID is missing for this PO.");

    const createPayload = {
  "customer_id": customerId,
  "reference_number": eeReferenceCode,
  "line_items": lineItems
};

// ONLY pass invoice_number for Amazon
if (String(channelName).toLowerCase() === 'amazon_fba') {
  createPayload.invoice_number = finalInvoiceNumber;
}

    let createUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices?organization_id=${orgId}`;

if (String(channelName).toLowerCase() === 'amazon_fba') {
  createUrl += `&ignore_auto_number_generation=true`;
}
  //Logger.log(createPayload);
    const createOptions = { 'method': 'post', 'headers': { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` }, 'contentType': 'application/json', 'payload': JSON.stringify(createPayload), 'muteHttpExceptions': true };
    const createResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(createUrl, createOptions);
    const createResponseData = JSON.parse(createResponse.getContentText());

    if (createResponse.getResponseCode() !== 201) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to create draft invoice. Zoho API Error: ${createResponse.getContentText()}`);
    }

    const newInvoiceId = createResponseData.invoice.invoice_id;
    const createdInvoiceNumber = createResponseData.invoice.invoice_number;
    Logger.log(`Step 1/3: Successfully created DRAFT invoice ${createdInvoiceNumber} (ID: ${newInvoiceId}).`);

    Logger.log(`Step 2/3: Pushing invoice ${newInvoiceId} to IRP...`);
    const pushUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices/${newInvoiceId}/einvoice/push?organization_id=${orgId}`;
    const pushOptions = { 'method': 'post', 'headers': { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` }, 'contentType': 'application/json', 'payload': JSON.stringify({}), 'muteHttpExceptions': true };
    
    const pushResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(pushUrl, pushOptions);
    const pushResponseText = pushResponse.getContentText();
    const pushResponseData = JSON.parse(pushResponseText);
    
  // The new, more robust check: The HTTP code must be in the 200s AND the internal code must be 0.
    const isSuccessStatusCode = pushResponse.getResponseCode() >= 200 && pushResponse.getResponseCode() < 300;
    
    if (isSuccessStatusCode && pushResponseData.code === 0) {
      Logger.log(`Step 2/3: Successfully pushed to IRP. Message: ${pushResponseData.message}`);
    } else {
      // If either check fails, throw an error, prioritizing the JSON message if it exists.
      const errorMessage = pushResponseData.message || pushResponseText;
      throw new Error(`Invoice was created, but failed to push to IRP. Zoho's Response: ${errorMessage}`);
    }

    // --- Step 4: Mark the Invoice as Sent (No changes here) ---
    Logger.log(`Step 3/3: Marking invoice ${newInvoiceId} as Sent...`);
    const updateStatusUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices/${newInvoiceId}/status/sent?organization_id=${orgId}`;
    const updateOptions = { 'method': 'post', 'headers': { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` }, 'contentType': 'application/json', 'payload': JSON.stringify({}), 'muteHttpExceptions': true };
    const updateResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(updateStatusUrl, updateOptions);
    if (updateResponse.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error(`Invoice was pushed to IRP, but failed to mark as Sent. Error: ${updateResponse.getContentText()}`);
    }
    Logger.log(`Step 3/3: Successfully marked invoice as Sent.`);

    
    // =========================================================================
    // NEW LOGIC: Create a corresponding Purchase Bill if the channel is Amazon
    // =========================================================================
    
    let billCreationMessage = ""; // A message to add to the final success response

    if (String(channelName).toLowerCase() === 'amazon_fba') {
      Logger.log("Channel is 'Amazon'. Proceeding to create a Purchase Bill.");
      
      const gstIndex = headers.indexOf('GST'); // Find the GST column
      if (gstIndex === -1) throw new Error("'GST' column not found in PO_Database.");
      
      const gstNumber = matchingRows[0][gstIndex];
      const branch_id = getBranchIdByGstFast_(gstNumber); // Your existing helper
      if (!branch_id) throw new Error(`Could not determine Branch ID for GSTIN: ${gstNumber}`);

      const bill_payload = {
        "vendor_id": '1975394000078488465', // Fixed for BSPL CG
        "reference_number": eeReferenceCode, // Use the same reference
        "branch_id": branch_id,
        "bill_number": finalBillNumber,
        "line_items": lineItems // Reuse the same line items from the invoice
      };

      const bill_params = {
        "method": "POST",
        "headers": { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` },
        "contentType": "application/json",
        "payload": JSON.stringify(bill_payload),
        "muteHttpExceptions": true
      };

      const billResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(`https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/bills?organization_id=${orgId}`, bill_params);
      const billResponseCode = billResponse.getResponseCode();
      
      if (billResponseCode === 201) {
        const billResponseData = JSON.parse(billResponse.getContentText());
        billCreationMessage = ` A corresponding Purchase Bill (${billResponseData.bill.bill_number}) was also created.`;
        Logger.log(`Successfully created Purchase Bill for Branch ID: ${branch_id}.`);
      } else {
        // We throw an error here because if the bill fails, it's a critical failure.
        throw new Error(`Invoice was finalized, but failed to create the Purchase Bill. Error: ${billResponse.getContentText()}`);
      }
    }

    
    // --- Final Success ---
    syncZohoInvoicesToDB(); // Trigger the sync-back process
    
    const successMessage = `Successfully created Zoho Invoice ${createdInvoiceNumber}, pushed to IRP, and marked as Sent.`;
    return { status: "success", message: successMessage, data: createResponseData.invoice };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR during Zoho Invoice Creation: ${e.message}`);
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}


/**
 * **OPTIMIZED & ROBUST:** Fetches the latest 10 invoices sorted by date to find
 * the highest invoice number. This is much faster than fetching all invoices and
 * more reliable than sorting by the invoice number string.
 *
 * @return {string|null} The new invoice number string, or null on failure.
 */
function _getNewZohoInvoiceNumber(token, orgId) {

  
  const invoicePrefix = 'BSPL/25-26/';
  
  // =========================================================================
  // THE FIX IS HERE: Fetch a small batch sorted by DATE.
  // =========================================================================
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices?organization_id=${orgId}` +
              `&invoice_number_startswith=${encodeURIComponent(invoicePrefix)}` +
              `&sort_column=date&sort_order=D&per_page=20`; // Fetch latest 10 by invoice date
  
  const options = {
    'method': 'get',
    'headers': { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` },
    'muteHttpExceptions': true
  };
  
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error(`Zoho API returned an error: ${response.getContentText()}`);
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    
    // If no invoices with our prefix exist, this is the first one.
    if (!data.invoices || data.invoices.length === 0) {
      Logger.log(`No existing invoices found with prefix '${invoicePrefix}'. Starting with 1.`);
      return `${invoicePrefix}1`;
    }
    
    // --- Step 2: Find the highest number from the batch of recent invoices ---
    Logger.log(`Scanning the latest ${data.invoices.length} invoices to find the max number.`);
    
    const allNumbers = data.invoices.map(inv => {
      const match = inv.invoice_number.match(/BSPL\/25-26\/(\d+)/i);
      return match && match[1] ? parseInt(match[1], 10) : 0;
    });
    
    // Use Math.max() to find the true numerical maximum from the fetched batch.
    const lastNumber = Math.max(...allNumbers);
    const newNumber = lastNumber + 1;
    
    Logger.log(`Found max number ${lastNumber} from the recent batch. New number is ${newNumber}.`);
    return `${invoicePrefix}${newNumber}`;

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log("Error fetching last invoice number: " + e.message);
    return null;
  }
}

// =================================================================================
// ZOHO BOOKS - ITEM ID SYNC
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **MAIN FUNCTION:** Fetches items from Zoho Books filtered by name (e.g., "Drift"),
 * matches them against the 'Master SKU Mapping' sheet, and updates the 'Zoho Item ID' column.
 */
function updateZohoItemIDs() {
  
  
  Logger.log('--- Starting Zoho Item ID Sync Process ---');

  // --- Step 1: Get credentials and fetch the filtered items from Zoho ---
  const token = getZohoAccessToken(); // Assumes this helper function exists
  if (!token) {
    Logger.log('Could not get Zoho token. Aborting.');
    return;
  }
  
  // Fetch all items from Zoho where the name contains "Drift".
  const zohoItemMap = _fetchZohoItems(token, "");
  if (zohoItemMap.size === 0) {
    Logger.log('No items containing "Drift" were found in Zoho Books.');
    return;
  }

  // --- Step 2: Read the Master SKU Mapping sheet ---
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
    Logger.log('Master SKU Mapping sheet is empty. Nothing to update.');
    return;
  }
  
  const allData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = allData.shift(); // Get headers and remove from data array

  // Find the column indexes dynamically. This is robust against column reordering.
  const masterSkuIndex = headers.indexOf('Master SKU');
  const zohoItemIdIndex = headers.indexOf('Zoho Item ID');

  if (masterSkuIndex === -1 || zohoItemIdIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error: Could not find 'Master SKU' or 'Zoho Item ID' columns in the mapping sheet.");
    return;
  }

  // --- Step 3: Prepare the updates by matching Master SKUs to Zoho item names ---
  let updatedCount = 0;
  const updates = allData.map(row => {
    const masterSku = String(row[masterSkuIndex]).trim();
    
    // Look up the Master SKU in the map of items we fetched from Zoho.
    // The assumption is that the Zoho Item 'name' IS the 'Master SKU'.
    if (masterSku && zohoItemMap.has(masterSku)) {
      const itemId = zohoItemMap.get(masterSku);
      
      // If the ID is new, increment our counter.
      if (row[zohoItemIdIndex] !== itemId) {
        updatedCount++;
      }
      return [itemId]; // Return the ID to be placed in the Zoho Item ID column
    } else {
      // If no match is found, return the existing value to avoid overwriting it.
      return [row[zohoItemIdIndex]];
    }
  });

  // --- Step 4: Perform a single, efficient batch write operation ---
  if (updates.length > 0) {
    // Write the 'updates' array to the 'Zoho Item ID' column.
    sheet.getRange(2, zohoItemIdIndex + 1, updates.length, 1).setValues(updates);
    Logger.log(`Sync complete. Found matches and updated/verified ${updatedCount} Zoho Item IDs.`);
  }
}


/**
 * **HELPER:** Fetches all paginated items from Zoho Books that match a name filter.
 * @param {string} token - The Zoho API authentication token.
 * @param {string} filterText - The text to search for in the item names (e.g., "Drift").
 * @return {Map<string, string>} A Map where the key is the Item Name and the value is the Item ID.
 */
function _fetchZohoItems(token, filterText) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const orgId = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');  const encodedFilter = encodeURIComponent(filterText);
  const baseUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/items?organization_id=${orgId}&name_contains=${encodedFilter}&page=`;
  
  const options = {
    method: "GET",
    headers: { "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  const itemMap = new Map();
  let page = 1;
  let hasMore = true;

  Logger.log(`Fetching Zoho items with name containing "${filterText}"...`);
  while (hasMore) {
    try {
      const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(baseUrl + page, options);
      if (response.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
        if (json.items && json.items.length > 0) {
          json.items.forEach(item => {
            // Create a map where the item name is the key and the ID is the value.
            itemMap.set(item.sku, item.item_id);
          });
          
          if (json.page_context && json.page_context.has_more_page) {
            page++;
          } else {
            hasMore = false;
          }
        } else {
          hasMore = false;
        }
      } else {
        Logger.log(`Zoho API Error: ${response.getContentText()}`);
        hasMore = false;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log("Zoho Item Fetch Error: " + e.message);
      hasMore = false;
    }
  }
  
  Logger.log(`Fetched a total of ${itemMap.size} matching items from Zoho.`);
  return itemMap;
}

function FETCH_LAST_14_DAYS_QUOTATIONS() {
  try {
    const token = getZohoAccessToken();

    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const ORG_ID = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');
    const BASE_URL = "https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates";
    const DAYS = 14;

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_QUOTATIONS);

    const headers = [
      "Estimate ID",
      "Customer ID",
      "Customer Name",
      "Quotation Date",
      "Quote Number",
      "Reference Number",
      "Zoho Item ID",
      "SKU",
      "Item Name",
      "Rate",
      "Quantity",
      "Shipping Charges",
      "Tax Amount"
    ];

    sheet.clearContents();
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);

    let page = 1;
    let allRows = [];

    const tz = ss.getSpreadsheetTimeZone();
    const dateAfter = new Date();
    dateAfter.setDate(dateAfter.getDate() - DAYS);
    const dateAfterStr = Utilities.formatDate(dateAfter, tz, "yyyy-MM-dd");

    const options = {
      method: "GET",
      headers: { "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    while (true) {
      const url =
        `${BASE_URL}?organization_id=${ORG_ID}` +
        `&status=draft` +
        `&date_after=${dateAfterStr}` +
        `&page=${page}` +
        `&per_page=200`;

      const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
      const statusCode = res.getResponseCode();
      const json = JSON.parse(res.getContentText());

      if (statusCode !== 200) {
        throw new Error(json.message || "Failed to fetch quotations list");
      }

      if (!json.estimates || json.estimates.length === 0) break;

      json.estimates.forEach(est => {

        const detailUrl =
          `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates/${est.estimate_id}` +
          `?organization_id=${ORG_ID}`;

        const detailRes = UrlFetchApp.fetch(detailUrl, options);
        const detailCode = detailRes.getResponseCode();
        const detailJson = JSON.parse(detailRes.getContentText());

        if (detailCode !== 200) {
          throw new Error(
            `Failed to fetch estimate ${est.estimate_id}: ${detailJson.message}`
          );
        }

        const e = detailJson.estimate;
        if (!e || !e.line_items) return;

        const shippingCharge = e.shipping_charge || 0;
        const taxAmount = e.tax_total || 0;

        e.line_items.forEach(li => {
          allRows.push([
            e.estimate_id || "",
            e.customer_id || "",
            e.customer_name || "",
            e.date || "",
            e.estimate_number || "",
            e.reference_number || "",
            li.item_id || "",
            li.sku || "",
            li.name || "",
            li.rate || "",
            li.quantity || "",
            shippingCharge,
            taxAmount
          ]);
        });

      });

      if (!json.page_context || !json.page_context.has_more_page) break;
      page++;
    }

    if (allRows.length > 0) {
      sheet
        .getRange(2, 1, allRows.length, headers.length)
        .setValues(allRows);
    }

    return {
      status: "success",
      message: `Fetched ${allRows.length} quotation line items from last ${DAYS} days`,
      count: allRows.length
    };

  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR in FETCH_LAST_14_DAYS_QUOTATIONS: ${err.message}`);

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: err.message
    };
  }
}


function ENSURE_MASTER_SKU_MAPPINGS_BATCH(mappings) {
  if (!Array.isArray(mappings) || mappings.length === 0) {
    return { status: "ignored", message: "No mappings provided." };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  if (!sheet) {
    return { status: "error", message: "Master SKU Mapping sheet not found." };
  }

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const existingData =
    lastRow > 1
      ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 3).getValues()
      : [];

  // Build lookup set: channel|item|sku
  const existingSet = new Set(
    existingData.map(r =>
      `${r[0]}|${r[1]}|${r[2]}`.toLowerCase().trim()
    )
  );

  const rowsToInsert = [];

  mappings.forEach(m => {
    const key =
      `${m.channel}|${m.channelItemCode}|${m.masterSku}`.toLowerCase().trim();

    if (!existingSet.has(key)) {
      rowsToInsert.push([
        m.channel,
        m.channelItemCode,
        m.masterSku
      ]);
      existingSet.add(key); // prevent duplicates in same batch
    }
  });

  if (rowsToInsert.length > 0) {
    sheet
      .getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rowsToInsert.length, 3)
      .setValues(rowsToInsert);
  }


  return {
    status: rowsToInsert.length ? "added" : "ignored",
    addedCount: rowsToInsert.length
  };
}

function SEND_AND_ACCEPT_ESTIMATE(data) {
  try {

    // ------------------ Validation ------------------
    if (!data || !data.estimateId || !Array.isArray(data.items) || data.items.length === 0) {
      return { status: "error", message: "Invalid data received from frontend." };
    }

    const estimateId = data.estimateId;
    const token = getZohoAccessToken();
    const ORG_ID = "60032126274";

    const options = {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token
      },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    // ------------------ STEP 1: MARK AS SENT ------------------
    const sentUrl =
      `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates/${estimateId}/status/sent` +
      `?organization_id=${ORG_ID}`;

    const sentResp = UrlFetchApp.fetch(sentUrl, options);
    const sentCode = sentResp.getResponseCode();

    if (sentCode !== 200 && sentCode !== 409) {
      const sentResult = JSON.parse(sentResp.getContentText());
      throw new Error(`Failed to mark estimate as sent: ${sentResult.message}`);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(600);

    // ------------------ STEP 2: MARK AS ACCEPTED ------------------
    const acceptUrl =
      `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates/${estimateId}/status/accepted` +
      `?organization_id=${ORG_ID}`;

    const acceptResp = UrlFetchApp.fetch(acceptUrl, options);
    const acceptResult = JSON.parse(acceptResp.getContentText());

    if (acceptResp.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to accept estimate: ${acceptResult.message}`);
    }

    // ------------------ STEP 3: ADD TO PO DATABASE ------------------
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const poSheet = ss.getSheetByName("PO_Database");
    if (!poSheet) throw new Error("PO_Database sheet not found.");

    const today = Utilities.formatDate(
      new Date(),
      ss.getSpreadsheetTimeZone(),
      "yyyy-MM-dd"
    );

    const channelName = "Bulk";

    const storeCode = data.customerName?.includes("Bulk_")
      ? data.customerName.split("Bulk_")[1]
      : data.customerName || "";

    const poNumber = data.referenceNumber || data.quotationNumber;

    const poRows = [];
    const skuMappings = [];

    data.items.forEach(item => {

      poRows.push([
        "New",
        today,
        channelName,
        poNumber,
        storeCode,
        "",
        "",
        item.sku || "",
        item.sku || "",
        item.itemName || "",
        Number(item.quantity),
        "",
        Number(item.rate),
        "",
        item.zohoItemId || "",
        Number(item.quantity),
        "",
        data.customerId || ""
      ]);

      if (item.sku) {
        skuMappings.push({
          channel: "Bulk",
          channelItemCode: item.sku,
          masterSku: item.sku
        });
      }

    });

    // Insert rows
    const startRow = poSheet.getLastRow() + 1;

    poSheet
      .getRange(startRow, 1, poRows.length, poRows[0].length)
      .setValues(poRows);

    SpreadsheetApp.flush();


    // ------------------ STEP 3B: UPDATE SHIPPING CHARGE ------------------

    const shippingCharge = Number(data.shippingCharges || data.shippingCharge || 0);

    if (shippingCharge > 0) {

      const headers = poSheet.getRange(1,1,1,poSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];

      const shippingCol = headers.indexOf("Shipping Charge");

      if (shippingCol !== -1) {

        const shippingValues = new Array(poRows.length)
          .fill([shippingCharge]);

        poSheet
          .getRange(startRow, shippingCol + 1, poRows.length, 1)
          .setValues(shippingValues);

      } else {
        Logger.log("Shipping Charge column not found.");
      }

    }

    SpreadsheetApp.flush();


    // ------------------ STEP 4: UPDATE CUSTOMER IDS ------------------
    updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();


    // ------------------ STEP 5: ENSURE MASTER SKU MAPPING ------------------
    if (skuMappings.length > 0) {

      const mappingResult = ENSURE_MASTER_SKU_MAPPINGS_BATCH(skuMappings);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush();

      Logger.log("SKU Mapping Result: " + JSON.stringify(mappingResult));
    }

    syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation();


    return {
      status: "success",
      message: `Estimate ${poNumber} accepted and PO created successfully.`,
      poNumber,
      rowsCreated: poRows.length
    };

  } catch (err) {

    Logger.log(`ERROR in SEND_AND_ACCEPT_ESTIMATE: ${err.message}`);

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: err.message
    };

  }
}

// =================================================================================
// NIMBUS POST - AUTHENTICATION
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **NEW & ROBUST:** Fetches the authentication token from the Nimbus Post API.
 * This function is self-contained and uses standard Apps Script methods.
 *
 * @return {string|null} The authentication token string on success, or null on failure.
 */
function getNimbusPostToken() {
  // --- 1. Securely retrieve credentials ---
  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const email = scriptProperties.getProperty('NIMBUS_POST_EMAIL');
  const password = scriptProperties.getProperty('NIMBUS_POST_PASSWORD');

  if (!email || !password) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: Nimbus Post email or password not found in script properties. Please run the setup function.');
    return null;
  }

  // --- 2. Configure the API request ---
  const url = "https://ship.nimbuspost.com/api/users/login";
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    email: email,
    password: password
  });
  
  const options = {
    'method': 'post',
    'contentType': 'application/json',
    'payload': payload,
    'muteHttpExceptions': true // This is crucial for error handling
  };

  // --- 3. Make the API call and handle the response ---
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
    const responseText = response.getContentText();
    
    if (responseCode === 200) {
      const data = JSON.parse(responseText);
      
      // Safely extract the token from the response. The most common structure is data.data.token
      const token = data.data;

      if (token) {
        Logger.log('Successfully retrieved Nimbus Post token.'+token);
        return token;
      } else {
        // This handles cases where the login was "successful" but the token was missing.
        throw new Error("Token not found in the successful API response. Full response: " + responseText);
      }
    } else {
      // This handles API errors like "401 Unauthorized" (wrong password).
      throw new Error(`API returned an error (Code: ${responseCode}): ${responseText}`);
    }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR fetching Nimbus Post token: ${e.message}`);
    return null;
  }
}

function getShiprocketToken() {

  Logger.log("ENTERED getShiprocketToken");

  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const email = props.getProperty('SHIPROCKET_EMAIL');
  const password = props.getProperty('SHIPROCKET_PASSWORD');

  if (!email || !password) {
    throw new Error("Shiprocket credentials missing");
  }

  const TOKEN_KEY = "SHIPROCKET_TOKEN";
  const EXPIRY_KEY = "SHIPROCKET_TOKEN_EXPIRY";

  const existingToken = props.getProperty(TOKEN_KEY);
  const expiry = props.getProperty(EXPIRY_KEY);

  const now = new Date().getTime();

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 1. RETURN EXISTING TOKEN IF VALID
  // --------------------------------------------------
  if (existingToken && expiry && now < Number(expiry)) {
    Logger.log("Using stored token");
    return existingToken;
  }

  Logger.log("Fetching new token...");

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 2. FETCH NEW TOKEN
  // --------------------------------------------------
  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
    "https://apiv2.shiprocket.in/v1/external/auth/login",
    {
      method: "post",
      contentType: "application/json",
      payload: JSON.stringify({
        email: email,
        password: password
      }),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }
  );

  const responseText = response.getContentText();
  Logger.log("TOKEN RESPONSE: " + responseText);

  const json = JSON.parse(responseText);

  if (!json.token) {
    throw new Error("Token not received");
  }

  const token = json.token;

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 3. STORE TOKEN + EXPIRY
  // --------------------------------------------------
  const expiryTime = now + (55 * 60 * 1000); // 55 mins

  props.setProperty(TOKEN_KEY, token);
  props.setProperty(EXPIRY_KEY, expiryTime.toString());

  Logger.log("New token stored");

  return token;
}
