function createShipment(eeReferenceCode) {

  if (!eeReferenceCode) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No EE Reference Code provided" };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const data = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const refIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
  const channelIdx = headers.indexOf("Channel Name");
  const boxIdx = headers.indexOf("Box Data");

  const row = data.find(r => String(r[refIdx]).trim() === eeReferenceCode);

  if (!row) {
    Logger.log("Order Not found");
    return { status: "error", message: "Order not found" };
  }

  const channel = String(row[channelIdx]).trim();
  const boxCount = Number(row[boxIdx]) || 0;

  const excluded = [
    "Instamart","Zepto","BB","RBL",
    "FlipkartMinutes","Blinkit","Amazon_FBA"
  ];

  const useShiprocket = !excluded.includes(channel) && boxCount === 1;
  Logger.log(channel);
  Logger.log(boxCount);

  Logger.log(useShiprocket);

  if (useShiprocket) {
    return createShiprocketShipment(eeReferenceCode);
  } else {
    return createNimbusPostShipment(eeReferenceCode);
  }
}

function createShiprocketShipment(eeReferenceCode) {

  Logger.log(`--- Starting Shiprocket Shipment Creation for: ${eeReferenceCode} ---`);

  /*const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(30000)) {
    return { status: "skipped", message: "Already processing" };
  }
  */

  let rowsToMark = [];
  let dbSheet;

  // ---------------- HELPERS ----------------
  const toStr = (val) => val ? String(val).trim() : "";
  const toInt = (val, def = 1) => {
    const n = parseInt(val);
    return isNaN(n) ? def : n;
  };
  const toFloat = (val, def = 0) => {
    const n = parseFloat(val);
    return isNaN(n) ? def : n;
  };

  try {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dbData.shift();

    const refIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
    const awbIdx = headers.indexOf("AWB");

    // ---------------- DUPLICATE CHECK ----------------
    const existing = dbData.find(r =>
      String(r[refIdx]).trim() === eeReferenceCode &&
      String(r[awbIdx]).trim() !== ""
    );

    if (existing) {
      Logger.log('skipped');
      return {
        status: "skipped",
        message: "Shipment already exists",
        awb: existing[awbIdx]
      };
    }

    // ---------------- MARK PROCESSING ----------------
    rowsToMark = dbData
      .map((r, i) => String(r[refIdx]).trim() === eeReferenceCode ? i + 2 : null)
      .filter(Boolean);

    rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
      dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIdx + 1).setValue("PROCESSING");
    });

    // ---------------- LOAD DATA ----------------
    const customerMap = _loadEECustomerData(ss);
    const packingData = _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode);
    const orderData = _loadOrderData(ss, eeReferenceCode);


    const cleanName = (name) => {return (name || "").replace(/^Bulk_/, "").trim();};
    const splitName = (name) => {const parts = name.split(" ");return {first: parts[0] || "Customer",last: parts.slice(1).join(" ") || "."};};

    const customer = customerMap.get(orderData.customerId);
    if (!customer) {
      Logger.log("Customer NOT FOUND for ID: " + orderData.customerId);
      throw new Error("Customer not found");
    }
    const cleanedName = cleanName(customer['Company Name']);
    const nameObj = splitName(cleanedName);

    

    const getVal = (row, col) => row[headers.indexOf(col)];
    const firstItem = orderData.items[0];

    // ---------------- ORDER VALUE ----------------
    const invoiceDate = new Date(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Date'));
    const invoiceValue = toFloat(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Total'), 0);
    const baseShipping = toFloat(getVal(firstItem, 'Shipping Charge'), 0);
    const shippingCharge = baseShipping * 1.05; // +5%
    const finalOrderValue = invoiceValue;

    // ---------------- PACKING ----------------
    const box = packingData[0]; // take first row only
    if (!box) {
      throw new Error("Packing data missing");
      }
    const weightGrams = toFloat(box['Box Weight'], 500);
    const length = toInt(box['Box Length'], 10);
    const breadth = toInt(box['Box Width'], 10);
    const height = toInt(box['Box Height'], 10);
    
    // convert to kg
    let weightKg = weightGrams / 1000;
    // safety fallback
    if (weightKg <= 0) weightKg = 0.5;

    // ---------------- ITEMS ----------------
    const items = orderData.items.map(row => ({
      name: toStr(getVal(row, 'Item Name')),
      sku: toStr(getVal(row, 'Master SKU')),
      units: toInt(getVal(row, 'Qty'), 1),
      selling_price: toFloat(getVal(row, 'Unit Cost (Tax Exclusive)'), 0),
      tax: "5"
    }));

    // ---------------- TOKEN ----------------
    const token = getShiprocketToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error("Token failed");

    // ---------------- FINAL PAYLOAD ----------------
    const payload = {
      request_pickup: true,
      print_label: true,
      generate_manifest: true,
      insurance: false,
      is_insured: 0, 

      order_id: eeReferenceCode,
      order_date: Utilities.formatDate(invoiceDate, "Asia/Kolkata", "yyyy-MM-dd"),

      billing_customer_name: nameObj.first,
      billing_last_name: nameObj.last,
      billing_address: toStr(customer['Billing Street']),
      billing_city: toStr(customer['Billing City']),
      billing_pincode: toInt(customer['Billing Zip']),
      billing_state: toStr(customer['Billing State']),
      billing_country: "India",
      billing_email: toStr(customer['Support Email']),
      billing_phone: toStr(customer['Support Contact']).replace(/\.0$/, ""),

      shipping_is_billing: true,

      order_items: items,

      payment_method: "Prepaid",
      sub_total: finalOrderValue,
      shipping_charges : shippingCharge,


      weight: weightKg.toFixed(2),
      length: length,
      breadth: breadth,
      height: height,

      pickup_location: "warehouse-2"
    };

    Logger.log("FORWARD PAYLOAD: " + JSON.stringify(payload));

    // ---------------- API CALL ----------------
    const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
      "https://apiv2.shiprocket.in/v1/external/shipments/create/forward-shipment",
      {
        method: "post",
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
          "Content-Type": "application/json"
        },
        payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      }
    );

    Logger.log("FORWARD RESPONSE: " + res.getContentText());

    

    const json = JSON.parse(res.getContentText());
    const payloadRes = json.payload || {};
    const awb = payloadRes.awb_code;
    const courier = payloadRes.courier_name || "Shiprocket";
    const labelUrl = payloadRes.label_url;

    if (!awb) throw new Error("AWB not generated");

    const trackingUrl = `https://shiprocket.co/tracking/${awb}`;

    // ---------------- UPDATE DB ----------------
    const carrierIdx = headers.indexOf('Carrier');
    const trackingIdx = headers.indexOf('Tracking Status');
    const trackingUrlIdx = headers.indexOf('Tracking URL');
    const labelIdx = headers.indexOf('Label URL');
    const bookedDateIdx = headers.indexOf('Booked Date');
    const pickupDateIdx = headers.indexOf('Pickup Date');

  rowsToMark.forEach(r => {

  const now = new Date();

  // ---------------- TODAY DATE ----------------
  const today = new Date(now);

  // ---------------- PICKUP DATE LOGIC ----------------
  const hourIST = Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "HH");
  
  let pickupDate = new Date(now);

  if (parseInt(hourIST) >= 14) {
    pickupDate.setDate(pickupDate.getDate() + 1);
  }

  // ---------------- UPDATE ----------------
  dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIdx + 1).setValue(awb);
  dbSheet.getRange(r, carrierIdx + 1).setValue(courier);

  if (trackingIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, trackingIdx + 1).setValue("AWB Assigned");
  }

  if (bookedDateIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, bookedDateIdx + 1).setValue(today);
  }

  if (pickupDateIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, pickupDateIdx + 1).setValue(pickupDate);
  }

  if (trackingUrlIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, trackingUrlIdx + 1).setValue(trackingUrl);
  }

  if (labelIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, labelIdx + 1).setValue(labelUrl);
  }
  });

  return {
      status: "success",
      awb,
      courier,
      label: labelUrl,
      tracking: trackingUrl
    };

  }
  catch (e) {

    if (rowsToMark.length && dbSheet) {
      const headers = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues()[0];
      const awbIdx = headers.indexOf("AWB");
      rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
        dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIdx + 1).setValue("");
      });
    }

    return { status: "error", message: e.message };

  } finally {
    //lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function createNimbusPostShipment(eeReferenceCode) {
  if (!eeReferenceCode) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No EE Order Reference ID was provided." };
  }

  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(30000)) { // 30 sec safety
    return {
      status: "skipped",
      message: "Shipment creation already in progress. Please wait."
    };
  }

  Logger.log(`--- Starting Nimbus Post Shipment Creation for: ${eeReferenceCode} ---`);

  let rowsToMark = [];
  let awbIndex = -1;
  let refIdIndex = -1;

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  try {

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    // READ DB + SAFETY CHECK (AWB / PROCESSING)
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dbData.shift();

    refIdIndex = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code');
    awbIndex = headers.indexOf('AWB');

    if (refIdIndex === -1 || awbIndex === -1) {
      throw new Error("Required columns ('EE_reference_code', 'AWB') not found in PO_Database.");
    }

    const blockingRow = dbData.find(row => {
      const awbVal = String(row[awbIndex]).trim().toUpperCase();
      return (
        String(row[refIdIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode &&
        awbVal !== ""
      );
    });

    if (blockingRow) {
      return {
        status: "skipped",
        message: "Shipment already created or in progress.",
        awb: blockingRow[awbIndex]
      };
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    // MARK AS PROCESSING (prevents retry while API is running)
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    rowsToMark = dbData
      .map((row, index) =>
        String(row[refIdIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode ? index + 2 : null
      )
      .filter(Boolean);

    rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
      dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIndex + 1).setValue("PROCESSING");
    });

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    // LOAD REQUIRED DATA
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    const customerMap = _loadEECustomerData(ss);
    const packingData = _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode);
    const orderData = _loadOrderData(ss, eeReferenceCode);

    if (!orderData.items.length) {
      throw new Error(`No items found for EE Ref: ${eeReferenceCode}`);
    }

    if (!customerMap.has(orderData.customerId)) {
      throw new Error(`Customer ID not found: ${orderData.customerId}`);
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    // BUILD PAYLOAD + API CALL
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    const payload = _buildNimbusPayload(
      eeReferenceCode,
      orderData,
      customerMap.get(orderData.customerId),
      packingData,
      dbSheet
    );

    const token = getNimbusPostToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error("Nimbus token generation failed.");

    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
      "https://ship.nimbuspost.com/api/shipmentcargo/create",
      {
        method: "post",
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
          "Content-Type": "application/json"
        },
        payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      }
    );

    const responseData = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

    if (!responseData.status) {
      throw new Error(responseData.message || "Nimbus API error");
    }

    const nimbus = responseData.data;
    const awbNumber = nimbus.awb_number;
    const trackingUrl = `https://ship.nimbuspost.com/shipping/tracking/${awbNumber}`;

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    // UPDATE PO_DATABASE (selective write)
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    const carrierIndex = headers.indexOf('Carrier');
    const trackingIndex = headers.indexOf('Tracking Status');
    const trackingUrlIndex = headers.indexOf('Tracking URL');
    const bookedDateIndex = headers.indexOf('Booked Date');
    const pickupDateIndex = headers.indexOf('Pickup Date');

    rowsToMark.forEach(row => {

  const now = new Date();

  // ---------------- BOOKED DATE ----------------
  const bookedDate = new Date(now);

  // ---------------- PICKUP DATE LOGIC ----------------
  const hourIST = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "HH"), 10);

  let pickupDate = new Date(now);

  if (hourIST >= 14) {
    pickupDate.setDate(pickupDate.getDate() + 1);
  }

  // ---------------- OPTIONAL: SKIP SUNDAY ----------------
  if (pickupDate.getDay() === 0) {
    pickupDate.setDate(pickupDate.getDate() + 1);
  }

  // ---------------- UPDATE ----------------
  dbSheet.getRange(row, carrierIndex + 1).setValue(nimbus.courier_name);
  dbSheet.getRange(row, awbIndex + 1).setValue(awbNumber);

  if (trackingIndex !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(row, trackingIndex + 1).setValue(nimbus.status);
  }

  if (trackingUrlIndex !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(row, trackingUrlIndex + 1).setValue(trackingUrl);
  }

  // ---------------- NEW FIELDS ----------------
  if (bookedDateIndex !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(row, bookedDateIndex + 1).setValue(bookedDate);
  }

  if (pickupDateIndex !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(row, pickupDateIndex + 1).setValue(pickupDate);
  }

  });

 

    return {
      status: "success",
      message: `Shipment created successfully`,
      awb: awbNumber
    };

  } catch (e) {
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    // CLEANUP: remove PROCESSING flag on failure
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    if (rowsToMark.length && awbIndex !== -1) {
      rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
        dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIndex + 1).setValue("");
      });
    }

    Logger.log(`ERROR: ${e.message}`);
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };

  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}


// --- DATA GATHERING HELPERS ---

function _loadEECustomerData(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_EE_CUSTOMERS);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();
  const map = new Map();
  // Dynamically find columns
  const idIndex = headers.indexOf('Customer ID');
  // ... find other necessary customer column indexes ...
  data.forEach(row => {
    const customerId = row[idIndex];
    if (customerId) {
      // Store the entire row object for easy access
      map.set(customerId.toString(), Object.fromEntries(headers.map((key, i) => [key, row[i]])));
    }
  });
  return map;
}

function _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_MASTER_DATA);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();
  const refCodeIndex = headers.indexOf('Reference Code');
  
  return data
    .filter(row => String(row[refCodeIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode)
    .map(row => Object.fromEntries(headers.map((key, i) => [key, row[i]])));
}

function _loadOrderData(ss, eeReferenceCode) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();
  const refIdIndex = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code');
  const customerIdIndex = headers.indexOf('EE Customer ID');
  
  const items = data.filter(row => String(row[refIdIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode);
  const customerId = items.length > 0 ? items[0][customerIdIndex] : null;

  return { items: items, customerId: customerId.toString() };
}

// --- PAYLOAD BUILDER HELPER ---

function _buildNimbusPayload(eeReferenceCode,orderData, customerDetails, packingData,dbSheet) {
  // --- Consignee & Invoice Details ---
  const firstItem = orderData.items[0];
  const orderHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 40).getValues()[0]; // Get headers once
  
  const getVal = (row, colName) => row[orderHeaders.indexOf(colName)];

  const invoiceNumber = getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Number');
  const invoiceDate = new Date(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Date'));
  const invoiceValue = parseFloat(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Total'));
  const ewb = parseFloat(getVal(firstItem, 'EWB'));



  // --- Group Packing Data by Box ID to create the 'products' array ---
  const boxes = packingData.reduce((acc, item) => {
    const boxId = item['Box ID'];
    if (!acc[boxId]) {
      acc[boxId] = {
        box_weight: 0,
        box_length: 0,
        box_breadth: 0,
        box_height: 0,
        box_price: 0
      };
    }
    acc[boxId].box_weight = parseFloat(item['Box Weight']);
    acc[boxId].box_length = Math.max(acc[boxId].box_length, parseFloat(item['Box Length']));
    acc[boxId].box_breadth = Math.max(acc[boxId].box_breadth, parseFloat(item['Box Width']));
    acc[boxId].box_height = Math.max(acc[boxId].box_height, parseFloat(item['Box Height']));
    acc[boxId].box_price += parseFloat(item['Value']);
    return acc;
  }, {});

  const productsArray = Object.values(boxes).map(box => ({
    "product_name": "Puzzles", // Or derive from item names if needed
    "product_hsn_code": "95036090", // Or derive from a master data sheet
    "product_lbh_unit": "cm",
    "no_of_box": "1",
    "product_tax_per": "5",
    "product_price": box.box_price.toFixed(2),
    "product_weight_unit": "gram",
    "product_length": box.box_length,
    "product_breadth": box.box_breadth,
    "product_height": box.box_height,
    "product_weight": box.box_weight
  }));

  // --- Construct the Final Payload ---
  const payload = {
    "order_id": eeReferenceCode,
    "payment_method": "prepaid",
    "consignee_name": customerDetails['Company Name'],
    "consignee_company_name": customerDetails['Company Name'],
    "consignee_phone": customerDetails['Support Contact'],
    "consignee_email": customerDetails['Support Email'],
    "consignee_gst_number":customerDetails['GST'],
    "consignee_address": customerDetails['Billing Street'],
    "consignee_pincode": customerDetails['Billing Zip'],
    "consignee_city": customerDetails['Billing City'],
    "consignee_state": customerDetails['Billing State'],
    "no_of_invoices": "1",
    "no_of_boxes": productsArray.length.toString(),
    "courier_id": "110", // Delhivery Bulk
    "request_auto_pickup": "yes",
    "invoice": [{
      "invoice_number": invoiceNumber,
      "invoice_date": Utilities.formatDate(invoiceDate, "GMT", "dd-MM-yyyy"),
      "invoice_value": invoiceValue,
      "ebn_number": ewb || ""
    }],
    "pickup": {
      "warehouse_name": "Brainlytic Solutions Private Limited", // Hard-coded as per example
      "name": "Mohan Dewangan",
      "address": "Khasra No. 325/5 325/22, Ring Road No, 1, DD Nagar, Raipura,",
      "address_2": "Near Shree Siddhi Vinayak Marriage Palace, Vinayaka Vihar",
      "city": "Raipur",
      "state": "Chhattisgarh",
      "pincode": "492013",
      "phone": "8103733766",
      "gst_number": "22AAICB3513C1ZF"
    },
    "products": productsArray
  };
  
  return payload;
}

// =.===============================================================================
// NIMBUS POST - BULK TRACKING STATUS UPDATE (OPTIMIZED)
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **MAIN FUNCTION:** Fetches the latest tracking status from Nimbus Post for all
 * non-delivered shipments and performs an efficient batch update on the 'PO_Database' sheet.
 */
function updateTrackingStatusFromNimbusPost() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PO_Database');
  
  if (dbSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
    Logger.log('No data in PO_Database to track.');
    return;
  }
  const TRACKING_COLUMNS = [
  'Tracking Status',
  'EDD',
  'Latest Status',
  'Latest Status Date',
  'Current Location',
  'Delivered Date'
 ];

  // --- 1. READ: Get all non-delivered AWBs from the sheet ---
  const dataRange = dbSheet.getDataRange();
  const allData = dataRange.getValues();
  const headers = allData.shift();

  // Find column indexes dynamically
  const awbIndex = headers.indexOf('AWB');
  const trackingStatusIndex = headers.indexOf('Tracking Status');
  
  if (awbIndex === -1 || trackingStatusIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error: 'AWB' or 'Tracking Status' column not found. Aborting.");
    return;
  }

  const awbToRowIndexes = new Map();
  const awbsToFetch = new Set();

  allData.forEach((row, index) => {
    const awb = String(row[awbIndex]).trim();
    const status = String(row[trackingStatusIndex]).toLowerCase();
    
    // Only add AWB to our fetch list if it exists and is not 'delivered' or 'rto delivered'
    if (awb && status !== 'delivered' && status !== 'rto delivered') {
      awbsToFetch.add(awb);
      // Map the AWB to all row numbers it appears in (0-indexed for the data array)
      if (!awbToRowIndexes.has(awb)) awbToRowIndexes.set(awb, []);
      awbToRowIndexes.get(awb).push(index);
    }
  });

  if (awbsToFetch.size === 0) {
    Logger.log('No shipments found that require a status update. All are delivered or have no AWB.');
    return;
  }

  // --- 2. FETCH: Get tracking data from Nimbus Post API ---
  const token = getNimbusPostToken(); // Assumes this helper exists
  if (!token) return;
  
  const apiUrl = "https://api.nimbuspost.com/v1/shipments/track/bulk"; // Endpoint for bulk AWB
  const options = {
    method: "POST", contentType: "application/json",
    headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + token },
    payload: JSON.stringify({ "awb": Array.from(awbsToFetch) }),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(apiUrl, options);
  const result = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

  if (!result.status || !Array.isArray(result.data)) {
    Logger.log(`Nimbus Post API Error: ${JSON.stringify(result)}`);
    return;
  }

  // --- 3. PROCESS: Create an update plan in memory ---
  const updates = {}; // Key: row index, Value: { colIndex: value, ... }
  
  result.data.forEach(entry => {
    const awb = String(entry.awb_number);
    const history = Array.isArray(entry.history) ? entry.history : [];
    const latestEvent = history.length > 0 ? history[0] : {};
    
    if (awbToRowIndexes.has(awb)) {
      const rowIndexes = awbToRowIndexes.get(awb);
      rowIndexes.forEach(rowIndex => {
        // Prepare the updates for this row
        updates[rowIndex] = {
          [trackingStatusIndex]: entry.status || '', // Tracking Status
          [headers.indexOf('EDD')]: entry.edd || '',
          [headers.indexOf('Latest Status')]: latestEvent.message || '',
          [headers.indexOf('Latest Status Date')]: latestEvent.event_time || '',
          [headers.indexOf('Current Location')]: latestEvent.location || '',
          [headers.indexOf('Delivered Date')]: entry.delivered_date || ''
        };
      });
    }
  });

  // --- 4. WRITE: Update ONLY tracking-related columns (SAFE) ---

const colIndexes = {};
TRACKING_COLUMNS.forEach(col => {
  const idx = headers.indexOf(col);
  if (idx !== -1) colIndexes[col] = idx;
});

let updatedRowCount = 0;

Object.entries(updates).forEach(([rowIndex, rowUpdates]) => {
  const sheetRow = Number(rowIndex) + 2; // +2 because header removed

  Object.entries(rowUpdates).forEach(([colIndex, value]) => {
    // Write only the specific cell
    dbSheet.getRange(sheetRow, Number(colIndex) + 1).setValue(value);
  });

  updatedRowCount++;
});

Logger.log(`Safely updated tracking fields for ${updatedRowCount} rows.`);


}

function handleNimbusWebhook(data) 
{

  try {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("PO_Database");

    const awb = String(data.awb_number).trim();
    const status = data.status || "";
    const message = data.message || "";
    const eventTime = data.event_time || "";
    const location = data.location || "";

    const range = sheet.getDataRange();
    const values = range.getValues();
    const headers = values[0];

    const awbIndex = headers.indexOf("AWB");
    const statusIndex = headers.indexOf("Tracking Status");
    const latestStatusIndex = headers.indexOf("Latest Status");
    const statusDateIndex = headers.indexOf("Latest Status Date");
    const locationIndex = headers.indexOf("Current Location");
    const deliveredIndex = headers.indexOf("Delivered Date");

    if (awbIndex === -1) {
      return responseJSON({status:'error',message:'AWB column missing'});
    }

    for (let i = 1; i < values.length; i++) {

      if (String(values[i][awbIndex]).trim() === awb) {

        if (statusIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,statusIndex+1).setValue(status);

        if (latestStatusIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,latestStatusIndex+1).setValue(message);

        if (statusDateIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,statusDateIndex+1).setValue(eventTime);

        if (locationIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,locationIndex+1).setValue(location);

        if (deliveredIndex !== -1 && status.toLowerCase() === "delivered")
          sheet.getRange(i+1,deliveredIndex+1).setValue(eventTime);

      }

    }

    return responseJSON({status:"success"});

  } catch(err) {

    return responseJSON({
      status:"error",
      message:err.toString()
    });

  }

}

function tere()
{
  getBoxSummaryByEEReference("AZ250568");
}


function getBoxSummaryByEEReference(eeReferenceCode) {
  const boxMap = {};

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const packingData = _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode);

  packingData.forEach(row => {
    const boxId   = row['Box ID'];
    const length  = Number(row['Box Length']);
    const width   = Number(row['Box Width']);
    const height  = Number(row['Box Height']);
    const weight  = Number(row['Box Weight']);

    if (!boxId) return;

    if (!boxMap[boxId]) {
      boxMap[boxId] = {
        boxId,
        length,
        width,
        height,
        weight
      };
    }
  });

  const data = Object.values(boxMap).map(box => ({
    "Box ID": box.boxId,
    "Weight": `${Math.round(box.weight / 1000)}`,
    "Dimensions": `${box.length}x${box.width}x${box.height}`
  }));

  Logger.log(data);

  return {
    status: 'success',
    data
  };
}

function saveEasyEcomShipmentDetails(payload) {

  // 1. Get Auth Token
  const token = getEasyEcomToken();
  if (!token) {
    return {
      status: "error",
      message: "Auth Token Failed."
    };
  }

  // 2. Get API Key
  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const X_API_KEY = scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');

  // 3. API Endpoint
  const url = "https://api.easyecom.io/oms/b2b/v1/save-shipment-details";

  // 4. API Request Options
  const options = {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": "Bearer " + token,
      "x-api-key": X_API_KEY,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  // 5. Send Request
  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
  const responseText = response.getContentText();

  Logger.log("EasyEcom Shipment Response Code: " + responseCode);
  Logger.log("EasyEcom Shipment Response: " + responseText);

  // 6. Parse Response
  let result;
  try {
    result = JSON.parse(responseText);
  } catch (e) {
    result = { rawResponse: responseText };
  }

  return {
    statusCode: responseCode,
    response: result
  };
}

function testGenerateEWayBillPartA() {
  const invoiceId = "1975394000254656003";

  const token = getZohoAccessToken(); 
  
  // Step 1: Create Zoho Record
  const ewayBillId = createEWayBillRecord(invoiceId,token);
  
  if (ewayBillId) {
    Logger.log("Step 1 Success: Record Created. Zoho ID: " + ewayBillId);
    
    // Step 2: Push to Portal
    const pushResult = pushToGovernmentPortal(ewayBillId,token);
    
    if (pushResult.code === 0) {
      Logger.log("Step 2 Success: Part A Slip Number: " + pushResult.ewaybill.part_a_slip_number);
    } else {
      // Common errors: "Invalid GSTIN", "PIN code distance mismatch"
      Logger.log("Step 2 Failed: " + pushResult.message);
    }
  }
}
/**
 * Step 1: Saves transportation details (Part A) to Zoho
 */
function createEWayBillRecord(invoiceId,token) {
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/ewaybills?organization_id=60032126274`;
  
  const payload = {

    "invoice_id": invoiceId,      // Try this first
    "transaction_type": "invoice",
    "document_type": "invoice",
    "transportation_details": {
      "transporter_id": "1975394000002734361", // Replace with valid Transporter GSTIN
      "distance": 150,
      "transport_mode": "road"
    }
  };
  Logger.log(payload);

  const options = {
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
      "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    "payload": JSON.stringify(payload),
    "muteHttpExceptions": true
  };

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

  if (json.code === 0) {
    return json.ewaybill.ewaybill_id;
  } else {
    Logger.log("Error creating record: " + json.message);
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Step 2: Pushes Part A to the government portal via Zoho GSP
 */
function pushToGovernmentPortal(ewayBillId,token) {
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/ewaybills/${ewayBillId}/generate?organization_id=60032126274`;
  
  const options = {
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
      "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token
    },
    "muteHttpExceptions": true
  };

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  return JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
}
// =================================================================================
// AMAZON FBA - TWO-STAGE INBOUND SHIPMENT WORKFLOW
// =================================================================================
//

function getAmazonAccessToken() {
  var scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  // ... (rest of the function is identical, no changes needed)
  var clientId = scriptProperties.getProperty('AMAZON_CLIENT_ID');
  var clientSecret = scriptProperties.getProperty('AMAZON_CLIENT_SECRET');
  var refreshToken = scriptProperties.getProperty('AMAZON_REFRESH_TOKEN');
  var url = 'https://api.amazon.com/auth/o2/token';
  var options = {
    'method': 'post',
    'contentType': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
    'muteHttpExceptions': true,
    'payload': { 'grant_type': 'refresh_token', 'refresh_token': refreshToken, 'client_id': clientId, 'client_secret': clientSecret }
  };
  try {
    var response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    var responseData = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    if (responseData.access_token) { return responseData.access_token; } 
    else { Logger.log('Error getting access token: ' + response.getContentText()); return null; }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Exception fetching access token: ' + e.message); return null; }
}



// ============================================================================
// SP API functions to create plan and shipments on Amazon for FBA Inbound
// ============================================================================
const AMAZON = {
  endpoint: 'https://sellingpartnerapi-eu.amazon.com',
  marketplaceId: 'A21TJRUUN4KGV',
  apiPath: '/inbound/fba/2024-03-20'
};

//Get Inbound ID
function createAmazonFbaInboundPlan(data,poRef) {
  try {
    const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error('Amazon access token missing');

    const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 0 — Reuse inbound plan if already known
    // ==================================================

    if (data.inboundPlanId) {
      Logger.log(
        `Inbound Plan ID provided in input for PO ${poRef}: ${data.inboundPlanId}. Reusing.`
      );

      return {
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Inbound plan reused from input data.',
        data: {
          inboundPlanId: data.inboundPlanId,
          reused: true,
          source: 'input'
        }
      };
    }


    // ==================================================
    // STEP 1 — Create inbound plan (only if needed)
    // ==================================================
    const { inboundPlanId, operationId } =
      createInboundPlan_(token, endpoint, poRef, data.items);

    // STEP 1.5 — Poll async creation
    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, operationId);

    Logger.log("Updating Database");

    // STEP 2 — Persist in DB
    updatePoDatabase_(poRef, inboundPlanId,"","");

    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Amazon FBA inbound plan created successfully.',
      data: {
        inboundPlanId,
        reused: false,
        source: 'created'
      }
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`Amazon FBA inbound plan failed: ${e.message}`);

    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

//Get Placement Option ID and Shipment ID
function generateAndListAmazonPlacementDirect(poRef) {
  try {
    const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error('Amazon access token missing');

    const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 0 — Fetch inboundPlanId from PO DB
    // ==================================================
    const { inboundPlanId } = getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef);
    if (!inboundPlanId) {
      throw new Error(`Inbound Plan ID not found for PO ${poRef}`);
    }

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 1 — Fetch items + warehouseId from PO DB
    // ==================================================
    const { items, warehouseId } = getPoItemsFromDB_(poRef);

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 2 — Generate placement options
    // ==================================================
    const url =
      `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions`;

    const payload = {
      customPlacement: [
        {
          warehouseId: warehouseId,
          items: items.map(i => ({
            msku: i.articleCode,
            quantity: i.qty,
            labelOwner: 'SELLER',
            prepOwner: 'NONE'
          }))
        }
      ]
    };

    Logger.log(JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2));

    

    const res = fetchSigned_(
      token,
      { method: 'POST', url, payload },
      [202]
    );

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 3 — Poll async operation
    // ==================================================
    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, res.operationId);
    

    const { placementOptionId, shipmentId } = listPlacementOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId);
    updatePoDatabase_(poRef, "", shipmentId, placementOptionId);

    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Amazon placement options generated successfully.',
      data: {
        inboundPlanId,
        placementOperationId: res.operationId,
        warehouseId
      }
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`generateAmazonPlacementDirect failed for PO ${poRef}: ${e.message}`);

    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

function setPackingInformationAndConfirmPlacementDirect(poRef) {
  try {
    // ==================================================
    // STEP 0 — Auth + endpoint
    // ==================================================
    const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error('Amazon access token missing');

    const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

    

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 1 — Fetch FBA IDs from PO DB
    // ==================================================
    const {
      inboundPlanId,
      placementId,
      shipmentId
    } = getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef);

    if (!inboundPlanId) {
      throw new Error(`Inbound Plan ID missing for PO ${poRef}`);
    }
    if (!placementId) {
      throw new Error(`Placement ID missing for PO ${poRef}`);
    }
    if (!shipmentId) {
      throw new Error(`Shipment ID missing for PO ${poRef}`);
    }

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 2 — Load + convert packing data
    // ==================================================
    const packingRows =
      _loadPackingData(SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(), poRef);

    if (!packingRows.length) {
      throw new Error(`No packing data found for PO ${poRef}`);
    }

    const boxes = buildBoxesFromPackingData_(packingRows);
    Logger.log('Packing boxes:');
    Logger.log(boxes);

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 3 — Set packing information (MANUAL_PROCESS)
    // ==================================================
    const packOpId = setPackingInformation_(
      token,
      endpoint,
      inboundPlanId,
      shipmentId,   // using shipmentId (post-placement flow)
      boxes
    );

    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, packOpId);

    const genTransopID = generateTransportationOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId,placementId, shipmentId);
     pollOperation_(token, endpoint, genTransopID);

 

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 4 — Confirm placement option
    // ==================================================
    const confirmOpId = confirmPlacement_(
      token,
      endpoint,
      inboundPlanId,
      placementId
    );

    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, confirmOpId);
    

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 5 — Fetch shipment confirmation ID ✅
    // ==================================================
    const shipmentConfirmationId =
      getShipmentConfirmationId_(
        token,
        endpoint,
        inboundPlanId,
        shipmentId
      );

    // (Optional) store in DB
    updatePoDatabase_(poRef, "", "", "", shipmentConfirmationId);

    const options = listTransportationOptions_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId);
    
    const atsTransportationOptionId = getATSTransportationOptionId_(options);
    
    const confirmTransOpId = confirmTransportationOption_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId,atsTransportationOptionId);
    
    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, confirmTransOpId);

    getShipmentConfirmationId_(
        token,
        endpoint,
        inboundPlanId,
        shipmentId
      );

    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: `Packing + placement confirmed for PO ${poRef}`,
      data: {
        inboundPlanId,
        placementId,
        shipmentId
      }
    };


  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(
      `setPackingInformationAndConfirmPlacementDirect failed for PO ${poRef}: ${e.message}`
    );

    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

function getShipmentConfirmationId_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId) 
{
  const url =`${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}` +`/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/shipments/${shipmentId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(token,{ method: 'GET', url },[200]);
  Logger.log(res);

  const confirmationId =
    res.shipmentConfirmationId ||
    res.shipmentConfirmation?.shipmentConfirmationId ||
    null;

  if (!confirmationId) {
    throw new Error(
      `ShipmentConfirmationId not found for shipment ${shipmentId}`
    );
  }

  return confirmationId;
}

function listTransportationOptions_(token,  endpoint,  inboundPlanId,  shipmentId)
  {
   const url =
    `${endpoint}/inbound/fba/2024-03-20/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}` +
    `/transportationOptions?shipmentId=${shipmentId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'GET', url },
    [200]
  );

  return res.transportationOptions || [];
}

function confirmPlacement_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, placementOptionId) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions/${placementOptionId}/confirmation`;
  return fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'POST', url, payload: {} }, [202]).operationId;
}


function confirmTransportationOption_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId,transportationOptionId)
{
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}` +
    `/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}` +
    `/transportationOptions/confirmation`;

  const payload = {
    transportationSelections: [
      {
        shipmentId,
        transportationOptionId
      }
    ]
  };

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'POST', url, payload },
    [202]
  );

  return res.operationId;
}


function setPackingInformation_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, shipmentId, boxes) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/packingInformation`;

  const payload = {
    packageGroupings: [
      {
        shipmentId: shipmentId, // ✅ REQUIRED for India
        boxes: boxes.map(b => ({
          quantity: b.quantity || 1,
          contentInformationSource: 'MANUAL_PROCESS',
          dimensions: {
            unitOfMeasurement: 'CM',
            length: Number(b.lengthCm),
            width: Number(b.widthCm),
            height: Number(b.heightCm)
          },
          weight: {
            unit: 'KG',
            value: Number(b.weightKg)
          }
        }))
      }
    ]
  };

  const response = fetchSigned_(token,{ method: 'POST', url, payload},[202]);

  return response.operationId;
}

function createInboundPlan_(token, endpoint, poNumber, items) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans`;

  const sourceAddress = JSON.parse(
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('FBA_SHIP_FROM_ADDRESS')
  );

  const payload = {
    destinationMarketplaces: [AMAZON.marketplaceId],
    name: String(poNumber),
    sourceAddress,
    items: items.map(i => ({
      msku: i.articleCode,
      quantity: i.qty,
      labelOwner: 'SELLER',
      prepOwner: 'NONE'
    }))
  };

  const response = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'POST', url, payload },
    [201, 202]
  );

  /*
    201 → synchronous success (rare)
    202 → async success (common)
  */

  if (!response.inboundPlanId) {
    throw new Error(
      `Inbound plan creation failed: ${JSON.stringify(response)}`
    );
  }

  return {
    inboundPlanId: response.inboundPlanId,
    operationId: response.operationId || null
  };
}




// ============================================================================
// HELPER NEW
// ============================================================================

function getPoItemsFromDB_(poRef) {
  const sh = SpreadsheetApp
    .getActive()
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const poIdx    = headers.indexOf('EE Order Ref ID');
  const skuIdx   = headers.indexOf('Item Code');
  const qtyIdx   = headers.indexOf('Qty');
  const storeIdx = headers.indexOf('Store Code');

  if ([poIdx, skuIdx, qtyIdx, storeIdx].includes(-1)) {
    throw new Error('Required columns missing in PO_Database');
  }

  const rows = data.filter(
    r => String(r[poIdx]).trim() === String(poRef).trim()
  );

  if (!rows.length) {
    throw new Error(`No rows found for PO ${poRef}`);
  }

  const warehouseId = String(rows[0][storeIdx]).trim();

  const items = rows
    .map(r => ({
      articleCode: String(r[skuIdx]).trim(),
      qty: Number(r[qtyIdx])
    }))
    .filter(i => i.articleCode && i.qty > 0);

  if (!items.length) {
    throw new Error(`No valid items found for PO ${poRef}`);
  }

  return { items, warehouseId };
}

function getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef) {
  const sh = SpreadsheetApp
    .getActive()
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  if (!sh) throw new Error(`Sheet ${SHEET_PO_DB} not found`);

  const data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const poIdx        = headers.indexOf('EE Order Ref ID');
  const inboundIdx   = headers.indexOf('Inbound Plan ID');
  const placementIdx = headers.indexOf('Placement ID');
  const shipmentIdx  = headers.indexOf('Shipment ID');

  if ([poIdx, inboundIdx, placementIdx, shipmentIdx].includes(-1)) {
    throw new Error(
      'Required columns missing: EE Order Ref ID / Inbound Plan ID / Placement ID / Shipment ID'
    );
  }

  for (const row of data) {
    if (String(row[poIdx]).trim() === String(poRef).trim()) {
      return {
        inboundPlanId:  String(row[inboundIdx]   || '').trim() || null,
        placementId:    String(row[placementIdx] || '').trim() || null,
        shipmentId:     String(row[shipmentIdx]  || '').trim() || null
      };
    }
  }

  return {
    inboundPlanId: null,
    placementId: null,
    shipmentId: null
  };
}

function buildBoxesFromPackingData_(rows) {
  const map = {};
  rows.forEach(r => {
    const id = r['Box ID'];
    if (!map[id]) {
      map[id] = {
        quantity: 0,
        lengthCm: r['Box Length'],
        widthCm: r['Box Width'],
        heightCm: r['Box Height'],
        weightKg: r['Box Weight']/1000
      };
    }
    map[id].quantity++;
  });
  return Object.values(map);
}

function updatePoDatabase_(po, inboundPlanId, shipmentId, placementId, shipmentConfirmationId) {
  const sh = SpreadsheetApp
    .getActive()
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  if (!sh) throw new Error(`Sheet ${SHEET_PO_DB} not found`);

  const data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const poIdx     = headers.indexOf('EE Order Ref ID');
  const planIdx   = headers.indexOf('Inbound Plan ID');
  const shipIdx   = headers.indexOf('Shipment ID');
  const placeIdx  = headers.indexOf('Placement ID');
  const fbashipIdx  = headers.indexOf('FBA Shipment IDs');

  if (poIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error('Column "EE Order Ref ID" missing in PO DB');
  }

  let updatedCount = 0;

  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (String(data[i][poIdx]).trim() !== String(po).trim()) continue;

    const rowNum = i + 1;

    // ✏️ Update ONLY if value is provided
    if (inboundPlanId && planIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, planIdx + 1).setValue(inboundPlanId);
    }

    if (shipmentId && shipIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, shipIdx + 1).setValue(shipmentId);
    }

    if (placementId && placeIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, placeIdx + 1).setValue(placementId);
    }

    if (shipmentConfirmationId && fbashipIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, fbashipIdx + 1).setValue(shipmentConfirmationId);
    }

    updatedCount++;
  }

  if (updatedCount === 0) {
    Logger.log(`No rows found for PO ${po} in PO database`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log(
    `Updated ${updatedCount} rows for PO ${po}` +
    `${inboundPlanId ? ` | inboundPlanId=${inboundPlanId}` : ''}` +
    `${shipmentId ? ` | shipmentId=${shipmentId}` : ''}` +
    `${placementId ? ` | placementId=${placementId}` : ''}`
  );
}

function getATSTransportationOptionId_(transportationOptions) 
{
  if (!transportationOptions || !transportationOptions.length) {
    throw new Error('No transportation options available');
  }

  const atsOption = transportationOptions.find(opt =>
    opt.shippingSolution === 'AMAZON_PARTNERED_CARRIER' ||
    opt.carrier?.alphaCode === 'AMAZNEMP'
  );

  if (!atsOption) {
    throw new Error('ATS transportation option not found');
  }

  return atsOption.transportationOptionId;
}


function listPlacementOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions`;

  const response = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'GET', url },
    [200]
  );

  const placementOptions = response.placementOptions || [];

  if (!placementOptions.length) {
    throw new Error('No placement options returned for inbound plan');
  }

  // India usually returns exactly one placement option
  const option = placementOptions[0];

  const placementOptionId = option.placementOptionId;
  const shipmentId = (option.shipmentIds && option.shipmentIds[0]) || null;

  if (!placementOptionId) {
    throw new Error('placementOptionId missing in placement option');
  }

  if (!shipmentId) {
    throw new Error('shipmentId missing in placement option');
  }

  return {
    placementOptionId,
    shipmentId
  };
}


function requestShipmentLabels_(
  token,
  endpoint,
  inboundPlanId,
  shipmentId,
  boxCount
) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}` +
    `/shipments/${shipmentId}/labels`;

  const payload = {
    labelType: 'PACKAGE_LABEL',
    pageType: 'A4',
    numberOfPackages: boxCount
  };

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'POST', url, payload },
    [202]
  );

  return res.operationId;
}


function downloadLabelDocument_(token, endpoint, documentId) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/documents/${documentId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'GET', url }, [200]);

  // res.url → pre-signed S3 URL (PDF)
  return res.url;
}

function downloadFbaShipmentLabels(poRef) {
  const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
  const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

  const { inboundPlanId, shipmentId } = getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef);

  const packingRows =
    _loadPackingData(SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(), poRef);

  const boxCount = packingRows.length;

  const opId = requestShipmentLabels_(
    token,
    endpoint,
    inboundPlanId,
    shipmentId,
    boxCount
  );

  const result = pollOperation_(token, endpoint, opId);

  const documentId = result.documents?.[0]?.documentId;
  if (!documentId) {
    throw new Error('Label document not generated');
  }

  return downloadLabelDocument_(token, endpoint, documentId);
}

function getInboundPlanItems_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'GET', url },
    [200]
  );

  if (!res.items || !res.items.length) {
    throw new Error(`No items found in inbound plan ${inboundPlanId}`);
  }

  return res.items.map(i => ({
    articleCode: i.msku,
    qty: i.quantity
  }));
}


function generatePlacementOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, warehouseId, items) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions`;

  const payload = {
    customPlacement: [{
      warehouseId,
      items: items.map(i => ({
        msku: i.articleCode,
        quantity: i.qty,
        labelOwner: 'SELLER',
        prepOwner: 'NONE'
      }))
    }]
  };

  return fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'POST', url, payload }, [202]).operationId;
}
