function generateTransportationOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, placementOptionId, shipmentId) 
{
  const url =`${endpoint}/inbound/fba/2024-03-20/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/transportationOptions`;

  const payload = {
    placementOptionId: placementOptionId,
    shipmentTransportationConfigurations: [
      {
        shipmentId: shipmentId,
        shipmentTransportationType: 'SP',
        contactInformation: {
          name: 'Mohan Dewangan',
          phoneNumber: '8103733766',
          email: 'avinav@cubelelo.com'
        },
        readyToShipWindow: {
          start: getReadyToShipDate_()
        }
      }
    ]
  };

  const res = fetchSigned_(token,{ method: 'POST', url, payload },[202]);

  return res.operationId;
}

function getReadyToShipDate_() {
  const d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1); // tomorrow
  d.setSeconds(0);
  d.setMilliseconds(0);
  return d.toISOString();
}



// ============================================================================
// OPERATION POLLING
// ============================================================================
function pollOperation_(token, endpoint, operationId, max = 25, waitMs = 12000) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/operations/${operationId}`;
  for (let i = 0; i < max; i++) {
    const res = fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'GET', url }, [200]);
    const status = String(res.operationStatus || '').toUpperCase();
    if (['SUCCESS', 'COMPLETED'].includes(status)) return;
    if (['FAILED', 'ERROR'].includes(status)) throw new Error(JSON.stringify(res));
    Utilities.sleep(waitMs);
  }
  throw new Error(`Operation ${operationId} timed out`);
}

// ============================================================================
// SIGNED FETCH WRAPPER
// ============================================================================

function fetchSigned_(token, req, okStatuses) {
  const options = {
    method: req.method,
    headers: {
      'x-amz-access-token': token,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  if (req.payload) {
    options.payload = JSON.stringify(req.payload);
  }
  Logger.log(req.url);
  Logger.log(options.payload);


  const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(req.url, options);
  Logger.log(res);
  const status = res.getResponseCode();
  const body = res.getContentText();

  if (!okStatuses.includes(status)) {
    throw new Error(`SP-API failed (${status}): ${body}`);
  }

  return body ? JSON.parse(body) : {};
}

/**
 * Processes ONLY Blinkit Appointment Pass emails.
 * Ignores all other channels and email types.
 */
/**
 * Processes ONLY Blinkit Appointment Pass emails.
 * Runs safely every 15 minutes using an independent timer property.
 */


function processBlinkitAppointmentPasses() {

  try {

    const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const LAST_RUN_KEY = 'BLINKIT_APPOINTMENT_LAST_RUN';

    let startTime = parseInt(scriptProperties.getProperty(LAST_RUN_KEY) || '0', 10);

    // First-run fallback → look back 120 hours
    if (startTime === 0) {
      const fallbackDate = new Date();
      fallbackDate.setHours(fallbackDate.getHours() - 24);
      startTime = Math.floor(fallbackDate.getTime() / 1000);
    }

    const currentRunTime = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
    const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

    if (!configSheet) {
      return { status: "error", message: "Channel Config sheet not found." };
    }

    const configData = configSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const newLogs = [];
    let processedCount = 0;

    configData.forEach(row => {

      const [channelName, status, rawEmails, subjectKeyword] = row;

      if (!channelName || channelName.toLowerCase() !== 'blinkit') return;
      if (String(status).toLowerCase() !== 'active') return;
      if (!rawEmails) return;

      const emailList = rawEmails.split(',')
        .map(e => e.trim().toLowerCase())
        .filter(Boolean);

      if (!emailList.length) return;

      const fromClause = `from:(${emailList.join(' OR ')})`;
      let query = `${fromClause} -from:me after:${startTime}`;
      if (subjectKeyword) query += ` subject:("${subjectKeyword}")`;

      const threads = GmailApp.search(query);
      if (!threads.length) return;

      const threadMessages = GmailApp.getMessagesForThreads(threads);

      threadMessages.forEach(messages => {
        messages.forEach(message => {

          const messageTime = Math.floor(message.getDate().getTime() / 1000);
          if (messageTime <= startTime) return;

          const sender = message.getFrom().toLowerCase();
          if (!emailList.some(e => sender.includes(e))) return;

          const subject = message.getSubject();
          if (!subject.toUpperCase().includes('APPOINTMENT PASS')) return;

          const appointmentDetails = _parseBlinkitAppointmentPass(message, folder);

          newLogs.push([
            message.getDate(),
            channelName,
            sender,
            subject,
            `QR Pass - ${appointmentDetails.appointmentId}`,
            appointmentDetails.qrCodeUrl,
            "Appointment Pass",
            appointmentDetails.poNumbers,
            "",
            appointmentDetails.appointmentId,
            appointmentDetails.appointmentDate,
            appointmentDetails.reportingTime,
            appointmentDetails.emailHtml
          ]);

          processedCount++;
        });
      });

    });

    // Write logs
    if (newLogs.length) {
      logSheet
        .getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, newLogs.length, newLogs[0].length)
        .setValues(newLogs);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      extractAppointmentPassDetails();
      scriptProperties.setProperty(LAST_RUN_KEY, String(currentRunTime));
    }

    return {
      status: "success",
      message: processedCount > 0
        ? `${processedCount} Blinkit appointment pass(es) processed successfully.`
        : "No new Blinkit appointment passes found.",
      processedCount: processedCount,
      scannedTill: new Date(currentRunTime * 1000)
    };

  } catch (e) {

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: "Error processing Blinkit appointment passes.",
      error: e.message
    };
  }
}

function updateZeptoASN(data) {
  const { eeReferenceCode, asnNumber } = data;
  if (!eeReferenceCode || !asnNumber) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing required fields' };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0];

  const eeRefIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
  let asnIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment ID");

  let updated = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][eeRefIdx]).trim() === String(eeReferenceCode).trim()) {
      if (asnIdx !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(i + 1, asnIdx + 1).setValue(asnNumber);
      }
      updated = true;
    }
  }

  if (updated) {
    return { status: 'success', message: 'ASN updated and status moved to Ready to Ship' };
  } else {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Order not found' };
  }
}

function updateInstamartAppointmentDetails(data) {
  const { eeReferenceCode, appointmentId, appointmentDate, appointmentTime } = data;
  if (!eeReferenceCode || (!appointmentId && !appointmentDate && !appointmentTime)) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing required fields' };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0];

  const eeRefIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
  const apptIdIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment ID");
  const apptDateIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment Date");
  const apptTimeIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment Time");

  if (eeRefIdx === -1 || apptIdIdx === -1 || apptDateIdx === -1 || apptTimeIdx === -1) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Required columns not found in PO_Database' };
  }

  let updated = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][eeRefIdx]).trim() === String(eeReferenceCode).trim()) {
      if (appointmentId) sheet.getRange(i + 1, apptIdIdx + 1).setValue(appointmentId);
      if (appointmentDate) sheet.getRange(i + 1, apptDateIdx + 1).setValue(appointmentDate);
      if (appointmentTime) sheet.getRange(i + 1, apptTimeIdx + 1).setValue(appointmentTime);
      updated = true;
    }
  }

  if (updated) {
    return { status: 'success', message: 'Appointment details updated successfully' };
  } else {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Order not found' };
  }
}


function extractAppointmentPassDetails() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  if (!repoSheet || !dbSheet) return;

  const lastRow = repoSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  const repoData = repoSheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, repoSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
  const headers = repoData[0];
  const dataRows = repoData.slice(1);

  const categoryIndex = headers.indexOf("Category");
  const statusIndex = headers.indexOf("Status");
  const poNumIndex = headers.indexOf("PO Number");
  const fileUrlIndex = headers.indexOf("Drive Link");
  const appointmentIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment ID");
  const appointmentDateIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment Date");
  const appointmentTimeIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment Time");

  if (
    categoryIndex === -1 ||
    statusIndex === -1 ||
    poNumIndex === -1 ||
    appointmentIdIndex === -1 ||
    appointmentDateIndex === -1 ||
    appointmentTimeIndex === -1
  ) {
    Logger.log("Required columns not found.");
    return;
  }

  const dbHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, dbSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const dbAppointmentColumnIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("Appointment ID");

  if (dbAppointmentColumnIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Appointment columns not found in PO DB sheet.");
    return;
  }

  const rowsToUpdate = {};

  // 🔥 ONLY APPOINTMENT PASS LOGIC
  dataRows.forEach((row, index) => {

    const category = String(row[categoryIndex] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    const currentStatus = String(row[statusIndex] || "").trim();
    const rowIndexInSheet = index + 2;

    if (category === "appointment pass" && currentStatus === "") {

      const poNumber = String(row[poNumIndex] || "").trim();
      if (!poNumber) return;

      const appointmentId = row[appointmentIdIndex] || "Not Found";
      const appointmentDate = row[appointmentDateIndex] || "Not Found";
      const appointmentTime = row[appointmentTimeIndex] || "Not Found";
      const fileUrl = row[fileUrlIndex] || "";

      const dbRowIndexes = findRowIndexesByPoNumber(dbSheet, poNumber);

      if (dbRowIndexes.length > 0) {

        const appointmentValues = [
          appointmentId,
          appointmentDate,
          appointmentTime,
          fileUrl
        ];

        dbRowIndexes.forEach(dbRowIndex => {
          dbSheet
            .getRange(dbRowIndex, dbAppointmentColumnIndex + 1, 1, 4)
            .setValues([appointmentValues]);
        });

        rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Extracted";

      } else {

        rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Skipped (PO Not Found in DB)";

      }

    }

  });

  // ✅ Update status column in Repo sheet
  for (const rowIndex in rowsToUpdate) {
    repoSheet
      .getRange(parseInt(rowIndex, 10), statusIndex + 1)
      .setValue(rowsToUpdate[rowIndex]);
  }

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  Logger.log("Appointment Pass processing completed.");
}


/**
 * **NEW HELPER:** Parses the email body of a Blinkit Appointment Pass to extract key details.
 *
 * @param {string} emailBody - The plain text content of the email.
 * @return {object} An object containing the extracted appointment details.
 */
/**
 * **NEW & UPGRADED HELPER:** Parses a Blinkit Appointment Pass. It now:
 * 1. Accepts the full GmailMessage object.
 * 2. Extracts all text details from the body.
 * 3. Finds the inline QR code image, saves it to Drive, and returns its URL.
 *
 * @param {GmailMessage} message - The full Gmail message object.
 * @param {Folder} folder - The Google Drive folder to save the QR code image to.
 * @return {object} An object containing all extracted appointment details, including the qrCodeUrl.
 */

function _parseBlinkitAppointmentPass(message, folder) {
  const emailBody = message.getPlainBody(); // Text
  const emailHtml = message.getBody();      // HTML (QR lives here)

  const details = {
    appointmentId: "Not Found",
    appointmentDate: "",
    reportingTime: "",
    poNumbers: "",
    qrCodeUrl: ""
  };

  // ----------------------------------------------------
  // TEXT PARSING
  // ----------------------------------------------------
  const idMatch = emailBody.match(/Appointment ID\s*\n\s*(\d+)/i);
  if (idMatch) details.appointmentId = idMatch[1].trim();

  const dateMatch = emailBody.match(/Appointment Date\s*\n\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})/i);
  if (dateMatch) details.appointmentDate = dateMatch[1].trim();

  const timeMatch = emailBody.match(/Reporting Time\s*\n\s*(\d{2}:\d{2}\s*(?:AM|PM))/i);
  if (timeMatch) details.reportingTime = timeMatch[1].trim();

  const poMatch = emailBody.match(/following POs:[\s\S]*?(\d+)/i);
  if (poMatch) details.poNumbers = poMatch[1];

  // ----------------------------------------------------
  // QR CODE EXTRACTION (FIXED)
  // ----------------------------------------------------
  try {
    /**
     * Match ANY img inside the qr-section
     * This avoids brittle URL assumptions
     */
    const qrImgMatch = emailHtml.match(
      /<div class="qr-section">[\s\S]*?<img[^>]+src="([^"]+)"/i
    );

    if (!qrImgMatch || !qrImgMatch[1]) {
      Logger.log("QR image not found in HTML");
      details.qrCodeUrl = "NOT FOUND";
      return details;
    }

    // HTML entities decode (&amp; → &)
    const qrImageUrl = qrImgMatch[1].replace(/&amp;/g, '&');

    const imageBlob = UrlFetchApp.fetch(qrImageUrl, {
      followRedirects: true,
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }).getBlob();

    const imageName = `QR_APPT_${details.appointmentId || 'UNKNOWN'}.jpeg`;
    const file = folder.createFile(imageBlob).setName(imageName);

    details.qrCodeUrl = file.getUrl();
    Logger.log(`QR code saved successfully: ${imageName}`);

  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log(`QR extraction failed: ${err.message}`);
    details.qrCodeUrl = "SAVE FAILED";
  }

  return details;
}

/**
 * ==========================================================
 * CHANNEL CONFIG
 * ==========================================================
 */

const EMAIL_CONFIG = {
  ZEPTO: { NAME: "Zepto", MODE: "sheet", VENDOR: "Brainlytic Solutions Pvt Ltd" },
  INSTAMART: { NAME: "Instamart", MODE: "file", VENDOR: "Brainlytic Solutions Pvt Ltd" },
  BB: { NAME: "BB", MODE: "email", VENDOR: "Brainlytic Solutions Pvt Ltd" }
};


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * MAIN ENGINE
 * ==========================================================
 */

function tetete()
{
  processChannelAppointments("BB","IRA34740046");
}

function processChannelAppointments(channelName, manualSaleOrderList = null) {

  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(30000)) {
    return { status: "error", message: "System busy. Try again." };
  }

  try {

    const channel = Object.values(EMAIL_CONFIG)
      .find(c => c.NAME === channelName);

    if (!channel) throw new Error("Invalid channel");

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    const rows = data.slice(1);

    const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

    const IDX = {
      CHANNEL: col("Channel Name"),
      ORDER_STATUS: col("EE_order_status"),
      AWB: col("AWB"),
      INVOICE_ID: col("Invoice Id"),
      PO_NUMBER: col("PO Number"),
      PO_DATE: col("PO Date"),
      EXPIRY_DATE: col("PO Expiry Date"),
      STORE_CODE: col("Store Code"),
      QTY: col("Qty"),
      BOXES: col("Box Data"),
      SALE_ORDER_NO: col("EE_reference_code"),
      APPT_REQ_ID: col("Appointment Request ID"),
      APPT_REQ_TS: col("Appointment Request Timestamp")
    };

    validateHeaders(IDX);

    const manualSet = manualSaleOrderList ? new Set(manualSaleOrderList) : null;

    const saleOrderMap = {};
    let hasOpenOrders = false;

    rows.forEach((row,i)=>{

      if(row[IDX.CHANNEL] !== channel.NAME) return;

      const status = String(row[IDX.ORDER_STATUS]||"").trim();
      const awb = String(row[IDX.AWB]||"").trim();
      const invoice = String(row[IDX.INVOICE_ID]||"").trim();
      const apptReq = String(row[IDX.APPT_REQ_ID]||"").trim();

      const saleOrder = String(row[IDX.SALE_ORDER_NO]||"").trim();
      if(!saleOrder) return;

      if(!manualSet && status==="Open") hasOpenOrders = true;

      let isTarget = true;
      if(manualSet) isTarget = manualSet.has(saleOrder);

      const boxCount = Number(row[IDX.BOXES]||0);

      if(
        isTarget &&
        awb === "" &&
        invoice !== "" &&
        status === "Confirmed" &&
        boxCount !== 0 &&
        apptReq === ""
      ){

        if(!saleOrderMap[saleOrder]){
          saleOrderMap[saleOrder] = {
            saleOrderNo:saleOrder,
            poNumber:row[IDX.PO_NUMBER],
            poDate:row[IDX.PO_DATE],
            expiryDate:row[IDX.EXPIRY_DATE],
            storeCode:row[IDX.STORE_CODE],
            totalQty:0,
            totalBoxes:boxCount,
            rowIndexes:[]
          };
        }

        saleOrderMap[saleOrder].totalQty += Number(row[IDX.QTY]||0);
        saleOrderMap[saleOrder].rowIndexes.push(i+2);
      }

    });

    const eligibleOrders = Object.values(saleOrderMap);
    const requestId = generateRequestId();

    if(!manualSet && hasOpenOrders){
      writeToLog("SYSTEM","Blocked","-","-","Batch blocked due to open orders");
      return {status:"error",message:"Open orders exist"};
    }

    if(eligibleOrders.length===0){
      writeToLog("SYSTEM","Skipped","-","-","No eligible orders");
      return {status:"error",message:"No eligible orders"};
    }
    
    const channelConfig = fetchChannelConfig(channel.NAME);


    if(channel.NAME==="BB"){
      return sendBigBasketEmails(
        eligibleOrders,
        sheet,
        rows.length,
        IDX,
        channelConfig.cc
      );
    }


    if(!channelConfig?.to) throw new Error("Channel email config missing");

    const htmlTable = buildAppointmentEmailTable(eligibleOrders);

    let attachment=null;
    let sheetUrl="";

    if(channel.MODE==="sheet"){
      sheetUrl = createZeptoAppointmentSheet(
        eligibleOrders,
        requestId,
        channelConfig.to,
        channelConfig.cc
      );
    }
    else if(channel.MODE==="file"){
      attachment = createAppointmentFile(
        eligibleOrders,
        requestId,
        channel,
        channelConfig.to,
        channelConfig.cc
      );
    }

    const htmlBody = buildEmailBody(htmlTable,requestId,sheetUrl);

    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to:channelConfig.to,
      cc:channelConfig.cc || "",
      subject:`${channel.NAME} Appointment Request | ${requestId}`,
      htmlBody,
      attachments:attachment ? [attachment] : []
    });

    updateRequestTracking(sheet,rows.length,IDX,eligibleOrders,requestId);

    writeToLog(
      requestId,
      "Success",
      eligibleOrders.map(o=>o.saleOrderNo).join(", "),
      `To:${channelConfig.to}`,
      `${channel.NAME} email sent`,
      sheetUrl
    );

    return {status:"success",requestId,count:eligibleOrders.length};

  }
  catch(err){
    writeToLog("SYSTEM","Failed","-","-",err.message);
    return {status:"error",message:err.message};
  }
  finally{
    lock.releaseLock();
  }

}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * BIGBASKET EMAIL ENGINE
 * ==========================================================
 */


function sendBigBasketEmails(orders,sheet,rowCount,IDX,ccmails){

  const storeEmailMap = getBBStoreEmailMap();

  const grouped = {};

  orders.forEach(o=>{
    if(!grouped[o.storeCode]) grouped[o.storeCode]=[];
    grouped[o.storeCode].push(o);
  });

  const results = [];

  Object.keys(grouped).forEach(storeCode=>{

    const requestId = generateRequestId();   // NEW ID PER EMAIL

    const email = storeEmailMap[storeCode];
    if(!email) return;

    const storeOrders = grouped[storeCode];

    const htmlTable = buildAppointmentEmailTable(storeOrders);

    const htmlBody = `
    <div style="font-family:Roboto,Arial;font-size:14px">
    <p>Dear Team,</p>

    ${htmlTable}

    <p>Kindly confirm the appointment date.</p>

    <p>Request ID: <b>${requestId}</b></p>

    <p>Regards<br>Team Cubelelo</p>
    </div>`;

    Logger.log(email);
    Logger.log(ccmails);
    Logger.log(requestId);
    Logger.log(htmlBody);

    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to:email,
      cc:ccmails || "",
      subject:`BigBasket Appointment Request | ${storeCode} | ${requestId}`,
      htmlBody
    });

    // update tracking per store
    updateRequestTracking(sheet,rowCount,IDX,storeOrders,requestId);

    results.push({
      storeCode,
      requestId
    });

  });

  writeToLog(
    "BB_BATCH",
    "Success",
    orders.map(o=>o.saleOrderNo).join(", "),
    "BB Store POCs",
    "BB appointment emails sent"
  );

  return {
    status:"success",
    results
  };

}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * REQUEST TRACKING UPDATE
 * ==========================================================
 */

function updateRequestTracking(sheet,rowCount,IDX,orders,requestId){

  const idRange = sheet.getRange(2,IDX.APPT_REQ_ID+1,rowCount,1);
  const tsRange = sheet.getRange(2,IDX.APPT_REQ_TS+1,rowCount,1);

  const idValues = idRange.getValues();
  const tsValues = tsRange.getValues();

  const now = new Date();

  orders.forEach(o=>{
    o.rowIndexes.forEach(r=>{
      const i = r-2;
      if(i>=0 && i<idValues.length){
        idValues[i][0]=requestId;
        tsValues[i][0]=now;
      }
    });
  });

  idRange.setValues(idValues);
  tsRange.setValues(tsValues);
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * FILE / SHEET CREATION
 * ==========================================================
 */

function createZeptoAppointmentSheet(orders,requestId,to,cc){

  const appointmentDate = getAppointmentDate();

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.create(`Zepto_Appointment_${requestId}`);
  const sheet = ss.getActiveSheet();

  const headers=[
    "PO Number","PO Date","Expiry Date","Store Code","Vendor Name",
    "Qty","Boxes","Appointment Requested Date","Confirmed Date"
  ];

  sheet.getRange(1,1,1,headers.length).setValues([headers]);

  const rows = orders.map(o=>[
    o.poNumber,
    o.poDate,
    o.expiryDate,
    o.storeCode,
    EMAIL_CONFIG.ZEPTO.VENDOR,
    o.totalQty,
    o.totalBoxes,
    appointmentDate,
    ""
  ]);

  sheet.getRange(2,1,rows.length,headers.length).setValues(rows);

  const file = DriveApp.getFileById(ss.getId());
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

  file.moveTo(folder);

  shareFile(file,to);
  shareFile(file,cc);

  return ss.getUrl();
}


function createAppointmentFile(orders,requestId,channel,to,cc){

  const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
  const appointmentDate = getAppointmentDate();

  const headers=[
    "PO Number","PO Date","Expiry Date","Store Code","Vendor Name",
    "Qty","Boxes","Appointment Requested Date","Confirmed Date"
  ];

  const rows = orders.map(o=>[
    o.poNumber,
    Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.poDate),tz,"dd-MM-yyyy"),
    Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.expiryDate),tz,"dd-MM-yyyy"),
    o.storeCode,
    channel.VENDOR,
    o.totalQty,
    o.totalBoxes,
    appointmentDate,
    ""
  ]);

  const csv=[headers.join(","),...rows.map(r=>r.join(","))].join("\n");

  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(
    csv,
    "text/csv",
    `${channel.NAME}_Appointment_${requestId}.csv`
  );

  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);
  const file = folder.createFile(blob);

  shareFile(file,to);
  shareFile(file,cc);

  return blob;
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * HELPERS
 * ==========================================================
 */

function getAppointmentDate(){

  const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

  let d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate()+10);

  while(d.getDay()===0) d.setDate(d.getDate()+1);

  return Utilities.formatDate(d,tz,"dd-MM-yyyy");
}

function generateRequestId(){
  return "REQ-"+Math.floor(Date.now()/1000);
}

function validateHeaders(obj){
  Object.entries(obj).forEach(([k,v])=>{
    if(v===-1) throw new Error(`Missing column: ${k}`);
  });
}

function shareFile(file,emails){

  if(!emails) return;

  emails.split(",").forEach(e=>{
    if(e.trim()) file.addEditor(e.trim());
  });
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * EMAIL BODY
 * ==========================================================
 */

function buildEmailBody(table,requestId,sheetUrl){

return `
<div style="font-family:Roboto,Arial;font-size:14px">

<p>Dear Team,</p>

${table}

<p>
Kindly update the <b>Confirmed Date</b> so that we can dispatch the shipment.
</p>

${sheetUrl ? `
<p>Update in sheet:<br>
<a href="${sheetUrl}" target="_blank">${sheetUrl}</a></p>
`:``}

<p>Request ID:<b>${requestId}</b></p>

<p>Regards<br>Team Cubelelo</p>

</div>`;
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * EMAIL TABLE
 * ==========================================================
 */

function buildAppointmentEmailTable(orders){

const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
const appointmentDate = getAppointmentDate();

return `
<table style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;font-size:14px">
<thead>
<tr style="background:#f1f3f4">
<th style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">PO Number</th>
<th style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">Store Code</th>
<th style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">Qty</th>
<th style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">Boxes</th>
<th style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">PO Date</th>
<th style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">Expiry Date</th>
<th style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px;background:#137333;color:#fff">Appointment Requested</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
${orders.map(o=>`
<tr>
<td style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">${o.poNumber}</td>
<td style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">${o.storeCode}</td>
<td style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">${o.totalQty}</td>
<td style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">${o.totalBoxes}</td>
<td style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">${Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.poDate),tz,"dd-MMM-yyyy")}</td>
<td style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">${Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.expiryDate),tz,"dd-MMM-yyyy")}</td>
<td style="border:1px solid #dadce0;padding:8px">${appointmentDate}</td>
</tr>`).join("")}
</tbody>
</table>`;
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * BIGBASKET STORE EMAIL MAP
 * ==========================================================
 */

function getBBStoreEmailMap()
{
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_ZOHO_CUSTOMERS);

  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const colName = headers.indexOf("Contact Name");
  const colEmail = headers.indexOf("Email");

  const map={};

  for(let i=1;i<data.length;i++)
  {
    const name=data[i][colName];
    const email=data[i][colEmail];
    if(!name || !email) continue;
    if(!name.startsWith("BB_")) continue;
    const store = name.replace("BB_","").trim();
    map[store]=email;
  }
  return map;
}

/**
 * ==========================================================
 * CHANNEL CONFIG FETCH
 * ==========================================================
 */

function fetchChannelConfig(channelName){

const sheet = SpreadsheetApp
.getActiveSpreadsheet()
.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);

const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
const headers = data[0].map(h=>String(h).toLowerCase());

const colChannel=headers.indexOf("channel name");
const colTo=headers.indexOf("appointment to");
const colCC=headers.indexOf("appointment cc");

for(let i=1;i<data.length;i++){

const rowChannel = String(data[i][colChannel]||"").toLowerCase();

if(rowChannel.includes(channelName.toLowerCase())){
return{
to:data[i][colTo],
cc:data[i][colCC]
};
}
}

return null;
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * LOGGING
 * ==========================================================
 */

function writeToLog(requestId,status,poNumbers,recipients,notes,fileUrl=""){

const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(EMAIL_LOGS);

if(!sheet){

sheet = ss.insertSheet(EMAIL_LOGS);

sheet.appendRow([
"Timestamp",
"Request ID",
"Status",
"PO Numbers",
"Recipients",
"Notes",
"File URL"
]);
}

sheet.appendRow([
new Date(),
requestId,
status,
poNumbers,
recipients,
notes,
fileUrl
]);

}

function sendBBOrderConfirmationEmail() 
{
  var poNumbers = ["IRA35561661","IRA35562612","IRA35563306","IRA35564145","IRA35564950"];

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  if (!sheet) throw new Error("PO Database sheet not found");

  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

  const IDX = {
    PO: col("PO Number"),
    STATUS: col("Status")
  };

  validateHeaders(IDX);

  const poSet = new Set(poNumbers.map(p => String(p).trim()));

  const validPOSet = new Set();   // ✅ UNIQUE PO
  const rowMap = {};             // po → [rowIndexes]

  // ================================
  // STEP 1: Filter + Map ALL rows
  // ================================
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {

    const po = String(data[i][IDX.PO]).trim();
    if (!poSet.has(po)) continue;

    const status = String(data[i][IDX.STATUS] || "").toLowerCase();
    if (status === "cancelled") continue;

    validPOSet.add(po);

    // ✅ store multiple rows per PO
    if (!rowMap[po]) rowMap[po] = [];
    rowMap[po].push(i + 1);
  }

  const validPOs = Array.from(validPOSet);

  if (validPOs.length === 0) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No valid POs found." };
  }

  const channelConfig = fetchChannelConfig("BB");

  if (!channelConfig?.to) {
    throw new Error("BB channel email config missing.");
  }

  // ================================
  // STEP 2: Clean Table (fixed width)
  // ================================
  const table = `
    <table style="border-collapse:collapse;width:400px;font-size:14px;">
      <thead>
        <tr style="background:#f1f3f4;">
          <th style="padding:10px;border:1px solid #dadce0;text-align:left;">PO Number</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        ${validPOs.map(po => `
          <tr>
            <td style="padding:10px;border:1px solid #dadce0;">${po}</td>
          </tr>
        `).join("")}
      </tbody>
    </table>`;

  const htmlBody = `
    <div style="font-family:Roboto,Arial;font-size:14px;color:#202124;">

      <p>Dear Team,</p>

      <p>Kindly confirm the following Purchase Orders:</p>

      ${table}

      <p>Awaiting your confirmation.</p>

      <p>
      Regards,<br>
      Team Cubelelo
      </p>

    </div>`;

  // ================================
  // STEP 3: Send Email
  // ================================
  MailApp.sendEmail({
    to: channelConfig.to,
    cc: channelConfig.cc || "",
    subject: `BigBasket PO Confirmation Required | ${validPOs.length} POs`,
    htmlBody
  });

  // ================================
  // STEP 4: Update ALL rows (FIXED)
  // ================================
  const statusRange = sheet.getRange(2, IDX.STATUS + 1, data.length - 1, 1);
  const statusValues = statusRange.getValues();

  validPOs.forEach(po => {

    const rowIndexes = rowMap[po] || [];

    rowIndexes.forEach(rowIndex => {

      const index = rowIndex - 2;

      if (index >= 0 && index < statusValues.length) {
        statusValues[index][0] = "Waiting for Confirmation";
      }

    });

  });

  statusRange.setValues(statusValues);

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  return {
    status: "success",
    message: "Email sent and all rows updated.",
    totalPOs: validPOs.length
  };
}
// ✅ Detect Revised / Amendment Emails
function isRevisedEmail(subject, body) {
  const text = (subject + " " + body).toLowerCase();
  return text.includes("amendment") || text.includes("revised");
}

// ✅ Extract Appointment Date ONLY from email body
function extractAppointmentFromBody(text) {
  if (!text) return "";

  const match = text.match(/appointment\s*date[:\-]?\s*([0-9\/\-]+)/i);
  return match ? match[1] : "";
}

// ✅ Read Excel attachment via blob
function getExcelDataViaBlobFromAttachment(blob) {
  const tempFile = DriveApp.createFile(blob);
  const fileId = tempFile.getId();

  const data = getExcelDataViaBlob(fileId);

  DriveApp.getFileById(fileId).setTrashed(true);

  return data;
}

function updateExistingPO(poNumber, newData) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const data = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

  const IDX = {
    PO: col("PO Number"),
    APPOINTMENT: col("Appointment Date"),
    EXPIRY: col("PO Expiry Date")
  };

  let appointmentChanged = false;
  let expiryChanged = false;

  let oldAppointment = null;
  let oldExpiry = null;

  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {

    const po = String(data[i][IDX.PO]).trim();
    if (po !== poNumber) continue;

    // Capture old values (only once)
    if (oldAppointment === null) oldAppointment = data[i][IDX.APPOINTMENT];
    if (oldExpiry === null) oldExpiry = data[i][IDX.EXPIRY];

    // -----------------------
    // Appointment Update
    // -----------------------
    if (newData.appointmentDate && newData.appointmentDate !== data[i][IDX.APPOINTMENT]) {

      dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, IDX.APPOINTMENT + 1)
        .setValue(newData.appointmentDate);

      appointmentChanged = true;
    }

    // -----------------------
    // Expiry Update
    // -----------------------
    if (newData.expiryDate && newData.expiryDate !== data[i][IDX.EXPIRY]) {

      dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, IDX.EXPIRY + 1)
        .setValue(newData.expiryDate);

      expiryChanged = true;
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------
  // 🔥 FINAL CLEAN CHANGE LOG
  // -----------------------------------

  let changes = [];

  if (appointmentChanged) {
    changes.push(`Appointment Date updated: ${oldAppointment} → ${newData.appointmentDate}`);
  }

  if (expiryChanged) {
    changes.push(`Expiry Date updated: ${oldExpiry} → ${newData.expiryDate}`);
  }

  return changes;
}

// ✅ Detect Amazon Pickup Email
function isAmazonPickupEmail(sender, subject) {
  return sender.includes("donotreply@amazon.com") &&
         subject.toLowerCase().includes("fba pickup appointment confirmed");
}

// ✅ Extract Shipment ID from subject
function extractShipmentId(subject) {

  if (!subject) return "";

  // Works for:
  // FBA Pickup Appointment Confirmed - FBA15LLKD2T4
  const match = subject.match(/-\s*(FBA[0-9A-Z]+)/i);

  return match ? match[1].trim() : "";
}
function formatPickupSlot(slot) {

  if (!slot) return "";

  const parts = slot.split(",");

  if (parts.length !== 2) return slot;

  const time = parts[0].trim();
  const date = parts[1].trim();

  const d = date.split("/");
  if (d.length === 3) {
    return `${d[2]}-${d[1]}-${d[0]} | ${time}`;
  }

  

  return slot;
}
// ✅ Extract Pickup Slot from body
function extractPickupSlot(body) {

  if (!body) return "";

  // Normalize line breaks
  const cleanBody = body.replace(/\r/g, "");

  // Match label + next line value
  const match = cleanBody.match(
    /Confirmed FBA Pickup Appointment Slot:\s*\n?\s*([^\n]+)/i
  );

  return match ? match[1].trim() : "";
}

function updateAmazonPickup(shipmentId, pickupSlot) {

  if (!shipmentId || !pickupSlot) return;

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const data = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

  const IDX = {
    FBA: col("FBA Shipment IDs"), // ✅ CHANGE HERE
    PICKUP: col("Pickup Date")
  };

  let found = false;

  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {

    const fbaId = String(data[i][IDX.FBA]).trim();

    if (fbaId === shipmentId) {

      found = true;

      const oldValue = data[i][IDX.PICKUP];

      if (pickupSlot !== oldValue) {

        dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, IDX.PICKUP + 1)
          .setValue(pickupSlot);

        Logger.log(`Pickup Updated → ${shipmentId} → ${pickupSlot}`);
      }

      // 🔥 Update ALL rows for same FBA ID
      // (important if multiple rows per shipment)

    }
  }

  if (!found) {
    Logger.log(`FBA Shipment not found: ${shipmentId}`);
  }
}/**
 * Nimbus Post Email Scheduler & Tracker Update
 * This script is designed to be added to the Google Apps Script project.
 * It sets up a time-driven trigger to run every 4 hours.
 */

// Configuration
const SHEET_PO_DATABASE = "PO_Database";
const SHEET_SYSTEM_CONFIG = "System_Config";

/**
 * Setup Function: Run this once manually to install the triggers.
 */
function setupNimbusTriggers() {
  const functionName = "processNimbusAndSendEmail";
  
  // Clear existing triggers to avoid duplicates
  const triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  for (let i = 0; i < triggers.length; i++) {
    if (triggers[i].getHandlerFunction() === functionName) {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(triggers[i]);
    }
  }

  // Create a trigger to run every 4 hours
  ScriptApp.newTrigger(functionName)
    .timeBased()
    .everyHours(4)
    .create();
    
  Logger.log("Trigger setup completed for " + functionName);
}

/**
 * Main Scheduled Function
 * Extrapolates Nimbus-associated shipments and emails a summary.
 */
function processNimbusAndSendEmail() {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet() || SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DATABASE);
    
    // Fetch Email from System Config
    const nimbusEmail = getSystemConfigEmail(ss, 'nimbus_notification_email');
    if (!nimbusEmail) {
      Logger.log("Nimbus notification email not configured in System Config. Exiting.");
      return;
    }

    // 1. Fetch relevant Nimbus shipments
    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dbData.shift();
    
    const awbIndex = headers.indexOf("AWB");
    const statusIndex = headers.indexOf("Tracking Status");
    const carrierIndex = headers.indexOf("Carrier");
    const eeRefIndex = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
    const lastUpdateIndex = headers.indexOf("Latest Status Date");
    const eddIndex = headers.indexOf("EDD");
    
    if (awbIndex === -1 || eeRefIndex === -1) {
      Logger.log("Required columns are missing from PO_Database");
      return;
    }
    
    // Filter active Nimbus shipments
    const nimbusShipments = [];
    
    dbData.forEach(row => {
      const awb = String(row[awbIndex] || "").trim();
      const carrier = String(row[carrierIndex] || "").toLowerCase();
      const trackingStatus = String(row[statusIndex] || "").toLowerCase();
      
      // Basic heuristic to capture Nimbus assigned shipments
      // Assuming carrier may say 'Nimbus' or AWB is present and not delivered via nimbus logic
      if (awb !== "" && trackingStatus !== "delivered" && trackingStatus !== "rto delivered") {
        nimbusShipments.push({
          eeRef: row[eeRefIndex],
          awb: awb,
          status: row[statusIndex] || "Pending",
          carrier: row[carrierIndex] || "Unknown",
          edd: row[eddIndex] ? new Date(row[eddIndex]).toLocaleDateString() : "N/A",
          lastUpdate: row[lastUpdateIndex] ? new Date(row[lastUpdateIndex]).toLocaleString() : "N/A"
        });
      }
    });
    
    if (nimbusShipments.length === 0) {
      Logger.log("No active Nimbus shipments to report.");
      return;
    }

    // 2. Build HTML Email
    const htmlEmail = buildHtmlEmailTemplate(nimbusShipments);
    
    // 3. Send Email
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: nimbusEmail,
      subject: `Nimbus Shipments Daily Update - ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}`,
      htmlBody: htmlEmail
    });
    
    Logger.log(`Successfully sent Nimbus update to ${nimbusEmail} for ${nimbusShipments.length} shipments.`);
    
  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("Error in processNimbusAndSendEmail: " + err.toString());
  }
}

/**
 * Gets a specific key from System_Config sheet
 */
function getSystemConfigEmail(ss, configKey) {
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_SYSTEM_CONFIG);
  if (!configSheet) return null;
  
  const data = configSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { // Skip header
    if (data[i][0] === configKey) {
      return data[i][1];
    }
  }
  return null;
}

/**
 * Generates an HTML table for the email body.
 */
function buildHtmlEmailTemplate(shipments) {
  let tableRows = shipments.map(s => {
    // Correctly formatted AWB-prefixed anchor text
    const trackingLink = `https://ship.nimbuspost.com/shipping/tracking/${s.awb}`;
    const awbLink = `<a href="${trackingLink}" style="color: #10B981; text-decoration: none;"><b>AWB-${s.awb}</b></a>`;
    
    return `
      <tr>
        <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB;">${s.eeRef}</td>
        <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB;">${awbLink}</td>
        <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB;">${s.carrier}</td>
        <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB;">
          <span style="background-color: #FEF3C7; color: #D97706; padding: 4px 8px; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 12px; font-weight: bold;">
            ${s.status}
          </span>
        </td>
        <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB;">${s.edd}</td>
        <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB;">${s.lastUpdate}</td>
      </tr>
    `;
  }).join("");

  return `
    <div style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; max-width: 800px; margin: 0 auto;">
      <div style="background-color: #10B981; padding: 20px; color: white; border-radius: 8px 8px 0 0;">
        <h2 style="margin: 0;">Automated Nimbus Dispatch Report</h2>
        <p style="margin: 5px 0 0 0; opacity: 0.9;">System Generated Trackers - ${new Date().toLocaleString()}</p>
      </div>
      
      <div style="padding: 20px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB; border-top: none; border-radius: 0 0 8px 8px;">
        <p>Hello,</p>
        <p>Please find the latest tracking statuses for pending shipments handled via the Nimbus Courier partner.</p>
        
        <table style="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; margin-top: 20px; font-size: 14px;">
          <thead>
            <tr style="background-color: #F3F4F6; text-align: left;">
              <th style="padding: 12px 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB; font-weight: 600; color: #374151;">Order Ref</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB; font-weight: 600; color: #374151;">Tracking Link</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB; font-weight: 600; color: #374151;">Carrier</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB; font-weight: 600; color: #374151;">Status</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB; font-weight: 600; color: #374151;">EDD</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px 10px; border: 1px solid #E5E7EB; font-weight: 600; color: #374151;">Last Update</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            ${tableRows}
          </tbody>
        </table>
        
        <p style="margin-top: 30px; font-size: 12px; color: #6B7280; text-align: center;">
          This is an automated 4-hourly summary generated by the Order Management Dashboard.
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
}
